#Author:Bhavatrāta
#Text:Jaiminīyaśrautasūtrabhāṣya
#Comments:Jaiminīyaśrautasūtra
#Edition:Asko Parpola
#Data entry:Asko Parpola
#Notes:Latex source provided by A. Parpola.
#Todo:Ranges of commented sutras starting only at 11.21. Before this, only the last commented sutra is indicated.


1.1.[1]	nanu pratijñāya prārabdhavyam idaṃ vakṣyāma iti /
1.1.[2]	vivakṣitasyārthasya pratijñāyāṃ kṛtāyām idam anena vakṣyata ity avahitamanasāṃ pratipattṝnāṃ pratipattau lāghavam upajāyate /
1.1.[3]	dṛśyate ca śāstrādau pratijñā /
1.1.[4]	athāto vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāraḥ /
1.1.[5]	yajñaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ /
1.1.[6]	athāto dharmajijñāseti /
1.1.[7]	na cāyam ekānto yat pratijñā kartavyeti /
1.1.[8]	pratijñātam api yadi na samyag vyākhyāyeta durbodha evārtho bhavati /
1.1.[9]	apratijñātam api sādhu varṇyamānam arthaṃ sadya eva śrāvakāḥ pratipadyante /
1.1.[10]	alpīyas tu pratipattilāghavam asty eva pratijñākaraṇe /
1.1.[11]	tadarthaṃ ke cid ācāryāḥ pratijānanti ke cid granthalāghavārtham apratijñāyaiva śāstrāṇi prārabhante /
1.1.[12]	dṛśyate hy āgneyañ cāgnīṣomīyañ ca puroḍāśāv āsādya hotāram āmantrayate vṛddhir ād aij ity evamādi śāstrāṇi /
1.1.[13]	śrutāv apy ubhayan dṛśyate /
1.1.[14]	sāvitram pūrvedyuḥ paśum ālabhanta ity athaiṣa upaśada iti ca /
1.1.[15]	śrutyanukaraṇārtham ācāryo 'py ubhayaṃ karoti yathātra na pratijānāti pratijñāsyati cāgnyādheyādiṣu /
1.1.[16]	tasmād apratijñānam adoṣam /
1.1.[17]	alam atiprasaṅgena /
1.1.[18]	sūtraṃ vyākhyeyam /
1.1.[19]	tatra somaṃ pravakti prabravītīti vā somapravākaḥ /
1.1.[20]	tam ātmānam ābhimukhyena gatam udgātā pratīkṣya mahan me 'voca ity etan mantrañ japet /
1.1.[21]	ayan tāvat samudāyārtho vistareṇa ca varṇyate /
1.1.[22]	somo yajño makha iti paryāyāḥ /
1.1.[23]	somadravyakatvāt somaśabdo yajñe pravartate /
1.1.[24]	sa ca sarveṣv ekāhāhīnasattreṣv aviśeṣeṇa pravartamāno 'pi jyotiṣṭomam evābhisandhāyātra prayujyate tasyaivātra vakṣyamāṇatvāt /
1.1.[25]	somenāsau yakṣyate tasya tvayaudgātraṃ kartavyam iti ya udgātāraṃ prabravīti sa somapravāko na yaḥ kaś cit somo vidyata ity etanmātraṃ prabravīti /
1.1.[26]	uttaratra hy anūcānair eva saha yājayed ityādy ārtvijyasaṃbandham eva vakṣyate /
1.1.[27]	nanu somapravākaṃ pratimantrayetety etāvataivārthasya siddhatvād āgataśabdo 'narthakaḥ /
1.1.[28]	nānarthakaḥ /
1.1.[29]	śaryāto vai mānava ity etadanuvākapradarśitasya sa yady adīkṣitam iti vākyenātrāpi vidhāsyamānasya svayam evodgānārtham abhigamanasyānabhipretatvapradarśanārthatvāt /
1.1.[30]	atha vā somapravacanasyāniyatakartṛtvam āgataśabdena jñāpyate /
1.1.[31]	ya āgatas taṃ pratimantrayeteti /
1.1.[32]	nanv anirdeśād eva somapravākasyāniyatatvaṃ sidhyati /
1.1.[33]	naivam /
1.1.[34]	anirdeśe yajamāna eva somapravāka iti gṛhyeta /
1.1.[35]	sa hy ātmana ārtvijyaṃ kārayitum ṛtvijas svayam evābhigamya vaktum arhati na yaḥ kaś cid anādareṇaiva prahetuḥ /
1.1.[36]	tatra yajamāno vānyo vā somapravāka ity āgataśabdena jñāpyate /
1.1.[37]	atha vodgātus sattre yajamānasya sato 'prārthitopanatatvād asya vidher abhāvo nyāyyaḥ /
1.1.[38]	tajjñāpanārtham āgatam iti /
1.1.[39]	prārthayitum āgatan nānyam iti /
1.1.[40]	kathaṃ punar ayājayiṣyatāpi vakṣyamāṇaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ pratimantraṇīyam uta yājayiṣyataiva /
1.1.[41]	ubhābhyām iti brūmaḥ /
1.1.[42]	yadi hi yājayiṣyataivābhaviṣyat sa yadi yājayiṣyan syād ity atraiva pratimantraṇaṃ vyadhāsyata /
1.1.[43]	ayājanabuddhiś ca yājane doṣajñānād utpadyate /
1.1.[44]	kac cin nāhīnā3 iti pṛṣṭvā tatprativacanena doṣādoṣau jñāyete na ca pūrvavihitaṃ pratimantraṇam akṛtvā praṣṭuṃ yuktam /
1.1.[45]	athaivam ucyeta /
1.1.[46]	prokte some tadānīm eva pratimantraṇam akurvan kac cin nāhīnā3 ity ato 'nyenaiva prakāreṇa guṇadoṣān yājane vijñāya tataḥ pratimantrayeta vā na veti /
1.1.[47]	tad ayuktam /
1.1.[48]	nityam anyenaivopāyena yājanadoṣābhāve 'pi vijñeye sati tadarthānām eṣāṃ praśnānām ānarthakyaprasaṅgāt /
1.1.[49]	na ca yājanam akariṣyatāpi pratimantraṇe kriyamāṇe kiñ cid virudhyate /
1.1.[50]	mahan me 'voca iti mantreṇa hi somasya mahābhāgyaṃ kīrtyate na ca tāvatā yājanam abhyupagataṃ bhavati /
1.1.[51]	tasmāt prokte some 'vicāryaiva guṇadoṣān pratimantrayeta /
1.1.[52]	kin tu yadi pūrvam eva vijñātam ayājanakāraṇaṃ prokte some buddhau pravarteta tadā pratimantraṇe 'pi nādaraḥ kāryo vyavasitatvād ayājanasya /
1.1.[53]	somapravākaśabdo 'nyatra kvādividhilakṣaṇaḥ /
1.1.[54]	kiṃ vā lakṣaṇavādena śrutir evātra lakṣaṇam //
1.5.[1]	athety ānantarye /
1.5.[2]	pratimantraṇānantaram enaṃ somapravākaṃ kac cin nāhīnā3 iti nigadena pañcārthān pṛcchati /
1.5.[3]	pāṭhakramād evānantaryasiddher athaśabdo 'narthakaḥ /
1.5.[4]	nānarthako 'tikramya pāṭhakramam arthakrameṇa pūrvaṃ pratimantraṇāt praśnasya prasajato nivṛttyarthatvāt /
1.5.[5]	atha vā sarvatrāpi na kiñ cid arthādhikyam athaśabdena kriyate /
1.5.[6]	alaṃkaraṇam evānena laukikavaidikānāṃ vākyasamudāyānāṃ prāyeṇa kriyate /
1.5.[7]	yathāthādhiśrayaty athāvadyotayaty athāpaḥ pratyānayatīti yathā ca snātavantas tīrthe vayam atha praviṣṭā gṛham atha bhuktavanta iti /
1.5.[8]	pāṭhakramād eva hi prayogakramas sidhyati /
1.5.[9]	evaṃ siddhasyaiva kramasya dṛḍhīkaraṇam athaśabdena kriyata iti vyākhyeyam /
1.5.[10]	kathaṃ punar āhiḥ pracchyartho bhavati /
1.5.[11]	praśnānām eṣān darśanād anekārthatvāc ca dhātūnāṃ pṛcchatyartho 'yam atra kalpyate /
1.5.[12]	śabdārthasāmānyāt tv anayor api sukalpyam evaitat /
1.5.[13]	vihitasyaivārthasyānuṣṭhānārhatvād avidhāyakatvāc ca laṭo brūyād iti liṅaiva vaktavyam /
1.5.[14]	nātra liṅaḥ prayojanam /
1.5.[15]	kutaḥ /
1.5.[16]	na kalpasūtrāṇi kriyamāṇāni vidhiparāṇi /
1.5.[17]	tair hi śrutivihitā eva kriyāviśeṣāḥ kramādiparijñānārtham anukramyante /
1.5.[18]	laṭaiva cāyam arthas sidhyati /
1.5.[19]	atas sūtre vidhiśabdā na dṛśyante /
1.5.[20]	yatra tu kva cid dṛśyante yathā pūrvasminn eva vākye tatrāpy avivakṣito vidhyartha iti mantavyam /
1.5.[21]	atha vā ye śrutau pratyakṣavihitāḥ padārthās te sūtre laḍantair nirdiśyante /
1.5.[22]	ye tv avihitāś śrutyā liṅgādibhir upādīyante te liṅādibhiś śabdair atra vidhīyanta iti grāhyam /
1.5.[23]	ye tu pratyakṣavihitā api vidhiśabdair evātra nirdiśyante padārthā yathā tam uttiṣṭhantam ārabhyānūttiṣṭhed bṛhatas stotraṃ pratigṛhya brūyāt pṛthivyāṃ hastau syātām ity evamādayaḥ /
1.5.[24]	teṣv ayaṃ parihāraś śrautāny evaitāni vākyāni prakṣipyanta iti /
1.5.[25]	nanu śrutāv api kriyāvidhau laḍ eva prāyeṇa dṛśyate /
1.5.[26]	yathā audumbarīm anvārabhate tam prohati pṛthivīm abhimṛśatīty evamādiṣu /
1.5.[27]	nedaṃ laṭo darśanam /
1.5.[28]	leḍ iyañ chandasi vidhāyikā vibhaktiḥ /
1.5.[29]	tasmāt sādhūktaṃ śrutivihitānāṃ sūtreṇānukramaṇam iti /
1.5.[30]	kac cin nāhīnā3 iti pañca praśnāḥ /
1.5.[31]	teṣām ayam arthaḥ /
1.5.[32]	yo bhavatā proktas somas sa kac cid ahīno na bhavati /
1.5.[33]	kac cic cāyam anūdeśyo na bhavati /
1.5.[34]	kac cid asya yajñasyārtvijyaṃ kena cid anyastam apratyākhyātam /
1.5.[35]	ke 'nena yajñena yājayanti /
1.5.[36]	kāś cāsya yajñasya dakṣiṇā iti /
1.5.[37]	prativacanasyābhāve praśnasyānarthakyaprasaṅgād acoditam api prativacanadānam arthāt somapravākena kartavyam /
1.5.[38]	nāhīnaḥ /
1.5.[39]	nānūdeśyaḥ /
1.5.[40]	na nyastam ārtvijyam /
1.5.[41]	devadattaḥ kṛṣṇarātaś śivaguptaś ca yājayanti /
1.5.[42]	dvādaśaśataṃ gāvo dakṣiṇā iti vā yathārthaṃ vā //
1.6.[1]	tasya yajamānasya janma karma rtvija ity etāni trīṇy udgātā vicārayed duṣṭāny aduṣṭānīti /
1.6.[2]	janmeti mātāpitarāv abhipretau /
1.6.[3]	karma prasiddham eva sasamācāram /
1.6.[4]	ṛtvijaś ca ye yajamānasya pratinibaddhāḥ pūrveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ kartāraḥ /
1.6.[5]	te tu mīmāṃsyante /
1.6.[6]	nanu prakṛtatvāt somapravākasyaiva tasyeti grahaṇaṃ yuktam /
1.6.[7]	naivam /
1.6.[8]	yajamānasya hi janmādivicāreṇātrārtho bhavati na somapravākasya /
1.6.[9]	arthataś ca yajamāno 'pi prakṛta eva /
1.6.[10]	yajamānasyaiva rtvijo grāhyāḥ /
1.6.[11]	trīṇīty anarthakam /
1.6.[12]	nānarthakam anyebhyo 'pi mīmāṃsebhyas trayāṇām eṣām eva mukhyatvapratipādanārthatvāt /
1.6.[13]	tataś caivaṃ grāhyam /
1.6.[14]	yady api yajamānasya janmādīnīmāni trīṇi saṃmatāny eva loke kathyante tathāpi bahuvidhair upāyair asakṛn mīmāṃsetaiva /
1.6.[15]	ye tu doṣā vātarogādayas te yadi sakāraṇam āśaṅkyeran santīti tata eva mīmāṃsyeran nānyatheti /
1.6.[16]	ṛtvijāñ ca mīmāṃsā na kevalaṃ guṇadoṣagrahaṇārthaiva /
1.6.[17]	tair apasṛṣṭasyānabhyupagamārthāpi //
1.7.[1]	janma karma rtvija ity etāny eva trīṇi yajamāna ṛtvijāṃ mīmāṃsate /
1.7.[2]	nipātadvayaṃ kimartham /
1.7.[3]	idam ucyate /
1.7.[4]	asati nipātadvaya etāni yajamāna ṛtvijāṃ mīmāṃsate nodgātā yajamānasyeti pūrvavākyārthapratiṣedhakam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhavet /
1.7.[5]	vidhidvayatvān mitho vā vākyaṃ vikalpyeta /
1.7.[6]	yathā uttarīyam upānahau chattram iti devadattāya dātavyam etad viṣṇumitrāya dātavyam ity ukte devadattāya pratiṣiddhaṃ matvā tad viṣṇumitrāyaiva dīyate /
1.7.[7]	aniyamena vā dvayor ekasmai /
1.7.[8]	tad evaśabdena nivartyate /
1.7.[9]	etāny eva yajamānasya mīmāmsitāny eveti /
1.7.[10]	evaśabde ca saty eṣām eva trayāṇām avadhāraṇam āśaṅkyeta /
1.7.[11]	etāny eva mīmāṃsyāni nāpare doṣā iti /
1.7.[12]	tan nipātānām anekārthatvād uśabdena samuccayārthena nivartyate /
1.7.[13]	etāni caiva trīṇi mukhyāny anye ca doṣā iti /
1.7.[14]	nanu yathā pūrvasmin vākye tasyety uktam arthād yajamānasyeti gṛhītam evam atrāpi sa ity eva vaktavyam /
1.7.[15]	arthād eva yajamāna iti gṛhṇīmaḥ /
1.7.[16]	nātra yajamānasyārthād grahaṇaṃ śakyate /
1.7.[17]	eṣa hi chandogānāṃ rāddhānta anādiṣṭakartṛkaṃ karmodgātrā kartavyam iti /
1.7.[18]	agnyādheyādhikāre cāyam arthas sādhu pratipādayiṣyate /
1.7.[19]	tasmād yajamānagrahaṇam acodyam /
1.7.[20]	kim idam udgātṛkarmavācini sūtre yājamānaṃ karmocyate /
1.7.[21]	atra brūmaḥ /
1.7.[22]	iha yajñe pañca padārthā hautram ādhvaryavam audgātraṃ brahmatvaṃ yājamānam iti /
1.7.[23]	teṣān trayo hautrādayas tribhir vedair vyavasthayā vidhīyante brahmatvayājamāne tu sarvair api /
1.7.[24]	na tau sākalyenaikasmin vede vidhīyete /
1.7.[25]	tasmād acodyaṃ yajamānakarmavacanam /
1.7.[26]	evam iyam ṛtvigyajamānaguṇadoṣaviṣayā mīmāṃsā kṛtā /
1.7.[27]	tasyāḥ prayojanam uttaratra vakṣyate //
1.8.[1]	tatrāhuḥ ko 'sāv ahīno yaḥ pūrvaṃ pṛcchatābhipreta iti /
1.8.[2]	ahīnayājane doṣam āśaṅkya pṛṣṭaṃ kac cin nāhīnā3 iti /
1.8.[3]	prasiddhānāñ ca dvirātrādīnām ahīnānām ārtvijyaṃ kartuṃ yuktam eva /
1.8.[4]	dvādaśāhabrāhmaṇe hi tad āhur yājayitavyan dvādaśāhenā3 nā3 iti neti brūyād ity adhikṛtya tasmād dvādaśāhena naiva yājayed iti pūrvam uktvā tad u vā āhur yājayitavyam eveti yājanapakṣa eva sthāpitaḥ /
1.8.[5]	tasmād dvādaśāhena tāvad yājayitavyam /
1.8.[6]	tatprakṛtitvād dvirātrādibhir api /
1.8.[7]	tasmād anyo 'sāv ahīnaḥ pṛṣṭo yasyārtvijyaṃ doṣavad iti matvā tacchravaṇārtho 'yaṃ praśnaḥ kriyate tad āhuḥ ko 'hīna iti //
1.10.[1]	idaṃ pūrvasya prativacanam /
1.10.[2]	atirātraḥ prathamo 'hīna ity āhur ācāryāḥ /
1.10.[3]	na hi so 'horātrayoḥ kiñcid api hīyata iti /
1.10.[4]	prathamagrahaṇam anarthakam /
1.10.[5]	nānarthakan dvirātrādīnām apy upādānārthatvāt /
1.10.[6]	ayam arthaḥ /
1.10.[7]	atirātraḥ prathamo 'hīnaḥ prasiddhāś ca dvirātrādaya iti /
1.10.[8]	atirātrasya tv ahīnatvenāprasiddher hetur upādīyate /
1.10.[9]	nanv evam ucyamāne dvirātrādibhir api yājanan doṣavat syāt /
1.10.[10]	bhavatu /
1.10.[11]	doṣavad eva hi tair yājanam /
1.10.[12]	tathā hi śrūyate tasmād dvādaśāhena na yājyam pāpmano vyāvṛttyā iti /
1.10.[13]	atha vā vaikalpikam ahīnayājanan tad u vā āhur yājayitavyam evety asmād vacanāt tasmād dvādaśāhena na yājyam iti paravacanāc ca /
1.10.[14]	ācāryeṇāpi kac cin nāhīnā3 iti praśnavacanakaraṇād doṣavad ahīnayājanaṃ khyāpitam anūdeśyādāv iva tu pratiṣedhākaraṇād anumatañ ca /
1.10.[15]	tasmād atra vikalpa eva yuktaḥ /
1.10.[16]	athāparaṃ vyākhyānam /
1.10.[17]	atirātraḥ prathamaḥ prathamaṃ prayujyamāno 'hīnaḥ /
1.10.[18]	so 'muṣmin praśne 'bhipretaḥ /
1.10.[19]	śrūyate hi tad āhur na prathamaṃ yajamāno 'tirātreṇa yajetetīti /
1.10.[20]	yady api yajanam evātra pratiṣidhyate yājanam apy arthāt pratiṣiddhaṃ bhavati /
1.10.[21]	yajanaṃ hīdaṃ pratiṣiddhatvād doṣavat /
1.10.[22]	tat kurvato yājanam api doṣāyaiva syāt /
1.10.[23]	tatparihārārthaṃ praśnaḥ kriyate /
1.10.[24]	kim ayaṃ prathamasomo 'tirātro na bhavatīti /
1.10.[25]	nanv atirātrasya dvitīyādāv api prayoge 'horātrayor avayavād ekasmād apy ahīnatvaṃ hetur vidyate /
1.10.[26]	tataś cedaṃ prasajati /
1.10.[27]	sarveṇātirātreṇa na yājayed iti /
1.10.[28]	tatra prathamaśabdo 'narthakaḥ /
1.10.[29]	nānarthakaḥ prathama eva prayogo 'hīno na dvitīyādir ity etadarthatvāt /
1.10.[30]	na hi hetusadbhāvamātreṇa dvitīyādiprayogo 'hīno bhavati /
1.10.[31]	vacanād idam atirātrasyāhīnatvam tac ca vacanaṃ prayogāśrayam eva /
1.10.[32]	nanv asādhāraṇena hetunā bhavitavyam /
1.10.[33]	satyam etat /
1.10.[34]	yatra hetunaivārthas sādhyate tatra hetur asādhāraṇa eva pradarśyate /
1.10.[35]	yathā anityaś śabdaḥ kṛtakatvād agnir atra dhūmadarśanād iti /
1.10.[36]	iha tu vacanenaivāhīnatvaṃ siddham hetus tv anaikāntiko 'pi tatra sattāmātram avalambya pradarśyate /
1.10.[37]	yathā loka aitihyapramāṇasiddhe sāsnādimati gośabde gamanād gaur iti gamanasadbhāvo gośabdapravṛttau kāraṇaṃ vyapadiśyate na ca tāvatā gotvam aśvādeḥ prasajati /
1.10.[38]	yathā ca vede śūrpeṇa juhotīti śūrpaṃ homakaraṇatvena vidhāya tena hy annaṃ kriyata iti vākyaśeṣeṇānnakaraṇatvaṃ hetur ucyate /
1.10.[39]	tathāpi śūrpeṇaiva hūyate na darvyādinā /
1.10.[40]	evam atrāpy atirātraḥ prathamo 'hīna ity āhur ity etāvataiva vacanena prathamaṃ prayujyamānasyātirātrasyāhīnatvaṃ siddham /
1.10.[41]	hetus tv ayaṃ sādhāraṇo 'py ahīnaśabdasyātra pravṛttinimittatvena pradarśyate dvitīyādeś ca prayogasyāhīnatve vacanan na paśyāmaḥ /
1.10.[42]	tataś caivaṃ siddham prathamasomena satātirātreṇa na yājayitavyam iti //
1.13.[1]	anūdeśyena yajñena na yājayet /
1.13.[2]	yasmin hi deśa antaśśavo grāmo bhavati tatrānadhyayanaṃ bhavati /
1.13.[3]	yajñaś cāyam antaśśavo yo 'nūdeśya iti /
1.13.[4]	tryavayavam idaṃ vākyam /
1.13.[5]	anūdeśyena na yājayed iti pratijñā /
1.13.[6]	yatra nv antaśśavo grāmo bhavati tad anadhyāyo bhavatīti dṛṣṭāntaḥ /
1.13.[7]	antaśśava eṣa yajño yo 'nūdeśya ity ayaṃ hetuḥ /
1.13.[8]	kaḥ punar ayam anūdeśyo nāma /
1.13.[9]	śunaskarṇastoma iti brūmaḥ /
1.13.[10]	sa hi maraṇakāmasya yajñaḥ /
1.13.[11]	tatas tena na yājayitavyam /
1.13.[12]	anūdeśyo vyākhyātavyaḥ /
1.13.[13]	evaṃ sa ity anūdeśyo bhavati /
1.13.[14]	antaśśavaś cāyaṃ yajñamadhya eva yajamānasya maraṇāt /
1.13.[15]	atha vā yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyeteti dīkṣitamaraṇam adhikṛtya saṃvatsare 'sthīni yājayeyur iti vihito 'sthiyajño nāma vidyate /
1.13.[16]	so 'nudiśyamānatvān mṛtaṃ praty anūdeśyo bhavati antaśśavatvañ ca tasya vidyate /
1.13.[17]	evaṃ hi tatra śrūyate stotre stotre 'sthikumbham upanidadhātīti //
1.15.[1]	nyastaṃ kena cit pratyākhyātam ārtvijyaṃ yasya yajñasya sa yajño nyastārtvijyaḥ /
1.15.[2]	tan na kuryāt /
1.15.[3]	itthañ ca tatra pratyācakṣīta /
1.15.[4]	yad eva te duṣṭaṃ karma pūrvas tvayā vṛtaḥ parivadan nyasyāt tad eva te vayam api paricakṣmahā iti /
1.15.[5]	vijñātam api doṣan na vadet /
1.15.[6]	evam eva pratyācakṣīta //
1.16.[1]	athāpi hetusamuccayārthaḥ /
1.16.[2]	nyastārtvijyasya yajñasyākaraṇe 'yam api hetuḥ /
1.16.[3]	nyastam ity etenaiva śabdena hetunā na kuryāt /
1.16.[4]	doṣas tu vijñāyeta vā na vā //
1.17.[1]	yaḥ pūrvaḥ praśnaḥ ke yājayantīti so 'yam anūdyate /
1.17.[2]	anyavivakṣayā ke yājayantītīdam adhikṛtya kiñ cid vakṣyata ity arthaḥ /
1.17.[3]	atha vā ke yājayantīti pṛcchatā kim abhipretam iti //
1.18.[1]	anūcānā vidvāṃsaḥ /
1.18.[2]	praśastabāndhavā bandhumantaḥ /
1.18.[3]	vihite karmaṇi pravartamānāḥ pratiṣiddhān nivartamānās sucaritinaḥ /
1.18.[4]	tatraivaṃ yojyam /
1.18.[5]	anūcānā eva rtvijo yājayanti /
1.18.[6]	anūcānam eva yajamānaṃ yājayanti /
1.18.[7]	bandhumanta evartvijo yājayanti /
1.18.[8]	bandhumantam eva yajamānaṃ yājayanti /
1.18.[9]	sucaritina evartvijo yājayanti /
1.18.[10]	sucaritinam eva yajamānaṃ yājayanti /
1.18.[11]	iti nyāya iti /
1.18.[12]	tatrāyam arthaḥ /
1.18.[13]	sarveṣām ṛtvigyajamānānām anūcānatvādiguṇābhilāṣayā yasmāt praśnaḥ kṛtas tasmād evaṃvidhā evartvijo yājayeyur evaṃvidham eva yajamānaṃ yājayeyur iti //
1.19.[1]	anūcānair eva rtvigbhis saha yājayen naikenāpy ananūcānena //
1.20.[1]	kṛṣṇañ janma yasya sa kṛṣṇajanmā /
1.20.[2]	duṣṭajanmety arthaḥ /
1.20.[3]	mātāpitṛdoṣeṇa ca janmano doṣaḥ /
1.20.[4]	tasmād apraśastamātāpitṛkan na yājayed ity arthaḥ //
1.21.[1]	pāpakarmāṇaṃ pratiṣiddhasevinan na yājayet //
1.23.[1]	anūcānā evetyādivacanata evānanūcānakṛṣṇajanmapāpakarmaṇām ṛtvigyajamānānām aprasaṅgād anūcānair evetyādīni pañcāpi vākyāny anarthakāni /
1.23.[2]	nānarthakāni yadi vacanam anādṛtyārthayaśo'bhilāṣādinā nimittena rtvijāṃ ke cid yajamāno vā yajñavidhau pravarteran tatra svayam anūcānatvādisaṃpadyukto 'pi tair asaṃparkārthaṃ yājanān nivartetety evamarthatvāt /
1.23.[3]	atha vānūcānā eveti śrautam etad vākyam ity apunaruktatā vācyā /
1.23.[4]	nanv anūcānam eva yājayed ity etad api vaktavyam /
1.23.[5]	satyam etat /
1.23.[6]	ananūcānasyāpi yajñaprasaṅgo vidyata iti jñāpanārthan nocyate /
1.23.[7]	evañ ca bahvṛcānāṃ pravargyādhikāre vacanam /
1.23.[8]	tan na prathamayajñe pravṛñjyāt /
1.23.[9]	upanāmuka evainam uttaro yajño bhavati yaḥ prathamayajñe na pravṛṇakti /
1.23.[10]	kāman tu yo 'nūcānaś śrotriyas syāt tasya pravṛñjyāt /
1.23.[11]	ātmā vai sa yajñasyātmanaiva tad yajñaṃ samardhayatīti /
1.23.[12]	ato 'pi hi vacanād ananūcānasyāpi yajño 'stīti nāyuktaṃ grahītum //
1.24.[1]	kā dakṣiṇā ity atra kiñ cid vakṣyate //
1.25.[1]	dakṣiṇā na pṛcched iti śāṭyāyanir ācārya āha sma ha sa uktavān kila /
1.25.[2]	ayañ ca hetuḥ /
1.25.[3]	vikrayasya tad rūpaṃ yad dakṣiṇāpraśna iti /
1.25.[4]	yathā loke paṭādīni vikrīṇantaṃ pṛcchanti kiṃ bhavatādeyam iti tadvad atrāpy ārtvijyārthaṃ prārthitena dakṣiṇāsu pṛcchyamānāsu vikrayasya rūpaṃ bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ /
1.25.[5]	tasmāt kā dakṣiṇā iti na pṛcchet //
1.26.[1]	pratiṣiddhasya praśnasya punaḥ pratiprasavaḥ kriyate /
1.26.[2]	pṛcched dakṣiṇā ity āha sma ha tāṇḍya ācāryaḥ /
1.26.[3]	ayañ ca hetuḥ /
1.26.[4]	yad etad dakṣiṇā iti kīrtyata etatphalo vai yajña iti /
1.26.[5]	dakṣiṇāphalo hi yajña ity arthaḥ /
1.26.[6]	nanu svargādiphalo yajño na dakṣiṇāphalaḥ /
1.26.[7]	satyam etat /
1.26.[8]	dakṣiṇābhis tu phalaṃ sādhyate /
1.26.[9]	tatra sādhanabhūtāsu dakṣiṇāsu sādhanavyapadeśo gauṇaḥ praśaṃsārthaḥ /
1.26.[10]	nanu phalasādhanatvam api dakṣiṇānān nāsti yajñasyaiva tad iti /
1.26.[11]	yady api nāsti dakṣiṇās svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayantīti liṅgāt sad ivopacaryate /
1.26.[12]	tatrāyam arthaḥ /
1.26.[13]	hīnadakṣiṇo yajñaḥ phalan na sādhayet /
1.26.[14]	phalasādhanasamarthenaiva ca yajñena yājayitavyam /
1.26.[15]	tasmād yajñasyaiva sāphalyacikīrṣayā dakṣiṇāḥ praṣṭavyā iti /
1.26.[16]	atha vaitatphalo vai yajña ṛtvijām iti vyākhyeyam /
1.26.[17]	dakṣiṇālābha eva hi phalaṃ yajñena rtvijāṃ sādhyate nānyat /
1.26.[18]	yadi ca dakṣiṇā na syur akaraṇīyam ārtvijyaṃ syāt /
1.26.[19]	tasmāt praṣṭavyā eva dakṣiṇā iti /
1.26.[20]	nanu pūrvasmin vākye pratiṣiddhatvād atra ca punarvihitatvād vaikalpiko dakṣiṇāpraśnaḥ /
1.26.[21]	neti brūmaḥ /
1.26.[22]	praśnanigade nityavac chrutatvād anitya eva pratiṣedhaḥ /
1.26.[23]	pratiṣedha idānīm kimarthaḥ /
1.26.[24]	dravyalobhena na pṛcched ity evamarthaḥ /
1.26.[25]	evañ cet punarvidhiḥ kimarthaḥ /
1.26.[26]	asati punarvidhau pūrvaṃ vacanaṃ pratiṣedhakam eva kevalaṃ praśnasya gṛhyeta /
1.26.[27]	tat punarvidhinā nivartyate /
1.26.[28]	vākyadvaye 'py ācāryagrahaṇaṃ pūjārtham eva //
1.27.[1]	sa evaṃ yājane guṇadoṣān mīmāṃsitavān udgātā yājayiṣyan yadi syād ābhimukhyena gacched yajñaṃ yajamānaṃ vā /
1.27.[2]	uktadoṣasadbhāve yājanapratiṣedhāt tadabhāve yājayiṣyan bhavati /
1.27.[3]	tatrāpy aniyama iti cen na yājanasyāpi ṣaṭkarmasv antarbhāvāt teṣāñ ca brāhmaṇasya vihitatvāt /
1.27.[4]	nanu yajanadānādhyayanāny eva smṛtikārair niyamyante na yājanapratigrahādhyāpanāni /
1.27.[5]	satyam etat /
1.27.[6]	itthan tu yājanādīnām aniyamaḥ /
1.27.[7]	yajanādivat svayaṃ prayatnena yājanādiṣu nāvaśyaṃ pravartitavyam iti /
1.27.[8]	tasmād aprayatnopanateṣu yājanādiṣu doṣābhāve pravartetaiva /
1.27.[9]	sati doṣe pratyācakṣīta //
1.28.[1]	sa udgātā dīkṣitaṃ yakṣyamāṇaṃ yadi gacchet tasyottarata upaviśya tam ātmānaṃ prati somaṃ pravācayeta /
1.28.[2]	nanu pūrvam eva somaḥ proktaḥ /
1.28.[3]	kim idānīṃ procyate /
1.28.[4]	anyaviṣayam evaitat somapravacanam /
1.28.[5]	yadi svayam evāprārthito dakṣiṇālābhanimittam ārtvijyaṃ kartum icchet tatrāsya viṣayaḥ /
1.28.[6]	asti ca śrutivacanam /
1.28.[7]	tasmād udgātāvṛta uttarato niveśanaṃ lipseta /
1.28.[8]	etad dhy anāruddhan niveśanaṃ yad uttarata iti /
1.28.[9]	avṛtasyodgātur uttarato niveśanaṃ kartavyam ucyate /
1.28.[10]	tad idam uktam uttarata upaviśya pravācayeteti /
1.28.[11]	sa iti cātra vacanam evam evopapadyate /
1.28.[12]	pūrvasmād api vākyāt sa iti śakyam anuvartayitum anyaviṣayatājñāpanārtham eva tv asya punaḥ prayujyate /
1.28.[13]	tatraivam uttarata upaviśyātmānaṃ prati somasya pravācane yajidhātuḥ prayojyate /
1.28.[14]	tataḥ prokte some mahan me 'voca ity ārabheta //
1.29.[1]	dīkṣitaṃ yajamānaṃ yadi gacched abhidrutyābhimukhyena taṃ samīpaṃ gatvābhivādayeta praśaṃset /
1.29.[2]	yajñārabdhiś śobhanā kṛteti brūyāt //
1.30.[1]	asmād abhivādanād udgātrā kṛtād ūrdhvaṃ yajamāna evodgātāram abhigacchati pariveṣaṇāya paricaraṇāya /
1.30.[2]	evety anarthakam /
1.30.[3]	nānarthakam vayasā jñānādinā vā yady api garīyān udgātur yajamāna syāt tathāpi svayam evodgātāram abhigatya satkuryād ity etadarthatvāt /
1.30.[4]	ata ūrdhvam ity anarthakam /
1.30.[5]	nānarthakam ahar ahar ā yajñaparisamāpter udgātā satkartavya ity etadarthatvāt //
2.1.[1]	gamanānantaram asmā udgātra āsanam āharanti yajamānapuruṣāḥ /
2.1.[2]	bahuvacanaprayogād aniyamena yaḥ kaś cid yajamānapuruṣa āharati nāvaśyaṃ bahava eva //
2.2.[1]	tasminn āsana upaviśati vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa //
2.3.[1]	tasmād āsanād anena mantreṇa yat tṛṇaṃ pratiśuṣkāgraṃ bhavati yad vā tṛṇaṃ praticchinnāgraṃ bhavati tan nirasyati /
2.3.[2]	pratiśuṣkāgram bhavati pratichinnāgraṃ vety etāvatā siddhe yad veti bruvann ubhayor api sator ekam eva nirasanīyam iti jñāpayati /
2.3.[3]	nanv ayatnasiddham etat /
2.3.[4]	asinā paraśunā vā chindyād ity ukte tayor ekenaiva chindanti hi /
2.3.[5]	[neti brūmaḥ /] na hi tenaitat tulyam /
2.3.[6]	nātra nirasanakriyāṃ prati tṛṇaṃ karaṇatvena codyate karaṇavibhakter aśravaṇāt /
2.3.[7]	karmatvena tu śravaṇāt tṛṇam atra pradhānam /
2.3.[8]	nirasanan tasya guṇabhūtam /
2.3.[9]	tatra tṛṇabhede tadguṇasya nirasanasyāvṛttir yuktā /
2.3.[10]	pratipradhānaṃ hi guṇabhedan nyāyavido vadanti /
2.3.[11]	loke ca śvā kāko vā nivāritavya ity ukte dvayam apy āgacchan nivāryate /
2.3.[12]	tadvad atrāpi dvividhasyāpi satas tṛṇasya nirasanaprasaktāv ekasyaiva nirasanārthaṃ yatno 'yaṃ kriyate /
2.3.[13]	tṛṇanirasanānyathānupapatteś śiṣṭācāratas tṛṇāstaraṇam āsane sidhyati //
2.4.[1]	tṛṇanirasanānantaram apa upaspṛśyānena mantreṇāsanam upaviśati /
2.4.[2]	anenaivopaveśanavidhinā siddhatvāt tasminn upaviśatīti pūrvaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
2.4.[3]	nānarthakan tṛṇanirasanasyopaveśanāṅgatvapratipādanārthatvāt /
2.4.[4]	upaveśanam adhikṛtya hy uktan tṛṇanirasanan tadaṅgaṃ syān nānyathā /
2.4.[5]	aṅgatvajñāpanañ ca kṛtasyānāvṛttir guṇalopa ity evamādyartham //
2.5.[1]	athāsmā āsīnāyodakam āharanti /
2.5.[2]	avacane 'pi śiṣṭācāratas tenodakena pādau prakṣālyācāmati /
2.5.[3]	āhṛtena codakenāvaśyam arthaḥ kāryas sa cāyam ācārata eṣa eva grāhyo nānyaḥ //
2.6.[1]	tad ity udakam evocyate /
2.6.[2]	punar anyad udakam āhṛtam anayarcā pratigṛhṇāti /
2.6.[3]	grahaṇacodanāyāṃ hy āharaṇam arthasiddham /
2.6.[4]	nanu pūrvasmin vākye yasyodakasyāharaṇan tasyaivedaṃ pratigrahaṇam iti vaktuṃ yuktam /
2.6.[5]	satyam /
2.6.[6]	ittham api vaktuṃ śakyam /
2.6.[7]	pādaprakṣālanācamanayos tu lopa eva prasajati /
2.6.[8]	tasmāt pūrvam eva vyākhyānaṃ sādhīyaḥ /
2.6.[9]	anyasya karaṇasyānuktatvāt pareṣāñ ca vacanād añjalinā pratigṛhṇāti /
2.6.[10]	ādigrahaṇenārthasiddhes samastāyā ṛco vacanam anarthakam /
2.6.[11]	nānarthakam ṛcaṃ vadan pratigṛhṇātīty etadarthatvāt /
2.6.[12]	eṣa hi nyāyaḥ /
2.6.[13]	karmakaraṇamantreṣu mantrānte karmārambha iti /
2.6.[14]	tathā coktaṃ kauṣītakinā mantrāntena karaṇesu karmaṇas sannipātanam iti /
2.6.[15]	tad atrāsyā ṛcas samastapāṭhena nivartyate /
2.6.[16]	tat kathaṃ bhavati /
2.6.[17]	idam ucyate /
2.6.[18]	vacanavairūpyam etad ācāryeṇa kriyate yad asmacchākhāntarbhūtānām eva rcāṃ kāsāñ cit pratīkaṃ gṛhṇāti pavitran te san te payāṃsīty evamādīnām kāsāñ cit pāṭhaṃ karoti yathā mayi varcas sadasas patim iti /
2.6.[19]	tad anena vacanavairūpyeṇārthavairūpyaṃ gṛhyate /
2.6.[20]	pratīkagṛhītānām ante karmārambhaḥ paṭhitānām ādāv iti /
2.6.[21]	tasmād asyā ādāv evodakagrahaṇam ārabdhavyaṃ sadasas patim ity asyāś ca sadaḥprapadanam /
2.6.[22]	kiñ cit sadaḥprapadane 'sya vyākhyānasya sahakāripratyayo 'py upodbalako vidyate /
2.6.[23]	pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ prapadyante /
2.6.[24]	sādhyā devā anu mā prasarpata /
2.6.[25]	indra tridhātu śaraṇaṃ yata indra bhayāmahe sadasas patim iti japanta iti /
2.6.[26]	tatas tatra tāvad etad vyākhyānaṃ yuktataram /
2.6.[27]	tat tatsāmānyād atrāpi sthālīpulākanyāyenaivam eva niścetavyam /aikasvaryārthaḥ pāṭha iti ke cid vyācakṣate /
2.6.[28]	tad ayuktam /
2.6.[29]	traisvaryapaṭhitānāṃ hi karaṇamantrāṇām aikasvaryaṃ ke cid ācāryā necchanti /
2.6.[30]	mantrādau punaḥ katipayānāṃ karmaṇām ārambhaḥ paratantreṣv api dṛśyate /
2.6.[31]	tatra kva cid upalabdhasyaivārthasya jñāpakabalena grahaṇam upapannan nānupalabdhasya /
2.6.[32]	tasmād uktārtha eva pāṭho naikasvaryārthaḥ /
2.6.[33]	atha vodakagrahaṇasadaḥprapadane prati liṅgasāmarthyam anayor ṛcor pāṭhena pradarśyate tac cāsatyām api codanāyām anayor ṛcor asmin karmadvaye 'vagamanārtham /
2.6.[34]	tasmād gṛhyokte 'pi madhuparke 'rghyam udakam mayi varca ity anayaivarcā pratigrāhyam /
2.6.[35]	sadasas patim ity anayaiva tṛtīyasavane 'pi sadaḥ praveṣṭavyam /
2.6.[36]	evam idan dvividhaṃ prayojanam ṛkpāṭhasya //
2.7.[1]	prasiddhaṃ madhupadenātra dadhno grahaṇam /
2.7.[2]	avacanād [vā] kevalam eva madhv āhartavyam //
2.8.[1]	tan madhu catasṛbhir aṅgulībhir aṅguṣṭhacaturthābhis triḥ prāśnāti /
2.8.[2]	sahāṅguṣṭhena pañcabhir iti cen na /
2.8.[3]	yadi hy evam aiṣiṣyata sarvābhiḥ pañcabhir ity evāvakṣyata /
2.8.[4]	aṅguṣṭhacaturthatvañ ca prāśanasaukaryārtham avyavadhānārthañ ca kaniṣṭhikayā vinā saṃpādyam //
2.9.[1]	anena mantreṇa prāśnāti /
2.9.[2]	ekavākyatvenaiva mantrasya prāśanasaṃbandhasiddheḥ prāśnātīty anarthakam /
2.9.[3]	nānarthakaṃ pratiprāśanaṃ mantrāvṛttipratipādanārthatvāt /
2.9.[4]	itarathā hi guṇānāñ ca parārthatvād asaṃbandhas samatvāt syād iti nyāyāt prāśanaguṇenābhyāsena mantro na saṃbadhyeta /
2.9.[5]	atas tu yatnāt saṃbadhyate //
2.11.[1]	ācamanānantaram asmai vāsasī āharanti /
2.11.[2]	śriyai rūpam iti ṣaṣṭhyartheyañ caturthī /
2.11.[3]	śriyo hi rūpaṃ vastrayugam /
2.11.[4]	śrīrūpatayā ca vacanāc chobhane vāsasī āhartavye /
2.11.[5]	atiśobhanaṃ hi dravyaṃ śrīrūpam iti loke prasiddham //
2.12.[1]	te vāsasī anena mantreṇa yathāyogaṃ paridhatte /
2.12.[2]	prativastrañ ca mantra āvartate //
2.13.[1]	pravartau kuṇḍale /
2.13.[2]	srajo mālāḥ /
2.13.[3]	alaṃkaraṇam anyad bhūṣaṇam /
2.13.[4]	tāny asmā āharanti /
2.13.[5]	alaṃkaraṇagrahaṇenaiva siddhe pravartau sraja iti pṛthaggrahaṇam anarthakam /
2.13.[6]	nānarthakaṃ pravartayos srajāñ ca niyamārthatvāt /
2.13.[7]	tasmād avaśyaṃ pravartau srajaś cāhartavyā yathopapādam anyad alaṃkaraṇam /
2.13.[8]	itikaraṇaprayogād anyad api yad asmai śraddhayā dīyate tasyāpy ayam eva kālaḥ /
2.13.[9]	atha vā pravartau sraja ity evamādy alaṃkaraṇam asmā āharantīti vyākhyeyam /
2.13.[10]	tatra ca pravartagrahaṇaṃ kaṭakakaṭisūtrāṅgulīyakādīnām upalakṣaṇārtham sraggrahaṇam añjanānulepanādīnām iti mantavyam /
2.13.[11]	vividheṣv api dravyeṣu pravartayos srajāñ ca mukhyatvād atropādānaṃ kriyate //
2.14.[1]	āhṛtenālaṃkaraṇenālaṃkṛtam enaṃ yajamāno 'nena mantreṇa vṛṇīte /
2.14.[2]	yathodgātrā śrūyeta tathā mantraṃ brūyāt //
2.16.[1]	taṃ yajamānam udgātānena mantreṇopāṃśu pratimantrayate /
2.16.[2]	itikaraṇādhyāhāreṇa vyākhyeyam //
2.17.[1]	om ity uccaiḥ //
2.17.[2]	pratimantrayeta //
2.18.[1]	devā ijyante 'sminn iti devayajanam /
2.18.[2]	devayajanaśabdo yajñabhūmau pravartate /
2.18.[3]	pratimantraṇānantaram enaṃ yajamāna eva devayajanaṃ yācati /
2.18.[4]	adṛṣṭārtham idaṃ yācanan na yāgadeśalabdhyartham /
2.18.[5]	katham avagamyate /
2.18.[6]	hotrādibhyo yācyamānatvāt /
2.18.[7]	yadi hi dṛṣṭārthas syād ekasmād eva labdhe deśe yāgasiddher anyebhyo labdhir vyarthā bhavet /
2.18.[8]	na ca yajamāna ṛtvigbhyo dravyam ādātum arhati /
2.18.[9]	ātmārthaṃ hi yajñe pravartamāna svena dravyeṇa svaiḥ karmakarais svasmin deśe svayam ṛtvigbhyo 'pi dattvā pravartitum arhati /
2.18.[10]	tasmād devayajanayācanād adṛṣṭaṃ phalam /
2.18.[11]	atha vā pūjāvacanam etad aupacārikam /
2.18.[12]	sarvasvan tubhyaṃ mayā niveditam /
2.18.[13]	devayajanam api deśan tvam eva me dehīti /
2.18.[14]	atha vā devayajanayācanadvāreṇa yajñasyaivāyaṃ prārambho 'nujñāpyate //
2.19.[1]	taṃ yajamānam udgātā tathety upāṃśu pratimantrayate //
2.20.[1]	om ity evoccaiḥ pratimantrayate /
2.20.[2]	om ity uccair iti pūrvoktasyaiva vacanād evakāraḥ prayukto nārthaviśeṣaṇārthaḥ //
2.21.[1]	pūrvam evāsanabhojanaśayanādyartham ṛtvijāṃ gṛhāṇi parikalpitāni bhavanti /
2.21.[2]	tadadhikṛtam idam ucyate /
2.21.[3]	athāsmā ātmārthaṃ parikalpitaṃ gṛhaṃ praviṣṭāya gām upājanti samīpan nayanti /atha vāvasatham upapannāyeti heturūpeṇocyate /
2.21.[4]	anyasmā apy ṛtvigbhyaś śreyase svagṛhaṃ praviṣṭāya gor upājanārtham //
2.22.[1]	tāṃ gām upanītām hanti /
2.22.[2]	ajer niṣṭhāyām aniḍbhāvaḥ /
2.22.[3]	hanteś cātmanepadañ chandasi bahulavacanād yuktam /
2.22.[4]	dṛśyate ca gām upāṣṭāṃ hanīta /
2.22.[5]	pāpmānam eva tad dhata iti /
2.22.[6]	cchando'nukaraṇārtham atrāpy evaṃ prayujyate /
2.22.[7]	arthavādo vākyaśeṣaḥ /
2.22.[8]	tasyāyam arthaḥ /
2.22.[9]	yathā pāpmano hananam evam asmin viṣaye gohananam apīti /
2.22.[10]	tasmād asmin goghāte doṣo na śaṅkyaḥ //
2.24.[1]	atha yadi tāṃ gām utsṛjed etenaiva mantreṇa gaur dhenur ityādinā tṛṇāny attv ityantenānumantryaum utsṛjatety uccair utsṛjet /
2.24.[2]	nanv anumantraṇasyāśrutatvād gaur dhenur ityādir utsṛjatetyantas sarvo 'yam utsarjanamantra eva bhavitum arhati /
2.24.[3]	naivam /
2.24.[4]	praṇavāt pūrveṇetikaraṇena kṛtena gaur dhenur ity asya mantrasyānto vijñāpyate na cānena kartavyā kriyocyate /
2.24.[5]	utsarjanan tv om utsṛjatety anenaiva liṅgāt kartavyam /
2.24.[6]	tatra tām anumantrayate gaur dhenur iti gṛhye dṛṣṭatvād anumantryety adhyāhriyate /
2.24.[7]	etenaivety anarthakam /
2.24.[8]	nānarthakam etenaiva pāpmano hananena hetunotsṛjed ity evamarthatvāt /
2.24.[9]	ayam abhiprāyaḥ /
2.24.[10]	hanane goḥ pāpmano hananaṃ bhavati gām upāṣṭāṃ hanīta /
2.24.[11]	pāpmānam eva tad dhata iti śrutivacanāt /
2.24.[12]	utsarjane 'pi hiṃsāvarjanāt pāpmaiva hanyata iti /
2.24.[13]	atha vaitenaiva gaur dhenur ity asya mantrasya liṅgeneti vyākhyeyam /
2.24.[14]	kiṃ punar ime hananotsarjane gos tulyaṃ vikalpyete /
2.24.[15]	kas sandehaḥ /
2.24.[16]	kin tūtsarjanapakṣa evāsmin kāle śiṣṭair ācaryate //
3.1.[1]	rājeti somaḥ kīrtyate /
3.1.[2]	dṛśyate hi somaṃ rājānaṃ varuṇaṃ somo rājā bhūto vāsītyādau some rājaśabdaḥ /
3.1.[3]	tadanukaraṇam ācāryeṇa kriyate /
3.1.[4]	krīte some subrahmaṇyam āmantrayante /
3.1.[5]	karmakālo bhavatah prāpta ity avabodhayanti //
3.3.[1]	sa subrahmaṇyo yajñopavītaṃ kṛtvāpa ācamya dakṣiṇena pāṇinā palāśaśākhāṃ vā śamīśākhāṃ vādāya rājavāhanasyānasaś cakrañ cānaḍvāhañ cāntareṇa dakṣiṇām īṣām anu prasṛpyāntarīṣe īṣayor madhye tiṣṭhann aniruktāṃ subrahmaṇyān trir āhvayaty upāṃśu /
3.3.[2]	evam evāhvayati subrahmaṇyoṃ subrahmaṇyoṃ subrahmaṇyom iti /
3.3.[3]	śaucārthasyācamanasya yajñopavītasya ca smṛtisiddhatvād atra tadvacanam anarthakam /
3.3.[4]	nānarthakam ajinaṃ vāso vā dakṣiṇata upavīya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum uddharate 'vadhatte savyam iti yajñopavītam iti śrutivacanasiddhasyājinasya vāsaso vā dvitīyasya yajñopavītasya kriyāṅgabhūtasya cānyasyācamanasya vidhānārthatvāt /
3.3.[5]	tasmād asaty api svapnādāv ācamananimitte karmādāv ācāmed uttarīyañ ca vastrājinayor anyatarat karmaṇy upādadīta /
3.3.[6]	avyavāyena ca rājāhavanīyayoḥ praviśet /
3.3.[7]	kim atra dakṣiṇeneti vacanād anyatrāvacane pāṇyor ekenāniyamena karmāṇi kriyeran /
3.3.[8]	naivam /
3.3.[9]	dakṣiṇenaiva pāṇinā tāny api kriyeran /
3.3.[10]	tathā ca pareṣāṃ vacanam ekāṅgavacane dakṣiṇaṃ pratīyād iti /
3.3.[11]	evam eva śiṣṭair ācaryate /
3.3.[12]	yāni tu karmāṇi vidhim anapekṣyārthād eva prāpnuvanti dṛṣṭārthāni tāni savyenāpi kriyeran /
3.3.[13]	yathedaṃ śākhādānaṃ śākhayā saṃspṛśatīti vacane 'saty arthaprāptam /
3.3.[14]	tad asmin dakṣiṇasyāpi prāptis savyasyāpi /
3.3.[15]	tatra dakṣiṇasyāyan niyamaḥ /
3.3.[16]	evañ cet ājyasthālīṃ sasruvām ādāyetyādau savyasyāpi prasaṅgaḥ /
3.3.[17]	bhavatu /
3.3.[18]	tathaivāsmābhir iṣyate /
3.3.[19]	trir iti vacanād eva siddher abhyastapāṭho 'narthakaḥ /
3.3.[20]	nānarthako niruktāyān dṛṣṭayos traisvaryāvasānayor asyām api prāpnuvator nivartanārthatvāt /
3.3.[21]	katham anayor asyāṃ prāptiḥ /
3.3.[22]	idam ucyate /
3.3.[23]	yan niruktāyās subrahmaṇyāyāḥ pratīkan tasyaiveyaṃ saṃjñānirukteti /
3.3.[24]	evaṃ hi parair iyam aniruktā kva cid vidhīyate subrahmaṇyāpratīkan trir upāṃśv abhivyāhṛtyeti /
3.3.[25]	tatrāyam anirukteti bahuvrīhisamāsa iti /
3.3.[26]	atha vā śrutyanukaraṇārtho 'yam abhyastapāṭhaḥ /
3.3.[27]	tasmāt traisvaryāvasānayor anivṛttir eva bhavati /
3.3.[28]	evañ cet pāṭhenaiva siddhatvāt trir ity anarthakam /
3.3.[29]	nānarthakaṃ triruktasyāsya subrahmaṇyāsaṃjñāyāṃ prasajato nivṛttyarthatvāt /
3.3.[30]	yadi triruktasyaiveyaṃ subrahmaṇyāsaṃjñā syād dve api niruktānirukte subrahmaṇye parācyau na syātām /
3.3.[31]	tatra te subrahmaṇyayā praṇavāntayā parācyā vācaṃ visṛjanta iti codanā nopapadyeta /
3.3.[32]	trir iti punar ucyamāne 'nabhyāsāyā eva saṃjñā sidhyati /
3.3.[33]	tatreyaṃ parācī bhavati /
3.3.[34]	aniruktety anvarthasaṃjñā /
3.3.[35]	na hy atra devatā nirucyate saṃjñānāñ ca prayojanaṃ saṃjñisaṃpratyayārtham /
3.3.[36]	tasmād aniruktāgrahaṇa iyaṃ pratyetavyā /
3.3.[37]	yatra subrahmaṇyāhvāyām adhvaryus saṃpreṣya śālāṃ prati nayati tatra saṃpraiṣānantaram eva subrahmaṇyāhvānam ārabheta /
3.3.[38]	asyān tu subrahmaṇyāyām evaṃ saṃpraiṣas subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvaya mā tu tvam āhvār yajamāna āhvāsyatīti /
3.3.[39]	tasmād yathāsaṃpraiṣaṃ yajamānāhvānād ūrdhvam atrāhvayet //
3.4.[1]	atha śakaṭaṃ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya śālāṃ prati nayanti /
3.4.[2]	atrāpi vakṣyati paryāvahanti rājavāhanam iti /
3.4.[3]	tatredam ucyate /
3.4.[4]	evam eva prācīn diśaṃ prati śakaṭe vartamāne subrahmaṇyām āhvayed iti /
3.4.[5]	nanu paryāvahanti rājavāhanam iti vidhāya paścād idaṃ vaktavyam /
3.4.[6]	satyam /
3.4.[7]	eṣa eva kramaḥ /
3.4.[8]	vyavahitatvāt tu subrahmaṇyāhvānam evam evety atideṣṭum aśakyaṃ syāt punarvacane ca granthagauravaṃ prasajatīti /
3.4.[9]	tat parihartum atraivedaṃ vidhitrayam upanyasyate //
3.4.[10]	evam eva dakṣiṇāṃ prati diśaṃ śakaṭe vartamāna āhvayati //
3.4.[11]	itthaṃ vyākhyāyamāne catasra imās subrahmaṇyā syus tathā ca saty atha yāṃ krīte rājani subrahmaṇyām iti bahuṣv ekavacanan nopapadyeta /
3.4.[12]	yat prāyaṇan tad udayanam asad iti cāyam arthavādaḥ prathamottame eva subrahmaṇye anirukte ity evamartham avalambya pravartamāno bahutve tāsān dussaṃpādārthas syāt /
3.4.[13]	tata idam anyathā vyākhyāyate //
3.5.[1]	āvarte śakaṭasya kriyamāṇe dakṣiṇam anaḍvāhan dviś śākhayā pāṇisthayā saṃspṛśati /
3.5.[2]	atha vā niṣṭhānto 'yam āvartaśabdaḥ /
3.5.[3]	tasmād āvarte śakaṭa iti vyākhyeyam /
3.5.[4]	nanv āvṛtta iti niṣṭhāyāṃ bhavitavyam /
3.5.[5]	satyam etat /
3.5.[6]	āvartaśabdo 'pi tu niṣṭhānta evāsaṃśayan dṛśyate /
3.5.[7]	yathā dakṣiṇata udakprāg āvarta iveti /
3.5.[8]	tatrāvaśyam ācāryaprāmāṇyān niṣṭhāntasyāvartaśabdasya sādhutvam anumanyāmahe /
3.5.[9]	tadvad atrāpi draṣṭavyam /
3.5.[10]	ktaś cāyam ādikarmaṇi /
3.5.[11]	tasmāt pravartamānādau śakaṭasyānaḍuho saṃsparśanam /
3.5.[12]	atha vāparaṃ vyākhyānam /
3.5.[13]	saṃsparśanapradeśo 'yaṃ kathyate /
3.5.[14]	yaḥ pṛṣṭhe romṇām āvartas tasminn anaḍvāhaṃ saṃspṛśati //
3.5.[15]	vāmam anaḍvāhaṃ sakṛt saṃspṛśati //
3.6.[1]	rājohyate 'neneti rājavāhanam idaṃ śakaṭam /
3.6.[2]	tad devayajanaṃ parītyāvahanti śālāṃ prati /
3.6.[3]	nanv idaṃ parakarma /
3.6.[4]	satyam etat /
3.6.[5]	uttaratrāpi bahūni parakarmāṇy evānukramyante /
3.6.[6]	ātithyayā caranti pravargyopasadbhyāñ carantīti /
3.6.[7]	tenāyam artho jñapyate /
3.6.[8]	anyo'nyasyāpi tantram ṛtvijo yathāśakti vijñāyaiva yājayeyur iti //
3.7.[1]	dvayor anaḍuhor vimuktayo rājānaṃ śālāṃ prapādayanti /
3.7.[2]	etāvantaṃ kālam anasy eva subrahmaṇyas tiṣṭhet /
3.7.[3]	tatra rājāhavanīyau subrahmaṇyena vyavetau /
3.7.[4]	tasmād vyavāyanivṛttyarthaṃ subrahmaṇyam agreṇa paryāvṛtya rājā prapādyaḥ /
3.7.[5]	yadi tu praveśakāla evāyam apareṇa śakaṭaṃ gatavān naivaṃ kartavyam //
3.8.[1]	śālāṃ prapanne rājani yathetam upanissṛpya yena pradeśena śakaṭam ārūḍhas tenaivāvaruhya śakaṭam uttareṇa pūrvayā dvārā śālāṃ prapadya śālāyā uttarasmin bhāge śākhām uparigūhaty anena mantreṇa //
3.9.[1]	atrāsmin subrahmaṇyāhvāne nimitta etad rājavāhanaṃ śakaṭam anaḍudbhyāṃ yuktaṃ yajamānas subrahmaṇyāya dadāti /
3.9.[2]	anasi vā yuktam anaḍuddvayam anoyuktaśabdenābhidhīyate /
3.9.[3]	tasmād anaḍvāhāv eva dadāti //
3.10.[1]	ātithyayā nāmeṣṭyāsmin kāle 'dhvaryavaś caranti vyāpriyante //
3.11.[1]	ātithyayā vyāpṛtya pravargyeṇopasadā ca vyāpriyante /
3.11.[2]	anukramaṇakrameṇaiva paurvāparyasiddher ātithyayā caritvety anarthakam /
3.11.[3]	nānarthakaṃ parapadārthānām iha dṛṣṭasya kramasyānityatvajñāpanārthatvāt /
3.11.[4]	tataś ca yāgnyādheye 'nvāhāryapacanādhānāt pūrvakālatoddharaṇasya parasya vāmadevyasyāsmākan dṛśyata iṣṭāsyā anityatā sidhyati /
3.11.[5]	evam audumbarīvyāpārasyāpi dhiṣṇyanivāpottarakālatā //
3.13.[1]	upasadi samāptāyām utkare tiṣṭhann etān niruktāṃ subrahmaṇyān trir āhvayati /
3.13.[2]	āhvātur avacane 'pi subrahmaṇyām iti samākhyayā subrahmaṇya āhvayati /
3.13.[3]	niruktety anvarthasaṃjñendrasya devatāyā nirvacanāt /
3.13.[4]	vyavahārābhāvān nirukteti saṃjñāvacanam anarthakam /
3.13.[5]	nānarthakaṃ sarvatra niruktāyās trirāhvānārthatvāt /
3.13.[6]	tataś ca yāsu subrahmaṇyāsu trir iti nocyata upavasathasutyākālāsu tāsām api trirāhvānaṃ siddham /
3.13.[7]	prāk pradhānotkarotpattes subrahmaṇyā kva tiṣṭhatāhvātavyā /
3.13.[8]	yo 'sti śālāyām utkaras tatra tiṣṭhatā //
3.16-19.[1]	evan trir āhūya subrahmaṇyāṃ yajamānam imān mantrān upāṃśu vācayati /
3.16-19.[2]	yajamānaṃ praty upāṃśutā codyate /
3.16-19.[3]	subrahmaṇyena tu yathā yajamānaś śṛṇoti tathā vaktavyam /
3.16-19.[4]	āhūya subrahmaṇyām iti padadvayam anarthakam /
3.16-19.[5]	nānarthakaṃ pitāputrīyāsv api prāpaṇārthatvāt /
3.16-19.[6]	evañ cen na pitāputrīyāsv eva tiṣṭhati /
3.16-19.[7]	aniruktāsv api subrahmaṇyāsv ayaṃ vidhiḥ prāpnoti /
3.16-19.[8]	na prāpnoti /
3.16-19.[9]	yadi hi tāsv apy aiṣiṣyatāniruktāyām evādau vyadhāsyata /
3.16-19.[10]	athaivam ucyeta /
3.16-19.[11]	aniruktādhikāre 'sya vidher akaraṇan niruktāyām aprāptibhayād iti siddho naḥ pakṣaḥ /
3.16-19.[12]	atrāpi niruktādhikārān nāniruktāsu prasajati //
3.20.[1]	aparāhṇa upasadi samāptāyām evam eva subrahmaṇyām āhvayati //
3.21.[1]	ete eva paurvāhṇikyāparāhṇikyāv upasadāv anv ā upavasathāt subrahmaṇyā vartate /
3.21.[2]	ayam āṅ kiṃ maryādāyām utābhividhau /
3.21.[3]	maryādāyām iti brūmaḥ /
3.21.[4]	uttarasmin hi vākye maryādāyām evāṅ grahītavyaḥ /
3.21.[5]	upavasatha iti śvassutyāvidheḥ prāg evopavasathāt sutyāvidhir upapadyate sarūpāṇāñ ca śabdānāṃ sati saṃbhave tulyārthataiva yuktopādātum /
3.21.[6]	tasmād atrāpy upavasathāt prāg ity eva varṇanīyam /
3.21.[7]	kaḥ punar upavasatho nāma /
3.21.[8]	ime brūmaḥ /
3.21.[9]	upavāsa upavasathas sa cātra samīpe vāsas sautyāt pūrvasminn ahani kartavyaḥ /
3.21.[10]	vakṣyate ca /
3.21.[11]	āgnīdhre patnīśālāyām iti saṃviśanti svaḥkarmaṇe 'napagā bhavantīti /
3.21.[12]	tam upavasathaṃ yaḥ karmakalāpo na vyabhicarati samāna evāhani kriyate gharmodvāsanādir agnipraṇayanādir vā sa ihopavasathaśabdena lakṣyate /
3.21.[13]	nanu mukhyāsaṃbhava eva lakṣaṇopādānaṃ yuktam /
3.21.[14]	satyam etat /
3.21.[15]	asaṃbhava eva tv iha mukhyasyopavasathaśabdasya grahaṇam /
3.21.[16]	katham iti ced upasadante kriyamāṇaṃ subrahmaṇyāhvānaṃ pravargyodvāsanādibahukarmavyavahitād rātrikālād upavasathāt prāg iti na yuktaṃ vaktum /
3.21.[17]	tasmād upavasathasannihitaḥ pravargyodvāsanādikarmakalāpo lakṣaṇayātropavasatha iti gṛhyate /
3.21.[18]	nanu yasminn ahany upavasathas tad ahar upavasathaśabdenābhidhīyata iti grahītavyam /
3.21.[19]	tathā ca pareṣān dṛśyate /
3.21.[20]	upavasathe prātar ubhe caraṇe saṃsthāpyeti /
3.21.[21]	naivaṃ yujyate /
3.21.[22]	uktaṃ hi pūrvaṃ maryādāyām ayam āṅ iti /
3.21.[23]	tatra sarvasminn ahany upavasathatvena gṛhyamāṇe tadahaḥkālayor upasador ante subrahmaṇyāhvānam avihitaṃ syāt tac ca neṣyate subrahmaṇya subrahmaṇyām āhvayeti saṃpraiṣasya tatrāpi vidyamānatvāt /
3.21.[24]	tasmād uktavad evopavasathasya grahaṇaṃ yuktam //
3.22.[1]	sutyām āgacchety ā upavasathād vadati /
3.22.[2]	subrahmaṇyāpāṭhād evāsyārthasya siddher idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
3.22.[3]	nānarthakaṃ ye subrahmaṇye upavasathīye 'hany upasadantabhāginyau tayoś śvaśśabdaprasaṅgasya nivṛttyarthatvāt /
3.22.[4]	kutaḥ punas tasya prasaṅgaḥ /
3.22.[5]	śvas sutyām ity upavasatha iti vacanāt /
3.22.[6]	nanūktaṃ pravargyodvāsanādikarmakalāpo 'tropavasatha iti /
3.22.[7]	satyam etat /
3.22.[8]	yadi tv etad vākyan na syād adhastanavākyāntarbhūtasyāṅo maryādāvacanataiva nāvadhāryeta /
3.22.[9]	abhividhāv apy āṅ gṛhyeta /
3.22.[10]	tatropavasathaśabdasyāharabhidhāne yo doṣa uktas sa na syāt /
3.22.[11]	ahni copavasathe sati tadahaḥkālāsu catasṛṣv api subrahmaṇyāsu śvassutyāvādaḥ prasajati sati tv asmin vākye nivartate //
3.23.[1]	upavasathe ye subrahmaṇye vidhāsyete vapānte parihṛtāsu vasatīvarīṣv iti tayoś śvas sutyām iti bravīti //
3.24.[1]	savas sutyādivasaḥ /
3.24.[2]	tasmin yā subrahmaṇyā vidhāsyata ājyagrahān gṛhṇatsv iti tasyām adya sutyām iti bravīti /
3.24.[3]	evaṃ vyākhyāyamāne punaruktatāprasaṅgaḥ /
3.24.[4]	tatrāpi hi vakṣyate subrahmaṇyām āhvayaty adya sutyām iti /
3.24.[5]	tasmād anyathā vyākhyāsyate /
3.24.[6]	upavasathakālayor eva subrahmaṇyayor ayaṃ vidhir upayujyate /
3.24.[7]	sutyādivasa evopavasathe kriyamāṇe śvas sutyām iti prakṛtitaḥ prasaktan nivartya sadyaskryādāv adya sutyām iti vidhir ayaṃ kriyate /
3.24.[8]	tasmāt sadyaskriyāṃ vapāntakālādyāsu tisṛṣv api subrahmaṇyāsv adya sutyām iti vacanaṃ siddham /
3.24.[9]	nanv arthād eva sadyaskriyāṃ śvaśśabdo nivartate /
3.24.[10]	kāman nivartatām /
3.24.[11]	adyaśabdas tv avihito na pravarteta /
3.24.[12]	atas tu vacanāt pravartate //
4.1.[1]	ity agnicayanam adhikriyate /
4.1.[2]	agniṃ yadi cinvīta yajamānas tatra pañca sāmāni suvarjyotiśśabdanidhanāny udgātā gāyet /
4.1.[3]	pañcānāṃ sāmnām anukramiṣyamānatvāt pañcety anarthakam /
4.1.[4]	nānarthakam anyāny api sāmāny agnicaye santi geyānīti jñāpanārthatvāt /
4.1.[5]	anyeṣv api vidyamāneṣu suvarjyotirnidhanānāṃ sāmnāṃ saṃkhyayā viśeṣaṇam upapadyate /
4.1.[6]	tāni cāgniparigāṇāni pareṣāṃ vihitāni /
4.1.[7]	tāni khalv agniparigāṇeṣv iti paryadhyāye 'smākam api dṛśyate /
4.1.[8]	yadi ... cinvīteti vacanād vaikalpiko 'gnicayaḥ //
4.2.[1]	puṣkaraparṇam adhvaryur upadadhāti /
4.2.[2]	tasminn upadhīyamāne satyam iti vyāhṛtisāma gāyet /
4.2.[3]	atrāvacane 'pi śiṣṭācārataḥ prāṅmukhatā grāhyā /
4.2.[4]	sthānāsane tu vikalpyete iva /
4.2.[5]	na vā vikalpaḥ /
4.2.[6]	tiṣṭhataivānādeśe gātavyam /
4.2.[7]	tad agnyādheye pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ /
4.2.[8]	tataś ca paścād agnes sthitenaitāni geyāni //
4.3.[1]	hiraṇmaye puruṣa upadhīyamāne puruṣa iti vyāhṛtisāma gāyet //
4.4.[1]	kaś cid upalaviśeṣa svayamātṛṇṇākhyaḥ /
4.4.[2]	tisra svayamātṛṇṇāḥ prathamatṛtīyottamāsu citiṣūpadhīyanta aparāś catasra uttamāyām eva /
4.4.[3]	tatra prathamāyāṃ svayamātṛṇṇāyāṃ bhūr iti sāma gāyet //
4.5.[1]	pūrvoktāsu tisṛṣv eva yā madhyamā tasyām idam ucyate /
4.5.[2]	netarābhis saha saptasu /
4.5.[3]	na hi tābhir āsāṃ sādharmyam //
4.7.[1]	sañcitaṃ pariniṣṭhitacayanam agniṃ sāmabhir vakṣyamāṇair upatiṣṭhate /
4.7.[2]	cayanād uparitaneṣu keṣu cit saṃskāreṣu kṛteṣūpastheyam /
4.7.[3]	tasmin hi kāle 'dhvaryavaś codayanti /
4.7.[4]	tadarthaṃ sañcitam ity uktan na citam iti //
4.8.[1]	yasya gāyatrasyodgītha ṛgakṣarasaṃsparśo nāsti tad aśarīram amṛtagāyatram /
4.8.[2]	gāyatraprakaraṇe hi śrūyate /
4.8.[3]	tasyāśarīreṇa sāmnā śarīrāṇy adhūnod iti /
4.8.[4]	yasya tv ṛgakṣareṣv eva gānan tac śarīravat /
4.8.[5]	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity āsv ṛkṣu yad gāyatraṃ śarīravat tenāgneś śira upatiṣṭhate /
4.8.[6]	atha vā yacchabdam anadhyāhṛtya vākyabhedaṃ kṛtvā vyākhyeyam /
4.8.[7]	tatra gāyatram ityantam ekaṃ vākyaṃ bhavati /
4.8.[8]	nanv asminn api pakṣe 'stīty adhyāhāryam eva /
4.8.[9]	naiṣa doṣaḥ pūrvasminn api pakṣe vidyamānatvāt //
4.8.[10]	agner dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣaṃ rathantareṇopatiṣṭhate //
4.8.[11]	prajāpatiśabdo hṛdayaśabdaś ca yasmin sāmni vidyete tat prajāpater hṛdayam //
4.8.[12]	bṛhadrathantaravāmadevyeṣu saṃśayaḥ /
4.8.[13]	kim atra tṛcasthāni tāni grāhyāṇy utaikarcasthānīti /
4.8.[14]	tatrāgnyādheyādau tṛcasthānām iṣṭe grahaṇe teṣāṃ yāni tṛcasthāni tṛceṣu tāni gāyed iti vacanād atra tadavacanād ekarcasthāny evātra grāhyāṇīti prāpte tṛcasthānām evātrāpi grahaṇaṃ yuktaṃ brūmaḥ /
4.8.[15]	kutaḥ /
4.8.[16]	āmnāyāt /
4.8.[17]	tṛcasthayor bṛhadrathantarayor ūharahasye samāmnāyo vidyate /
4.8.[18]	nanv agnyādheye tṛcasthānām eṣām upayogāt kṛtārthas samāmnāya syāt /
4.8.[19]	naivaṃ yuktam /
4.8.[20]	kramād ayam āmnāyo 'gnyartha eva /
4.8.[21]	śarīravato hi gāyatrasyānantare tṛcasthe bṛhadrathantare /
4.8.[22]	evam atrāmnāyata eva tṛcasthagrahaṇasiddhes tadartham akṛto yatnaḥ /
4.8.[23]	kṛtārthasya cātra samāmnāyasyāgnyādheyādāv aprayogaprasaṅge tatrāsthito yatnaḥ /
4.8.[24]	bṛhadrathantarayos tāvad evaṃ bhavatu /
4.8.[25]	kathaṃ vāmadevye /
4.8.[26]	tad api tṛcastham eva grāhyaṃ bṛhadrathantarasahacāritvāt /
4.8.[27]	yac cedaṃ śarīravad vāmadevyan tṛce samāmnāyate tasya sthānan na smaryate /
4.8.[28]	tatrāgnikrama eva sa na indrāyety asmāt saindhukṣitāt prāktanam idaṃ vāmadevyam anumātavyam /
4.8.[29]	atha vānārabhyādhītam idaṃ vāmadevyaṃ prakṛtipraveśārhatvāt /
4.8.[30]	prakṛtau jyotiṣṭome maitrāvaruṇapṛṣṭhatām āpitsamānaṃ prākaraṇikena vāmadevyena bādhitam anarthakaṃ sad ānarthakyāt tadaṅgeṣv iti nyāyāj jyotiṣṭomāṅgaṃ pravargyam agnicayanañ ca praviśati //
4.9.[1]	atrāsminn upasthāne kṛte śānto 'gnir bhavati /
4.9.[2]	ayam arthavādas sāmabhir upasthānasya stutyarthaḥ /
4.9.[3]	sarvatra cārthavādānāṃ sūtre vacanam arthavādajñāpanapūrve prayoge phalabhūyastvajñāpanārtham //
4.10.[1]	varo varaṇīyo 'bhilaṣaṇīyaḥ /
4.10.[2]	yad udgātābhilaṣati tad asmin karmaṇi dadāti yajamānaḥ /
4.10.[3]	atha vā gaur dātavyā varaḥ /
4.10.[4]	paratantre hi paribhāṣitaṃ gaur brāhmaṇasya vara iti //
5.1.[1]	udvāsya pravargyaṃ mahāvīram anantaram enaṃ prastotāram āmantrayante /
5.1.[2]	atra pravargyodvāsanārtham ādānam udvāsanam abhipreyate /
5.1.[3]	prasiddhe tu pravargyodvāsane gṛhyamāṇa udvāsyeti paurvakālikapratyayo nopapadyeta /
5.1.[4]	pūrvam eva hi prasiddhād udvāsanāt prastotāmantranīya udvāsane sāmagānārtham /
5.1.[5]	atha vā prasiddham evodvāsanam astu /
5.1.[6]	ekam etat padam udvāsyapravargyam iti /
5.1.[7]	udvāsyaḥ pravargyo 'nenety udvāsyapravargyaḥ prastotā /
5.1.[8]	chandogeṣu hi prastotaiva pravargyodvāsana upayujyate /
5.1.[9]	tasmād udgātrādyapekṣayā prastotodvāsyapravargyaḥ /
5.1.[10]	tam āmantrayante /
5.1.[11]	kiṃ punar aprakṛtasya prastotur enam ity abhidhātuṃ yujyate /
5.1.[12]	prakṛta eva prastotā pravargyopasados sāmagānāt /
5.1.[13]	kasmāt punar adhastanavākyāpekṣayā prakṛtasyodgātur evedam āmantraṇaṃ na gṛhyate /
5.1.[14]	nāmantritenātra prayojanam udgātrā /
5.1.[15]	na hy atrodgātṛkartṛkaṃ karma vakṣyate /
5.1.[16]	tasmāt prastotur eveyañ codanā /
5.1.[17]	ayañ cārthaḥ prastotur anvādeśena jñāpyate /
5.1.[18]	agniparigāṇāni prastotā gāyatīti //
5.2.[1]	sa prastotā yajñopavīty ācāntas tatraiva bhavati /
5.2.[2]	anapagaḥ karmadeśa eva syāt /
5.2.[3]	nāpagacched ity arthaḥ /
5.2.[4]	ācamanaprabhṛtivyavāyaparihārārtham etad uktaṃ sarvatrāpi paribhāṣārūpeṇa grāhyam /
5.2.[5]	tad uktaṃ kauṣītakinā /
5.2.[6]	ācamanaprabhṛti yenādhikaraṇena saṃyujyeta na tena vyāvarteta /
5.2.[7]	na ca vyaveyād iti //
5.3.[1]	taṃ yadādhvaryuḥ prastotas sāma gāyeti saṃpreṣyati sa tadā hiṃkṛtyāgniṃ hotāram manye dāsvantam ity asyām ṛci gītānām eteṣāṃ sāmnām uttamaṃ sāma trir gāyati /
5.3.[2]	na cātraiva trir gāyati /
5.3.[3]	pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhita iti vidhāsyamānatvāt sakṛd evāsmin kāle gāyati /
5.3.[4]	yadi cātraiva trir gīyeta pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhita iti ca vidher dvir uttaratrāpi tadā pañcakṛtvo 'pi gānaṃ saṃpadyeta /
5.3.[5]	tatra trayo vā iti vakṣyamāṇā trirgānasya stutir nopapadyeta /
5.3.[6]	tasmād uttaragānadvayāpekṣayā trir ity ucyate /
5.3.[7]	evañ cet trir ity anarthakaṃ vacanam /
5.3.[8]	nānarthakaṃ yadi kaiś cid adhvaryubhis triḥ pratiṣṭhāpan na hriyeta tatrādāv eva trir gātavyam ity etadarthatvāt /
5.3.[9]	atra hiṃkāratritvayor ubhayor api sāmaguṇayor mithassaṃbandhābhāvāt sakṛd eva hiṃkartavyam //
5.3.[10]	ṛcaḥ pāde padaśabdo 'tra vijñeyaḥ /
5.3.[11]	yo 'tra sāmni stobhas taṃ pratipādaṃ brūyāt /
5.3.[12]	purastāc ca padānāṃ brūyāt tathā prathame dṛṣṭatvāt /
5.3.[13]	caturthī ceyan tādarthye stobhasya padaguṇatvajñāpanārthā //
5.4.[1]	sarva ṛtvigyajamānās saha patnyāsya sāmnas trir nidhanam upayanti /
5.4.[2]	asya nidhanopāyanasya pravargyodvāsanāṅgatvāt sarvādīnāñ ca śabdānām adhikṛtāpekṣatvād ye pravargyasaṃbaddhās tair idan nidhanam upetavyan nānyair udgātrādibhir api /
5.4.[3]	tathā ca tāṇḍinān nidhanopāyavidhau /
5.4.[4]	ye gharma upayuktā syur iti /
5.4.[5]	bahvṛcānāñ ca gharmasaṃbandhāddhotur eva nidhanopāyanañ codyate na praśāstrādīnām /
5.4.[6]	evaṃ hi kauṣītakinoktam /
5.4.[7]	tatra prastotā sāma gāyati /
5.4.[8]	tatra hotur nidhanopāya iti /
5.4.[9]	tasmād brahmāgnīdhrāv adhvaryupratiprasthātārau hotā prastotā yajamānaś ca saha patnyā pravargyodvāsane nidhanam upeyuḥ /
5.4.[10]	saptānān tv iyañ codanā na prastotuḥ sāmagānacodanayaiva siddhatvāt //
5.8.[1]	ayaṃ vākyaśeṣo 'rthavādas sa ca sarveṣāṃ vihitasya nidhanopāyasya stutyarthaḥ /
5.8.[2]	tasyaivam artho yojyaḥ /
5.8.[3]	devān khalv etasmin pravargyodvāsanakāle rakṣāṃsy āśrayanti sma /
5.8.[4]	sa deveṣv antarbhūto rakṣohā nāmāgnir etat sāmāpaśyat /
5.8.[5]	tena sāmnā devā rakṣāṃsy apāghnata /
5.8.[6]	tasmād yat sarve nidhanam upayanti rakṣasām evāpahananārthaṃ tad bhavatīti //
5.9.[1]	āhavanīyottaravedyor madhyatas triḥ pratiṣṭhāpaṃ pravargyaṃ haranti //
5.12.[1]	pūrvoktaṃ sāma pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhite gāyati /
5.12.[2]	evan trir gātavyam iti /
5.12.[3]	trayo hīme lokāḥ /
5.12.[4]	tasmād eṣāṃ lokānāṃ vidharaṇāya trir gāyati //
5.13.[1]	sāma gāyatas sthānam idaṃ vidhīyate /
5.13.[2]	apareṇa pravargyam asminn udvāsanāṅgabhūte sāmagāne prastotā tiṣṭhati //
5.13.[3]	pravargyam adhvaryavo yuñjanti /
5.13.[4]	tathā te vadanti /
5.13.[5]	prastotāpy uttaraṃ saṃpraiṣam ākāṅkṣamāṇas tatraiva tiṣṭhati /
5.13.[6]	ke cid etad vākyadvayam ekavākyatayā vyācakṣate /
5.13.[7]	tiṣṭhatīti śatus saptamī /
5.13.[8]	apareṇa pravargyam asmin prastotari tiṣṭhati pravargyaṃ yuñjantīti /
5.13.[9]	asmin vyākhyāne sāma gāyataḥ prastotus sthānaviśeṣo na jñāyeta //
5.14.[1]	dvau pariṣekau tatra vidyete /
5.14.[2]	yasmin kāle dvitīyam apaḥ pariṣiñcaty athainam evaṃ saṃpreṣyati /
5.14.[3]	yugapad eva ke cid sāmadvayāya saṃpreṣyanti /
5.14.[4]	prastotar vārṣāharaṃ sāma gāyeṣṭāhotrīyañ ceti /
5.14.[5]	nanu pariṣiñcaty āpa ity na yujyate /
5.14.[6]	satyam etat /
5.14.[7]	ācāryaprāmāṇyāt tu lakṣaṇam atrānumātavyam /
5.14.[8]	ā apa iti vā vyākhyeyam /
5.14.[9]	āṅ punaḥ kimarthaḥ /
5.14.[10]	īṣadartho vākyālaṃkārārtho vā //
5.16.[1]	anyasya deśasyāvihitasyāprasaṅgād atraiva tiṣṭhann ity anarthakam /
5.16.[2]	nānarthakam īṣad api vārṣāharasthānān na calitavyam ity etadarthatvāt /
5.16.[3]	visṛjyāpi hi vārṣāharasthānan tad agreṇa jaghanena vā kiñ cid apasṛtya pravargyam apareṇaiva sthātuṃ śakyam /
5.16.[4]	tad atraiva tiṣṭhann iti vacanān nivartate //
5.17.[1]	iṣṭāhotrīyasya nidhanaṃ pravargyasaṃbaddhās sarve saha patnyopayanti /
5.17.[2]	nanu tasyety api vacane sannidher iṣṭāhotrīyasyeti vijñātuṃ śakyam /
5.17.[3]	satyam etat /
5.17.[4]	tadādayas tu śabdāḥ kadā cid asannihitam api śabdato vadantīti jñāpanārtham iṣṭāhotrīyagrahaṇam /
5.17.[5]	tena prayojanam taṃ yadi brūyur viśvarūpā gāyetyādau sannihitasya subrahmaṇyāder agrahaṇam //
5.17.[6]	yān prati pūrvayos sāmnor atra nidhanopāyaś coditas te vārṣāharasya nidhanan nopayanti /
5.17.[7]	prastotur anya ity arthaḥ /
5.17.[8]	kutas teṣām atra prāptiḥ /
5.17.[9]	na lakṣyate prāptiḥ /
5.17.[10]	pratiṣedhakaraṇasāmarthyāt tu manyāmahe /
5.17.[11]	vārṣāharasya nidhanopāyaḥ kasyāñ cic chrutau sarveṣāṃ vihita iti /
5.17.[12]	evañ ced ayam ācāryasya śrutiviruddhaḥ pratiṣedho doṣaḥ /
5.17.[13]	pratiṣedhakam api vacanan dṛṣṭam ity adoṣaḥ /
5.17.[14]	vacanadvayam idam aśrutam akalpayitvā prastotur eva vārṣāharaṃ gāyato nidhanamātraṃ pratiṣidhyata iti grahaṇe 'tyantaṃ ghaṭata iti /
5.17.[15]	evaṃ hi gṛhyamāṇe vārṣāharasya nidhanamātran na brūyād iti śrutiparikalpanam asty eva /
5.17.[16]	kin tu-upayantīti bahuvacanāntam anuvartamānaṃ vinā prastotur grahaṇenaikavacanāntatvena vipariṇamitum aśakyaṃ bhavet /
5.17.[17]	sāmnaś ca nidhanād ṛte gānaṃ kva cid apy adṛṣṭaṃ parigṛhyeta /
5.17.[18]	asmiṃś ca vākye sāmarthyāvagatasya prastotur anuvartayituṃ śakyatvād uttarasmin vākye prastotur grahaṇam ayuktaṃ syāt /
5.17.[19]	uttaravākyārtham api prastotur grahaṇam abhaviṣyad yady atraivākariṣyata /
5.17.[20]	na caivaṃ kṛtam /
5.17.[21]	tasmād ayaṃ pakṣo bahudoṣatvān nāśriyate /
5.17.[22]	kalpyavacanadvaye 'pi pūrva eva pakṣaś śreyān /
5.17.[23]	sarvatra kalpasūtrakārāṇāṃ vacanam asatyāṃ pratyakṣaśrutau śrutivacanānumānenaiva prāmāṇyaṃ labhate /
5.17.[24]	tasmāc chrutivacanaparikalpanam adoṣaḥ /
5.17.[25]	atha vāsya vārṣāharasya tulyasthānasyeṣṭāhotrīyeṇa sarvair upetavyanidhanenāprasaktanidhanopāyapratiṣedhād ayam artho jñāpyate /
5.17.[26]	sthānasāmānyād anyadharmo 'pi kva cid grāhya iti /
5.17.[27]	kim etasya jñāpane prayojanam /
5.17.[28]	santi pravargyaparigāṇāni teṣāñ ca brahmajajñānīyādibhis tulyasthānīyatāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
5.17.[29]	atas tāny api sakṛd evodaṅmukhenaiva ca satā gātavyānīti /
5.17.[30]	atha vaikasaṃpraiṣāṇān tulyadharmataiṣāñ jñāpyate /
5.17.[31]	tenāpy ukto 'rthas sidhyati /
5.17.[32]	nanu brahmajajñānīyādyartha evāsau saṃpraiṣaḥ /
5.17.[33]	kuta idaṃ labhyate /
5.17.[34]	yadi pravargye parigāṇāni gīyeran tatra viśeṣāgrahaṇād ubhayārtha eva saṃpraiṣas saṃpadyate //
5.18.[1]	athāsmin karmaṇi samāpta etad vāsaḥ prastotādatte yena patnī cchāditā bhavati //
5.19.[1]	śālāṃ pratyāvrajan śyaitaṃ gāyet /
5.19.[2]	trir ity atra nānuvartate /
5.19.[3]	atas sakṛd eva śyaitaṃ gāyet //
6.4.[1]	pravargyodvāsanād ūrdhvam agniṃ praṇīya sadohavirdhānavyāpāraṃ pariniṣṭhāpya dhiṣṇyān nivapanti /
6.4.[2]	tatra yadā dhiṣṇyān adhvaryavo nivapanti tadanantaram udgātāntareṇa cātvālotkarau prapadyājyasthālīṃ sasruvām ādāyāgnīdhrañ ca sadaś cottareṇa parivrajyāparayā dvārā sadaḥ prapadya sadasas sthūṇām audumbarīm ārabhamāṇam adhvaryum anvārabhate 'nena mantreṇa //
6.6.[1]	athainām anena mantreṇocchrayaty utthāpayati //
6.8.[1]	pūrvam evādhvaryusaṃpreṣiteṇodgātraudumbaryavaṭaṃ khānitaṃ bhavati /
6.8.[2]	tasminn enām anena mantreṇa minoti /
6.8.[3]	yathodañcaṃ vaṃśan dhārayet tathaināṃ saṃpādayati //
6.10.[1]	athainām ājyasthālyā sruvenopahatenājyenāgrād upakramyā mūlād avicchindann eva dhārām anena mantreṇābhijuhoti //
6.12.[1]	athainān triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ pāṃsunā paryūhaty anena mantreṇa /
6.12.[2]	sakṛd eva mantravacanam evaṃvidhāsu codanāsu /
6.12.[3]	tatra nyāyaṃ madhuprāśanādhikāra eva prasaṅgenāvādiṣma /
6.12.[4]	samastam avaṭaṃ pūrayati //
6.14.[1]	athainān dīkṣitasya daṇḍena ṣaḍbhir ebhir mantrair dṛṃhati /
6.14.[2]	abhitaṣ ṣaṭ dṛṃhaty abhito 'vahanti /
6.14.[3]	na caikamantratvam eṣām abhipretavyam anyo'nyānākāṅkṣatvād ākhyātābhyāsāc ca /
6.14.[4]	tasmāt pratimantram atra dṛṃhaṇam āvarteta /
6.14.[5]	avadac ca kauṣītakiḥ mantrapṛthaktvāt karmapṛthaktvam iti //
6.15.[1]	athainām ūrdhvāgrais tṛṇais sarvato veṣṭayati /
6.15.[2]	yathā ca tāni nāpabhraṃśeran tathā rajjvā badhnāti //
6.16.[1]	athainām uparidaśena vāsasā paridadhāti samastāṃ veṣṭayati /
6.16.[2]	asyā anagnabhāvāya //
6.18.[1]	athaināṃ hastābhyām anena mantreṇa paryārabhate //
6.19.[1]	evam evānenaiva mantreṇa stotre stotra upakramyamāṇa audumbarīṃ parigṛhṇāti /
6.19.[2]	kiṃ bahiṣpavamāne 'pi /
6.19.[3]	neti brūmaḥ /
6.19.[4]	na hi tasyaudumbaryā saṃbandhaḥ /
6.19.[5]	ato 'syāṃ kṛtas saṃskāro bahiṣpavamānasya nopakaroti /
6.19.[6]	nanu vihitatvād audumbarīparigrahaḥ kriyamāṇo bahiṣpavamānasyāpy upakarotīti mantavyam /
6.19.[7]	naivaṃ yuktam /
6.19.[8]	ittham idam avagamyatām /
6.19.[9]	ekacodanāprāpitam aṅgaṃ bahūnām apy upakurvad ekadhaivopakarotīti /
6.19.[10]	ataś ca yeṣāṃ stotrāṇām aikarūpyeṇopakarotīty anena janayituṃ śakyan teṣām evaitad aṅgaṃ vidhīyata iti mantavyam /
6.19.[11]	tasmān nāyaṃ vidhir bahiṣpavamānam upasarpati /
6.19.[12]	yatra tu bahiṣpavamānaṃ sadasi gīyate 'hargaṇeṣu tatra saṃbandhād bahiṣpavamāne 'pi parigrāhyaivaudumbarī //
7.1.[1]	agniñ ca somañ ca praṇīyāgnīṣomadevatākaṃ paśum ālabhante 'dhvaryavaḥ /
7.1.[2]	vakṣyamāṇasya vidher viṣayapradarśanārtham idam uktam //
7.2.[1]	tasmin paśau vapāyā ante vapāhome kṛta utkare tiṣṭhan subrahmaṇyaḥ pitāputrīyākhyāṃ subrahmaṇyām āhvayati /
7.2.[2]	pitāputrīyām iti saṃjñākaraṇaṃ saṃvyavahārābhāvād anarthakam /
7.2.[3]	nānarthakam uttaratra subrahmaṇyāgrahaṇe pitāputrīyāyās saṃpratyayārthatvāt /
7.2.[4]	ayam abhiprāyaḥ /
7.2.[5]	atra subrahmaṇyāṃ pitāputrīyām iti sāmānādhikaraṇyoktes sārthavatvād yottaratra subrahmaṇyāgrahaṇe pitāputrīyā grāhyeti /
7.2.[6]	atha vā pitāputrīyām iti pṛthag evedaṃ paribhāṣāvākyam /
7.2.[7]	tatra pūrvasmād vākyāt subrahmaṇyām āhvayatīty anuvartate /
7.2.[8]	ayam arthaḥ /
7.2.[9]	subrahmaṇyām āhvayatīty ukte pitāputrīyāṃ vidyād iti /
7.2.[10]	tata idaṃ sidhyati /
7.2.[11]	dve apy uttare subrahmaṇye pitāputrīye iti /
7.2.[12]	avadac ca baudhāyanaḥ pitāputrīyām adhikṛtyāgnīṣomīyasya hutāyāṃ vapāyām /
7.2.[13]	parihṛtāsu vasatīvarīṣu dvitīyā /
7.2.[14]	prātaranuvāke tṛtīyeti //
7.4.[1]	kā sā pitāputrīyā subrahmaṇyety ākāṅkṣāyām ayam asyām upadeśo lakṣaṇataḥ kriyate /
7.4.[2]	kauśikabrāhmaṇa kauśikabruvāṇety ā atas subrahmaṇyāvayavam uktvāsminn avasare vakṣyamāṇāni nāmāny āvapati /
7.4.[3]	āta ity anarthakam /
7.4.[4]	nānarthakaṃ pitāputrīyeti viśeṣanāmadheyadarśanād anyeyam ihāmnātamātraiva subrahmaṇyeti kṛtvā kauśikabrāhmaṇety evāsyā upakramasya prasajato nivṛttyarthatvāt /
7.4.[5]	kauśikabruvāṇety anenaivopalakṣaṇe sidhyaty ubhayasya vacanañ śrutyanukaraṇārtham /
7.4.[6]	śrutāv api hi dvayor anayor uttarasyaiva satyāṃ vivakṣāyāṃ pūrvam apy upādīyate /
7.4.[7]	atha ha vā eke kauśikabrāhmaṇa gautamabruvāṇety āhvayanti-iti tasmāt kauśikabrāhmaṇa kauśikabruvāṇety evāhvayed iti ca //
7.5.[1]	asāv ity asya sthāne yajamānasya nāma prathamayā nirdiśed amuṣyeti ṣaṣṭhyā pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahānām /
7.5.[2]	evañ catuṣpuruṣañ caturaḥ puruṣān nāmnā nirdiśet /
7.5.[3]	tac ca sukhāvagamāya kathyate /
7.5.[4]	devadatto yajate yajñadattasya putro yajate viṣṇumitrasya pautro yajate haradattasya naptā yajata iti /
7.5.[5]	yac ca nāmāthāto nāmakarmety adhikṛtya vihitaṃ tad evātra nirdeṣṭavyam /
7.5.[6]	tad eva hi vyavahārārtham /
7.5.[7]	pāṭhasiddheś catuṣpuruṣam ity anarthakam /
7.5.[8]	nānarthakañ catuṣpuruṣam avaśyan nirdiśed ity evaṃ yojyamāne vakṣyamāṇānāṃ putrādīnāṃ kva cid anirdeśajñāpanārthatvāt /
7.5.[9]	tasmād evaṃ grāhyam /
7.5.[10]	jīvatām evātra putrādīnān nirdeśaḥ /
7.5.[11]	mṛtānām api tu pitrādīnām iti /
7.5.[12]	nanu yajamānasyāpi mṛtasya sattre nirdeśaḥ prasajati /
7.5.[13]	na prasajati /
7.5.[14]	na hi mṛto yajate /
7.5.[15]	mṛtā api tu pitrādibhāvena nirdiśyanta eva /
7.5.[16]	nanu putrādibhir api mṛtair asty eva loke nirdeśaḥ /
7.5.[17]	satyam etat /
7.5.[18]	prasaktam eva lokato mṛtair api putrādibhir nirdeśam ayaṃ yatno nivartayati //
7.6.[1]	yajata ity anuvartate /
7.6.[2]	agniśarmaṇaḥ pitā yajate nārāyaṇaśarmaṇaḥ pitā yajata iti putrāṇāñ janmakrameṇa nāmāni gṛhṇāti /
7.6.[3]	amuṣya pitety etāvataiva putrāṇām iti vijñātuṃ śakyatvāt tathā ca pūrvasmin vākye yajata ity evāvagatatvād yajamānasyeti ca putrapautranaptṛgrahaṇe 'vagatatvāt pituḥ pitāmahasya prapitāmahasyeti cāprayuktatvāt putrāṇām ity anarthakam /
7.6.[4]	nānarthakam akṛtanāmakān api putrān nirdiśed iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
7.6.[5]	katham eṣān nirdeśaḥ /
7.6.[6]	asti jātamātrasyaiva devakṛtan nāma yan nakṣatranāmeti kathyate /
7.6.[7]	tenātra nirdeśaś śātabhiṣajasya proṣṭhapādasyeti /
7.6.[8]	pūrvavayasāṃ pūrvagrahaṇasya lokata eva siddhatvād yathājātam ity anarthakam /
7.6.[9]	nānarthakaṃ vittaṃ bandhur vayaḥ karma vidyā bhavati pañcamī /
7.6.[10]	etāni mānyasthānāni garīyo yad yad uttaram //
7.6.[11]	iti smṛtivacanānurodhena vidyāvṛtādhikānām avaravayasāṃ pūrvanirdeśasya prasajato nivṛttyarthatvāt //
7.7.[1]	strīṇām api nāmāny eke nirdiśanti /
7.7.[2]	eka iti vacanaṃ vikalpārtham /
7.7.[3]	ata strīṇān nāmāni gṛhṇīta vā na vā /
7.7.[4]	kiṃ punar etad duhitṛviṣayam evāho svid anyaviṣayam api /
7.7.[5]	anyaviṣayam apīti brūmaḥ /
7.7.[6]	yadi hi duhitṛviṣayam evābhaviṣyad duhitṛrṇām ity evāvakṣyata na strīṇām iti /
7.7.[7]	tatraivaṃ yojyam /
7.7.[8]	putraḥ pautro naptā pitety anukrānte viṣayacatuṣṭaye mātuḥ pitāmahyāḥ prapitāmahyā duhituś ca nāmāny amuṣyā iti nirdiśed iti /
7.7.[9]	nanu patnyā apy asau yajata iti nirdeśo yajamānavat prāpnoti /
7.7.[10]	na prāpnoti /
7.7.[11]	yajatiśabdaṃ hi patnīviṣayan na kva cid upalabhāmahe /
7.7.[12]	patnīyajamānāviti ca dṛśyate prayogo na yajamānāv iti /
7.7.[13]	yady api yajamāneti patnī kva cid upalakṣyate tathāpi nātra patnīnirdeśaḥ prāpnoti /
7.7.[14]	evam adhvaryuṇā yajamāno 'vabodhyate /
7.7.[15]	nāma grāhan te pitṛbhiḥ pitāmahaiḥ prapitāmahaiḥ putraiḥ pautrais subrahmaṇyas subrahmaṇyām āhvayatv iti /
7.7.[16]	patnyā api cen nāmagrahaṇam abhipraiṣyata nāma grāhaṃ yuvayor ity avakṣyata /
7.7.[17]	yatas tu nāma grāhan ta ity uktan tasmān na patnyā nirdeśaḥ /
7.7.[18]	atha vā strīṇām api nāmabhir eke yajamānaṃ viśeṣayantīti vyākhyeyam /
7.7.[19]	tataś ca patnyām aprasaṅgaḥ //
7.8.[1]	janiṣyamāṇānām ity etad vākyaṃ sarvasmān nāmanirdeśād uttamam āha /
7.8.[2]	uttamagrahaṇam anarthakam /
7.8.[3]	nānarthakaṃ pautranaptṛnirdeśajñāpanārthatvāt /
7.8.[4]	kasmāt punaḥ pautranaptṛnirdeśa spaṣṭan nābhihitaḥ /
7.8.[5]	niyogataḥ pautrotpatteḥ prāk somena yaṣṭavyam iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
7.8.[6]	na ca purastāj jātaiḥ pautranaptṛbhir anupalakṣitasya paścāj janiṣyamāṇair yuktam upalakṣaṇam /
7.8.[7]	tasmād amuṣya pitāmaho yajate 'muṣya prapitāmaho yajata iti pautranaptṛṛn nirdiśya paścāj janiṣyamāṇānām iti vākyaṃ prakṣetavyam /
7.8.[8]	nanv ādyantapadānuṣaṅgeṇa vākyatrayam etat kalpayitavyam /
7.8.[9]	naivam /
7.8.[10]	ekavākyatayāpy abhipretārthāvagamāt /
7.8.[11]	yady ayam ekavākyatayā naiṣiṣyatāsau yajata ityādivaj janiṣyamāṇānāṃ pitā yajata ity evaṃ bhedenaivāvakṣyata /
7.8.[12]	yatas tv evan noktan tasmād yathāmnātam eva vaktavyam //
7.9.[1]	śeṣam avaśiṣṭaṃ subrahmaṇyāvayavaṃ yathāmnātam āha /
7.9.[2]	kiṃ śvaśśabdasyāyaṃ pratiṣedho yathāmnātam iti /
7.9.[3]	naivañ śvas sutyām ity upavasatha iti vākyasyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt /
7.9.[4]	evañ ced yathāmnātam ity anarthakam /
7.9.[5]	nānarthakam asau yajata ityāder janiṣyamāṇavākyāntasya yathāmnātavacananivāraṇārthatvāt /
7.9.[6]	tasmād imāni vākyāny aikasvaryeṇāpy āmnātāni lākṣaṇikenaiva svareṇa vaktavyāni /
7.9.[7]	svaralakṣaṇañ cātra vyākaraṇato grāhyam /
7.9.[8]	nanv ayatnasiddham etat /
7.9.[9]	lākṣaṇikas svaro grāhya iti /
7.9.[10]	satyam etat /
7.9.[11]	sarvasyā api subrahmaṇyāyā vyākaraṇata eva svaras sidhyati /
7.9.[12]	evaṃ siddhe sati yat pūrvasyāṃ subrahmaṇyāyāṃ lākṣaṇikam eva svaram ācāryaḥ pāṭhena pradarśayati taj jñāpayati /
7.9.[13]	aikasvaryapaṭhiteṣu lakṣaṇato na svaraḥ pravartata iti /
7.9.[14]	tataś ca sarveṣv ṛgyajurnigadeṣu yas svaro 'smākam āmnāye dṛśyate sa eva prayoge 'pi gṛhyate /
7.9.[15]	tasmād eṣān nāmavākyānāṃ vyākaraṇoktam api svaram uktajñāpanānurodhārtham anupāditsitam ato yatnād upādadmahe /
7.9.[16]	atha vā pūrveṇa vidhānenāsya saṃbandhaḥ /
7.9.[17]	janiṣyamāṇānām ity etan nigadaṃ yathāmnātam āheti /
7.9.[18]	tataś ca vākyatrayan na kalpyam ity uktaṃ bhavati /
7.9.[19]	tataś ca śeṣam iti vākyam /
7.9.[20]	śeṣam āheti //
7.10.[1]	asmin karmaṇi nimitta ṛṣabhaṃ yajamānas subrahmaṇyāya dadāti /
7.10.[2]	adhikārād evāsya vidheḥ pitāputrīyāsaṃbandhasiddher atrety anarthakam /
7.10.[3]	nānarthakam asyām eva pitāputrīyāyām ṛṣabhadānaṃ nottarayor ity etadarthatvāt /
7.10.[4]	uttare api hi pitāputrīye ity avādiṣma /
7.10.[5]	tatra nāmadheyena dharmaprāptir iti prasaktam ṛṣabhadānam ato yatnān nivartate //
7.12.[1]	etām upavasathīyāṃ rātriṃ kaś cana puruṣas sado na prapadyeta na praviśet /
7.12.[2]	ko hetur iti ced ṛksāme atra mithunībhavata ity asminn arthe brāhmaṇam asti /
7.12.[3]	ṛksāme adhikṛtya śrūyate tābhyāṃ sado mithunāya paryaśrayan /
7.12.[4]	tasmād upavasathīyāṃ rātriṃ sadasi na śayīta /
7.12.[5]	atra hy etāv ṛksāme upavasathīyāṃ rātriṃ sadasi saṃbhavata iti /
7.12.[6]	atha vā naitāṃ rātrim ityādi mithunībhavata ityantaṃ śākhāntarīyam idaṃ vākyaṃ brāhmaṇam iti pradarśyate //
7.13.[1]	parihṛtāsu vasatīvarīṣv adhvaryusaṃpreṣitas subrahmaṇyaś śvassutyāpravacanīn nāma subrahmaṇyām āhūya svayam udgātrādayaś cāgnīdhre patnīśālāyāñ ca saṃviśanti /
7.13.[2]	atrotkare tiṣṭhann ity avacane 'pi sthānāntarasyāvijñānād utkaram āsthāya subrahmaṇyām āhvayatīti śrutivacanasya [ca] śākaṭīvarjasubrahmaṇyāviṣayatvād utkara eva tiṣṭhann āhvayati /
7.13.[3]	atrotkarasyācodanayā jñāpyate deśāvacane svajātīyadeśagrahaṇam iti /
7.13.[4]	tena saṃsavaviśvarūpāṇām api paścād akṣam evopaviśya gānaṃ sidhyati //
7.14.[1]	śvaḥ kartavyaṃ karma śvaḥkarma /
7.14.[2]	śvaḥkarmārtham anapagā bhavanti /
7.14.[3]	āgnīdhrapatnīśālāsaṃveśanavidhānād eva yajñadeśād ṛtvigyajamānānām anapagamanasya siddhatvād idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
7.14.[4]	nānarthakaṃ sarvapuruṣārthatvāt /
7.14.[5]	tasmāt subrahmaṇyāhvānakāle ye yajñadeśāntarvartinaḥ puruṣās te śvaḥkarmaṇy aparisamāpte nāpagaccheyuḥ /
7.14.[6]	yajñam evekṣamāṇā āsīran //
8.1.[1]	śvaḥkarmaṇa iti pūrvam uktatvāt tasya karmaṇaḥ kāla āgata enam arthatas tasya karmaṇaḥ kartāram āmantrayante /
8.1.[2]	evañ cet kartṛṛṇāṃ bahutvād enān iti vaktavyam /
8.1.[3]	na vaktavyam ekavacanaprayoge 'py āmantryamāṇān puruṣān praty āmantraṇasya guṇabhūtatvāt /
8.1.[4]	pratipradhānaṃ guṇabheda iti nyāyena sarveṣāñ cāmantraṇaṃ sidhyati /
8.1.[5]	yadi caikasyaiva gṛhyeta viśeṣo nāvagamyeta /
8.1.[6]	na cātra samākhyayā śakyam udgātur evāmantraṇaṃ vaktum /
8.1.[7]	kartṛviṣayā hi samākhyā /
8.1.[8]	āmantraṇañ ca prati karmabhūtāḥ puruṣāḥ /
8.1.[9]	atas sarveṣām udgātrādīnāṃ karmakaraṇārtham idam āmantraṇañ codyate //
8.3.[1]	sa āmantritaḥ kartā yajñopavīty ācamya cātvālañ cotkarañ cāntareṇānena yajuṣā mahāvediṃ prapadyate /
8.3.[2]	yeṣām antarvedi prayojanan teṣām evaitad vidhānam /
8.3.[3]	atas subrahmaṇyo bahirvedy evāsīta /
8.3.[4]	udgeṣmeti mantraliṅgasyānavak.lptiprasaṅgān nānena yajuṣā brahmayajamānau prapadyeyātām //
8.4.[1]	prapadyante 'neneti prapadanam /
8.4.[2]	yad antareṇa cātvālotkarāv uktaṃ vartma tad atidiśyate /
8.4.[3]	etad eva sarvatra mahāvedyāṃ prapadanaṃ praveśanavartma bhavati //
8.4.[4]	udyanty anenety udayanam /
8.4.[5]	uktam eva vartma nirdiśyate /
8.4.[6]	etad eva sarvatra mahāvedyā udayanan niṣkramaṇavartma bhavati /
8.4.[7]	dvayam idaṃ paribhāṣāvākyam /
8.4.[8]	ata snānabhojanādyartham api mahāveder niṣkrāmatāṃ punaś ca tāṃ prapadyamānānām idam eva vartma syāt //
8.4.[9]	santy ājyagrahā nāma grahāḥ /
8.4.[10]	tān adhvaryuṣu gṛhṇatsu subrahmaṇya utkare tiṣṭhann adya sutyām iti nirdiśan subrahmaṇyām āhvayati //
8.5.[1]	prakṛtasya subrahmaṇyasya gānānupapatter atrodgātā nirdiśyate /
8.5.[2]	tam udgātāraṃ viśvarūpā gāyeti yadi brūyur adhvaryava akarmaṇa etat trayodaśaṃ stotraṃ virājaṃ lobhayatīti pratibrūyāt /
8.5.[3]	prativacanasyāyam arthaḥ /
8.5.[4]	akāryam etat trayodaśaṃ stotram /
8.5.[5]	virājaṃ lobhayatīti vināśayatīti hetunā /
8.5.[6]	viśvarūpāgāne virājo lobhanan doṣaḥ kīrtyate /
8.5.[7]	agniṣṭomasya hi prākṛtasya navatiśataṃ stotriyās saṃpadyante /
8.5.[8]	tā navadaśa virājo daśākṣarā virāḍ iti darśanāt /
8.5.[9]	asti ca vacanaṃ virāṭsampadaiva yajñena yajeteti /
8.5.[10]	yadi cāsmin kāle viśvarūpāgānaṃ kriyeta vasatīvarībhir graheṇa prātaranuvākena śastreṇa trayodaśam ivedaṃ stotraṃ bhavet /
8.5.[11]	uktaṃ hi baudhāyanena vāsatīvaraṃ graham adhikṛtya viśvarūpā u hāsya stotrabhaktir bhavati prātaranuvāka u śastrabhaktir iti /
8.5.[12]	yad asmābhir asmin kāle viśvarūpāgānam akurvadbhis stotrabhāvo 'sya parihriyate vasatīvarīgrahaṇaprātaranuvākāntarvartitā hi viśvarūpāṇāṃ stotratve kāraṇam tasmād itthaṃ pratyākhyāya paścād eva viśvarūpāgānaṃ kariṣyate //
8.6.[1]	dvayor yajamānayor ekasminn ahani somābhiṣavas saṃsavaḥ /
8.6.[2]	sa ca śatruviṣaya eva nāvidviṣāṇayos saṃsavo vidyata iti vacanāt /
8.6.[3]	so 'yaṃ saṃsavo 'smākam api śrutau dṛśyate yadi somau saṃsutau syātām iti /
8.6.[4]	tatredam ucyate /
8.6.[5]	saṃsave tu virājo lobhanam anapekṣyāsminn eva kāle viśvarūpāgānaṃ kāryam /
8.6.[6]	saṃsave hi yasya soma stotrair adhikas sa yajamāno jayati /
8.6.[7]	tasmād idan trayodaśam api stotraṃ guṇāyaiva tatra bhavati //
8.7.[1]	somābhiṣavasya kāla āgacchati /
8.7.[2]	uttarasya vidheḥ kālāvagamārtham idam uktam //
8.7.[3]	sa udgātābhiṣavakāle pūrvayā dvārā havirdhānagṛhaṃ prapadya dakṣiṇaṃ havirdhānam anena mantreṇābhimṛśati //
8.8.[1]	anena mantreṇottaraṃ havirdhānam abhimṛśati /
8.8.[2]	uttarasmin vākye so 'ntareṇa havirdhāne gatveti vidhānāt purastād eva tiṣṭhan havirdhāne abhimṛśet //
8.9.[1]	so 'ntareṇa havirdhāne pratyaṅmukho gatvā dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya paścād akṣaṃ vakṣyamāṇena krameṇopaviśati //
8.13.[1]	yatra yatra deśa āsīnaḥ karma kariṣyan bhavati tatra tatropaviśann etenaiva krameṇopaviśati /
8.13.[2]	nanv ayam upaveśanakramo madhuprāśane 'pi vyadhīyata /
8.13.[3]	tatraiveyaṃ paribhāṣā kasmān na kriyeta /
8.13.[4]	tatra ca kṛtāyām atropaveśanakramasyāvacane granthalāghavaṃ bhavatīti /
8.13.[5]	atra brūmaḥ /
8.13.[6]	yady eṣā paribhāṣā madhuprāśanādhikāre 'kariṣyatodgātur evāyam upaveśanakramo 'bhaviṣyat /
8.13.[7]	sa eva hi tatra prakṛtaḥ /
8.13.[8]	atrāpi sa eveti cen na kāla enam ity atroktena nyāyena sarveṣāṃ prakṛtatvāt /
8.13.[9]	tasmāt prastotrādīnām api karmārtham upaviśatām asya kramasya prāpaṇārtham atreyaṃ paribhāṣā kriyate /
8.13.[10]	evañ ced anenaiva paribhāṣāvākyena sarvatra siddhatvān madhuprāśane vacanam anarthakam /
8.13.[11]	nānarthakam asyāḥ paribhāṣāyās sāmagānārthopaveśanaviṣayatvajñāpanārthatvāt /
8.13.[12]	tataś ca bhakṣācamanahomādyarthaṃ yad upaveśanan tatra tūṣṇīm eva kartavyam /
8.13.[13]	asmin viṣaye paścāt prāñca upasīdanti-iti śrutau bahuvacanadarśanāt prastotṛpratihartror apy upaveśanaṃ ke cid icchanti /
8.13.[14]	tat tv anyāyyam udgātur evātra karmadarśanāt /
8.13.[15]	bahuvacanadarśanañ caivaṃ parihāryam /
8.13.[16]	asti droṇakalaśaprohaṇe 'pi śrutau bahuvacanam /
8.13.[17]	yad adho 'dho 'kṣan droṇakalaśam prohanti-iti /
8.13.[18]	tasmin pakṣe sarveṣām upaveśanārthaṃ bahuvacanam /
8.13.[19]	paścāt prāñca upasīdantīti /
8.13.[20]	ācāryeṇa tv adho 'dho 'kṣan droṇakalaśam prohatīti yad ekavacanayuktaṃ prohaṇan tad āśrīyate /
8.13.[21]	tathā hi vakṣyati taṃ prohatīti /
8.13.[22]	tasmād asya prohaṇasya kartodgātaivopaviśet //
8.16.[1]	atha namaḥ pitṛbhya ity etān sapta pādān udgātāha /
8.16.[2]	viśvarūpā iti bahuvacanenāsām anyatra grahaṇāt sāmni caivan darśanāt tisra etā ṛcaḥ /
8.16.[3]	tāsāṃ prathamā gāyatry uttare dvipade /
8.16.[4]	pādadvayābhyāsena sāmni sarvā gāyatryaḥ /
8.16.[5]	tatra dvābhyāṃ pādābhyām ekena dvābhyān dvābhyām ity avasyet /
8.16.[6]	evam etā ardharcaśa uktā bhavanti /
8.16.[7]	pratīkagrahaṇenāpi sidhyati liṅgapradarśanārtham āsām atra pāṭhaḥ kriyate /
8.16.[8]	tataś ca gāyatran traiṣṭubhañ jagad iti liṅgānurodhena savanatrayārtho 'yaṃ prayogo grāhya iti jñāpitaṃ bhavati /
8.16.[9]	tenottarasmin savana āsām aprayogas sidhyati /
8.16.[10]	atha vā yatraitāḥ paṭhyante tatraivāsāṃ prayogo grāhya iti vijñāpitaṃ bhavatīty ayam arthaḥ pāṭhena jñāpyate /
8.16.[11]	evam apy ukto 'rthas sidhyati /
8.16.[12]	idamādijapakarmakaraṇavarjaṃ savanasvarair eva prayogaḥ //
8.17.[1]	athāsmā udgātre 'dho 'dho 'kṣam akṣasya samīpata evādhastād droṇakalaśam adhvaryur anyo vā prayacchati //
8.20.[1]	taṃ pratigṛhya dakṣiṇa ūrau nidhāyākṣam upary upary akṣasya samīpata evopari pavitram apahṛtya tena pavitreṇa tribhir ebhir mantrais triḥ pavayati //
8.22.[1]	taṃ pavayitvā paścād akṣam akṣasya paścād anena mantreṇa sādayati //
8.23.[1]	tan droṇakalaśam akṣasya paścāt sādayitvā viśvarūpāsv ṛkṣu gāyatraṃ gāyati /
8.23.[2]	namaḥ pitṛbhya ity etā viśvarūpāḥ /
8.23.[3]	vidyate hy āsu viśvā rūpāṇi saṃbhṛtam iti //
8.23.[4]	itiśabdaḥ pūrvavidhiṃ parāmṛśati /
8.23.[5]	itthaṃ brāhmaṇam api vidyate /
8.23.[6]	taṃ paścād akṣaṃ sādayitvā gāyatraṃ viśvarūpāsu gāyati-iti /
8.23.[7]	kimartham idam ucyate /
8.23.[8]	asya viśvarūpāgānasya droṇakalaśavyāpāramadhyavartinas tadaṅgatvāśaṅkānivṛttyartham /
8.23.[9]	ayam abhiprāyaḥ /
8.23.[10]	kasya cit karmaṇo madhye tadasaṃbaddhasya karmaṇo 'nyāyyā kriyā /
8.23.[11]	tathāpy atra viśvarūpā gīyante yata idaṃ brāhmaṇam /
8.23.[12]	na hi vacanavihitam anyāyyan nāmeti /
8.23.[13]	atha vā yāni prātassavanāṅgāni śrutāv eva vidhīyante na tv ācāryeṇātra kīrtyante tair asya sādharmyam anena vākyena pratipādyata iti brāhmaṇam [iti] /
8.23.[14]	na vidadhāti brāhmaṇata evedam āgatam iti mantavyaṃ devasomabhakṣaṇādivad ity arthaḥ /
8.23.[15]	kim ataḥ phalam /
8.23.[16]	uttarasavanādau vakṣyāmaḥ //
9.1.[1]	tan droṇakalaśan tribhir ebhir mantrair akṣam adho 'dhas triḥ prohati //
9.2.[1]	akṣam upary upari pavitraṃ droṇakalaśe 'tyasyati /
9.2.[2]	tam antarīṣāt pavitram avahṛtyety uttaratra darśanād dhavirdhāna ity adhyāhartuṃ yuktan na droṇakalaśa iti /
9.2.[3]	satyam /
9.2.[4]	evam evābhaviṣyad yad asyaiva pavitrasya tad api darśanam abhaviṣyat /
9.2.[5]	anyat tu tat pavitraṃ yena droṇakalaśasaṃmārgas somapavanañ ca kriyate /
9.2.[6]	śrutau hi svarbhānur vā āsura ādityan tamasāvidhyad ity adhikṛtya phālgunam asya pavitraṃ kuryād iti phālgunasya pavitrasya vidhir droṇakalaśadṛṃhaṇavidhyanantaraṃ kriyate /
9.2.[7]	tadanantarañ ca śrūyate tad antareṣe avahṛtya sammārṣṭīti tad udīcīnadaśam pavitravatyā vitanoti-iti ca /
9.2.[8]	yadi caikenaiva pavitreṇa sarvo 'yam udgātṛvyāpāra syād droṇakalaśapavanādhikāra eva prāthamyāt pavitrotpattiḥ kathyeta /
9.2.[9]	tasmād droṇakalaśa evedaṃ pavitram atyasyet /
9.2.[10]	tad adhvaryugrahasaṃmārgārtham ādadīta //
9.3.[1]	akṣan nopaspṛśet /
9.3.[2]	akṣasya samīpe vyāpriyamāṇaḥ pramādenākṣam upaspṛśed apīti kṛtvā tatpratiṣedhaḥ kriyate //
9.4.[1]	yathetam antareṇaiva havirdhāne paretyoparavān apareṇa prāṅmukha upaviśyānena yajuṣā droṇakalaśam abhimṛśati /
9.4.[2]	asminn upaveśane sāma geyaṃ vakṣyate /
9.4.[3]	tasmād atrāvṛtaivopaviśet //
9.5.[1]	saṃgatamukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvānena mantreṇābhimṛśati //
9.6.[1]	teṣu saṃmukheṣu grāvasv anena mantreṇa droṇakalaśam adhyūhaty adhiśrayati //
9.7.[1]	tam anena yajuṣā dṛṃhati dṛḍhīkaroti /
9.7.[2]	yathā na kampate tathā karoti //
9.8.[1]	dvitīyam pavitram antarīṣād avahṛtya tena droṇakalaśan tribhir ebhir mantrais tris saṃmārṣṭi //
9.9.[1]	tat pavitram udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitran ta ity etenaiva tṛcena vitanoti droṇakalaśasyopari /
9.9.[2]	tatra hi somaḥ pavayiṣyate /
9.9.[3]	atha vā tacchabdo 'yan na pavitraviśeṣanārthaḥ /
9.9.[4]	nipāto 'yaṃ saptamyarthaḥ /
9.9.[5]	tasmāt tad iti tatra droṇakalaśa iti vyākhyeyam /
9.9.[6]	mantrāṇāṃ pṛthaktvāt trir vitanoti /
9.9.[7]	nanu tisṛbhir ity anuktatvāt tṛcenety uktatvāt tṛcasyānte sakṛd eva vitanitavyam /
9.9.[8]	yadi ca trir vitanyeta pūrvaṃ vitānadvayaṃ vyarthaṃ bhavet /
9.9.[9]	atra brūmaḥ /
9.9.[10]	tisṛbhir ṛgbhir iti padadvayena yo 'rtho vācyaḥ sa evocyate tṛceneti /
9.9.[11]	yadi cātra bhedo na gṛhyeta puruṣasūktena juhuyād ity atra sūktānte sakṛd eva hūyeta na ca tatraivaṃ kriyate /
9.9.[12]	tasmād atrāpi trir eva vitanitavyam /
9.9.[13]	vitānadvayavaiyarthyañ caivaṃ parihriyate /
9.9.[14]	prathamayā pavitrasyaiko bhāgo vitanitavyo dvitīyayāpy ekas tṛtīyayāpy eka iti //
9.10.[1]	somam unnetā pavitra ānayati //
9.12.[1]	tam ānīyamānam udgātābhyām ṛgyajuṣābhyām abhimantrayate /
9.12.[2]	mahyam pavasvetyantaṃ yajuḥ /
9.12.[3]	ṛg uttarā //
9.13.[1]	śukras somaḥ /
9.13.[2]	taṃ santatam avicchinnadhāram udgātāraḥ pavayanti /
9.13.[3]	kathaṃ pavayanti /
9.13.[4]	pavitraṃ parigṛhṇanti /
9.13.[5]	nanu secane mukhyaḥ pavanaśabdaḥ /
9.13.[6]	neti brūmaḥ /
9.13.[7]	ubhayasminn asmin kriyamāṇe rasarjīṣayor viveko bhavati somānayane pavitraparigrahe ca /
9.13.[8]	tatra somānayanam unnetuś coditam /
9.13.[9]	ataḥ pavitram evodgātāraḥ parigṛhṇantas somaṃ pavayanti /
9.13.[10]	asmin pavitraparigrahaṇakāle prastotṛpratihartārau prapadyeyātām /
9.13.[11]	sāmagānābhāvāc ca tūṣṇīm evopaviśetām /
9.13.[12]	āvṛtaiva tu prastotā parigāṇagrahaṇa upaviśet //
9.14.[1]	somagrahān adhvaryavo gṛhṇanti //
9.15.[1]	āgrayaṇan nāma grahaṃ gṛhṇann adhvaryur hiṃkaroti /
9.15.[2]	vakṣyamāṇasya vidheḥ kālajñāpanārtham idam uktam //
9.16.[1]	tad eva hiṃkṛtaṃ hiṃkāro bhavati /
9.16.[2]	yad uttarasmin vākya udgātrā geyaṃ sāma vidhāsyate tasyādhvaryukṛto hiṃkāro 'ṅgaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ /
9.16.[3]	na caitad ayuktam ity āśaṅkyaṃ yad āgrayaṇāṅgatvenādhvaryuṇā kriyamāṇo 'yaṃ hiṃkāra udgātrā gīyamānasya sāmno 'py aṅgatvenopakaroti /
9.16.[4]	śrutyā hy ayam artho vihitaḥ /
9.16.[5]	adhvaryur āgrayaṇaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇan hiṃkaroti /
9.16.[6]	tad eva hiṃkṛtam bhavati /
9.16.[7]	athodgātaikarce gāyatraṃ gāyaty uccā te jātam andhaseti /
9.16.[8]	na cāsti śrutivihitam ayuktan nāma /
9.16.[9]	atha vā na vidhir arthavādo 'yan tad eva hiṃkṛtaṃ bhavatīti /
9.16.[10]	arthavādeṣu ca sato 'sato vārthasya stutyartham upādānam adoṣaḥ /
9.16.[11]	kiṃ punar arthavādena sūtre prayojanam /
9.16.[12]	nāsti prayojanam /
9.16.[13]	śīlam etad ācāryasya yat kva cic chrautam arthaṃ śrutivākyenaiva vadatīti /
9.16.[14]	śrutyanāpattaye ca granthagauravam apariharann arthavādam api noddharati //
9.17.[1]	adhvaryuhiṃkārānantaram udgātoccā te jātam andhasety asminn ekarce gāyatraṃ gāyati /
9.17.[2]	śrutivākyatvād udgātṛgrahaṇam aparihāryam /
9.17.[3]	atha vāsaty asminn udgātṛgrahaṇa ānantaryād aṅgabhūtahiṃkārakartṛtvāc cādhvaryuṇedaṃ sāma geyam āśaṅkyeta /
9.17.[4]	yady apy āśaṅkyeta-athodgātaikarce gāyatraṃ gāyatīti śrutir eveyam āśaṅkān nivartayati /
9.17.[5]	evañ ced idam udgātṛgrahaṇaṃ kurvann ācāryo jñāpayaty anādiṣṭakartṛkaṃ gānam anudgātāpi kva cid ānantaryāt kuryād iti /
9.17.[6]	kiṃ prayojanam /
9.17.[7]	santi parigāṇāni dīkṣaṇīyāyān tārkṣyasāmanī gāyed ity ārabhya vihitāni /
9.17.[8]	tāni kartranādeśād udgātuḥ prasaktāni jñāpakād asmāt prastotur gātavyāni /
9.17.[9]	asti hi tasyānantaryaṃ yato 'yam anantaravihitāni pravargyasāmāni gāyati /
9.17.[10]	uktañ ca tāṇḍināṃ sūtre sarvatrānādeśe parigāṇāni prastotā gāyed iti /
9.17.[11]	asmākam apy anyārthan darśanam evam evopapadyate /
9.17.[12]	yad udgātā prathamena karmaṇaudumbarīm anvārabhata iti //
9.18-19.[1]	sarveṣu graheṣu gṛhīteṣv apa upaspṛśyādbhir hastau prakṣālya pṛthivīm anaya rcābhimṛśati //
9.20.[1]	anena yajuṣātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati /
9.20.[2]	uraḥ praty ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśatīti paravacanadarśanād uro 'bhimraṣṭavyam /
9.20.[3]	atha vā pratiśabdo 'yan nopasargaḥ /
9.20.[4]	karmapravacanīyo 'yaṃ lakṣaṇe 'tra pravartate /
9.20.[5]	tasmād evaṃ yojyam /
9.20.[6]	ātmābhimarśanaṃ praty ātmābhilakṣitan deśam abhimṛśatīti /
9.20.[7]	ataś cātmanas sthānaṃ hṛdayam abhinimraṣṭavyam /
9.20.[8]	kutaḥ punas sarvagatasyātmano hṛdayam eva viśeṣeṇa sthānam /
9.20.[9]	kathyate /
9.20.[10]	śrutāv eva darśanāt /
9.20.[11]	tasyai haitasyai devatāyai yathā mṛtpiṇḍa iṣīke adhihate syātām evam eva hṛdaye pādāv adhihatāv iti /
9.20.[12]	bhagavadgītāsu ca dṛśyate īśvaras sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛddeśe 'rjuna tiṣṭhati /
9.20.[13]	bhrāmayan sarvabhūtāni yantrārūḍhāni māyayeti //
10.1.[1]	apa upaspṛśya santatā anyo'nyasmād avicchinnā vakṣyamāṇāḥ puruṣā havirdhānāt sarpanti /
10.1.[2]	idam apām upasparśanaṃ sahavidhānāt sarpaṇāṅgam //
10.2.[1]	prathamo bhūtvādhvaryus sarpati //
10.2.[2]	anantaram adhvaryos tam anvārabhya prastotā sarpati //
10.2.[3]	pūrvavad atha brahmeti vaktavye ṣaṣṭhas sarpatīti vacanaṃ śrutyanukaraṇārtham /
10.2.[4]	atha vā pratiprasthātus sarpaṇapakṣe yad brahmā paścād bhavatīti vacanāt saptamatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prāptam /
10.2.[5]	brahmā ṣaṣṭhas sarpatīti vacanād eva ṣaṣṭhatvam /
10.2.[6]	tatrācāryeṇa ṣaṣṭhatvam evedan niyamyate //
10.3.[1]	pravṛtahomā nāma homāḥ /
10.3.[2]	tān adhvaryvādayo 'smin kāle juhvati /
