10.3.[3]	nanūpariṣṭāt pravarasya pravṛtahomā hūyamānā drśyante samākhyāpi caiṣām evam eva yujyate /
10.3.[4]	satyam etat /
10.3.[5]	atra tv eṣāñ coditatvād evam eva mantavyam /
10.3.[6]	prakaraṇataḥ paśukarma somābhiṣavāt prāg eva ke cid icchanti //
10.5.[1]	anaya rcaitām āhutim udgātāro juhvati /
10.5.[2]	kva juhvati /
10.5.[3]	sannidhānād āhavanīye /
10.5.[4]	kena dravyeṇa /
10.5.[5]	anyasyāvacanāt sarvārthasyājyasyādhvaryubhis saṃskṛtasya vidyamānatvāj juhotīty ukte sarpiḥ pratīyeteti ca paraiḥ paribhāṣitatvād ājyena /
10.5.[6]	yady api cānādiṣṭe srucaiva hotavyam iti paribhāṣā pareṣām asti tathāpy asmābhis sruveṇaiva hotavyam iti /
10.5.[7]	ayaṃ hy ācārya auṣadham api sruveṇaiva hotavyaṃ vadati /
10.5.[8]	sruve sakṛd ājyam upastṛṇāti dvir haviṣo 'vadyatīti /
10.5.[9]	atha vaikam evedaṃ vākyam //
10.6.[1]	anena yajuṣā dvitīyām āhutiñ juhoti /
10.6.[2]	kim udgātaiva juhoti /
10.6.[3]	naivam /
10.6.[4]	yady apy ekavacanād udgātur eva prāpnoti tathāpi sarveṣām atra prakṛtatvād brāhmaṇe cāraṇyam iva vā ete yantīti sarvān evādhikṛtya vihitatvāt sarve juhvati /
10.6.[5]	nanu tatrāpy ekavacanam eva gṛhyate 'tha dvitīyāñ juhotīti /
10.6.[6]	ko nety āha /
10.6.[7]	prakaraṇād dhi sarve juhvatīty uktam /
10.6.[8]	nanv ekavacanaśruter ekasya prāpnoti prakaraṇāt sarveṣāñ śrutiś ca prakaraṇād balīyasī /
10.6.[9]	atra brūmaḥ /
10.6.[10]	evaṃ vākyārthavido vyavasyanty upakramavaśena samāptir grāhyeti /
10.6.[11]	asya ca vākyasyopakramo bahvāśrayo 'raṇyam iva vā ete yantīti /
10.6.[12]	tatropakramavaśenārthe gṛhyamāṇe 'tha dvitīyāñ juhotīty ekavacanam ekatvavivakṣayā na śrūyate /
10.6.[13]	vidhyartham evedam iti manyāmahe /
10.6.[14]	kiñ ca mantraliṅgenārthavādena ceyam āhutiḥ puruṣasaṃskārārthā /
10.6.[15]	tasyāḥ puruṣabhede yuktaivāvṛttiḥ /
10.6.[16]	pratipradhānaṃ hi guṇo bhidyate /
10.6.[17]	tasmāt sarvatrāpi puruṣārthāni karmāṇy ekavacanavihitāny api kartranādeśe sarvair adhikṛtaiḥ kartavyāni //
10.7.[1]	te 'dhvaryuprabhṛtayo bahiṣpavamānārtham udañcas sarpanti /
10.7.[2]	ānantaryavidhānād dṛṣṭopakārakatvāc ca sarpaṇasya bahiṣpavamānāṅgatvāvagamād bahiṣpavamānāyety anarthakam /
10.7.[3]	nānarthakaṃ prahvārā iva prakupitā iva sarpantīti vidhidvayasya parigrahārthatvāt //
10.8.[1]	sarpatsu sarpaṇakāle 'nena yajuṣādhvaryum anumantrayate /
10.8.[2]	sarpatsv ity anarthakam /
10.8.[3]	nānarthakaṃ vidhikrameṇa sarpaṇasamāptāv asya vidheḥ prasaktasya sarpaṇamadhye kriyārthatvāt /
10.8.[4]	nirdhāraṇe veyaṃ saptamī sarpatsv iti /
10.8.[5]	tathāpi vartamānakālopadeśādiṣṭaṃ sidhyati //
10.9.[1]	asmin kāle kaś cit karmakaraś cātvālan dakṣiṇena tṛṇāny udapātreṇa saha saṃstṛṇāti /
10.9.[2]	vikaraṇavyatyayo 'yañ chāndasaḥ /
10.9.[3]	stṛṇotīti hi prāpnoti /
10.9.[4]	tṛṇāni saṃstīrya teṣūdapātran nidadhātīty arthaḥ /
10.9.[5]	nanv anādiṣṭakartṛkaṃ karmodgātrā kartavyam iti /
10.9.[6]	satyam etat /
10.9.[7]	udgātrā tu sarpaṇāvicchedenāsya vidher asau na kuryāt /
10.9.[8]	karmakara eva karoti //
10.10.[1]	teṣu tṛṇeṣūpaveśanasyāvṛtā krameṇāhe daidhiṣavyetyādinopaviśanti /
10.10.[2]	viśeṣaś ca vakṣyata udagāvṛtta udgāteti /
10.10.[3]	etenaivopaviśatīti paribhāṣayaiva siddhatvād upaveśanasyāvṛtety anarthakam /
10.10.[4]	nānarthakam idam ekam upaveśanam uttarayoḥ pavamānayor anāvṛtaiva kartavyam ity etadarthatvāt /
10.10.[5]	nanu tatra savanādāv upaveśanam āvṛtaiva kartavyaṃ vakṣyate /
10.10.[6]	kim ataḥ /
10.10.[7]	idam ato bhavati /
10.10.[8]	pavamānakāle yad upaveśanan tad asaty apy asmin yatne 'nāvṛtaiva tatra siddham iti /
10.10.[9]	naivaṃ yujyate /
10.10.[10]	ubhayathāpy upaveśanam āvṛtaiva tatra prasaktaṃ savanādau vacanena pavamānakāle paribhāṣayā /
10.10.[11]	tatrāyam uktārthasiddhyarthaṃ yatnaḥ kriyate /
10.10.[12]	ke cid anyathā vyācakṣate /
10.10.[13]	yāsau paribhāṣaitenaivopaviśatīti sodgātṛviṣayaiva /
10.10.[14]	yāni tv imāni vacanāny upaveśanasyāvṛtopaviśantīti tāni prastotṛpratihartror api tatropaveśanāvṛtaṃ prāpakāṇīti //
11.1.[1]	udaṅmukha udgātopaviśati //
11.2.[1]	āstāvasya purastāt pūrvārdhe pratyaṅmukhaḥ prastotopaviśati //
11.3.[1]	āstāvasya paścād aparārdhe dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ pratihartopaviśati /
11.3.[2]	nanu prathame vākya udgātṛśabdo vidhīyate /
11.3.[3]	tasmād udgātuḥ purastād udgātuḥ paścād iti vyākhyātuṃ yuktam /
11.3.[4]	atra brūmaḥ /
11.3.[5]	yady evaṃ vyākhyāyetānyo'nyaprātimukhyam udgātṝṇāṃ kiñ cid api na syāt /
11.3.[6]	dṛśyante ca loke prātimukhyenaivānyo'nyasya saha gāyanto vadantaś ca /
11.3.[7]	upakāraś ca kaś cit prātimukhye vidyata eva /
11.3.[8]	tasmād āstāvasyety eva vākyadvaye 'dhyāhriyate nodgātur iti /
11.3.[9]	asti śrutivihitan devasomabhakṣaṇan nāma /
11.3.[10]	tasyāyaṃ kālaḥ /
11.3.[11]	idañ cāsya rūpam /
11.3.[12]	samīpa āsīnānām ṛtvijām anyeṣāṃ vā brāhmaṇānāṃ yaṃ viśeṣeṇa śuciṃ manyeta taṃ brūyād āhara hastam iti /
11.3.[13]	tatas tasya dakṣiṇaṃ hastam ālabhyāsāv upahvayasvety uktvā labdhopahavas tasmād idaṃ yajur japed yo devānām iha somapītho 'smin yajñe barhiṣi vedyān tasyedaṃ bhakṣayāmasīti /
11.3.[14]	asmin kṛte stotram adhvaryuḥ prayacchati //
11.6.[1]	stotram ity adhvaryuṇā dīyamānasya barhirdvayasya saṃjñā /
11.6.[2]	pavamāneṣu tu prastaraṃ barhirdvayañ ca kāsu cid vikṛtiṣv anyad anyad api dravyaṃ stotratvena vakṣyate /
11.6.[3]	stavanasya ca karaṇam ivedam upacaryate /
11.6.[4]	stuvanti teneti hi stotraṃ bhavati /
11.6.[5]	stotram adhvaryuhastataḥ pratigṛhyemaṃ pavamānajapañ japati /
11.6.[6]	pavamānajapam ity anarthakam /
11.6.[7]	nānarthakam atra vidhīyamānānān dharmāṇāṃ sarvastotreṣu prāpaṇārthatvāt /
11.6.[8]	stotrapratigrahaṇādīnāṃ hi bahiṣpavamānāṅgataiva prakaraṇāt prāptā /
11.6.[9]	tatrāsyaiva japasya pavamānena viśeṣaṇād anyeṣāṃ sarvastotrāṅgatā grahītuṃ śakyā //
11.7.[1]	āvartiṣu stotraṃ pratigṛhyedaṃ yajur japati /
11.7.[2]	kāni punar āvartīni /
11.7.[3]	yāni pavamānebhyo 'nyāni stotrāṇi tāny āvartīni /
11.7.[4]	āvṛttyā hi rksāmayos tāni niṣṭhīyante /
11.7.[5]	evañ cet sandhimānasīnayor ayañ japo na prāpnoti /
11.7.[6]	na hi tayor ṛksāmāvṛttiḥ /
11.7.[7]	atra brūmaḥ /
11.7.[8]	naivam asmābhiḥ pratijñātam yeṣv ṛksāmāvṛttis tāny evāvartīnīti /
11.7.[9]	yeṣv āvartiśabdo dṛśyate tāny āvartīni /
11.7.[10]	sa ca śabdo yājñikair apavamāneṣu sarvastotreṣu prayujyamāno dṛśyate /
11.7.[11]	kevalan tu śabdapravṛttyavalambanam āvṛttiḥ kathitā /
11.7.[12]	na ca tāvatā yeṣu nāvṛttis tāny anāvartīnīti bhavanti /
11.7.[13]	yathā gamanād gaur iti niścīyate nisargapaṅgvām api gavi gośabdo mukhya evābhyupagamyate /
11.7.[14]	tasmāt sandhimānasīnayor apy āvartitvād ayañ japaḥ prāpnoty eva /
11.7.[15]	yadi ca sandher anāvartitvam uttamām āvartiṣu hotra ity ayaṃ vidhis sandhau na syāt /
11.7.[16]	tatrāpi tu baudhāyanenānūdito 'yaṃ vidhiḥ /
11.7.[17]	hotra eṣottameti prāhur iti /
11.7.[18]	tena jñāpyate sandhir āvartīti /
11.7.[19]	audumbarīparigraho yatrāsti tatra so 'sminn avasare kartavyaḥ //
11.8.[1]	anena mantreṇopagātṝn pratyabhimṛśati /
11.8.[2]	bahuvacanaprayogān mantreṇa sakṛd evoktena sarve 'bhinimraṣṭavyāḥ /
11.8.[3]	ke punar upagātāro bhavanti /
11.8.[4]	idaṃ brūmaḥ /
11.8.[5]	yeṣām ṛtvijām udgātṛbhyo 'nyeṣāṃ stotrasaṃbandhaḥ kaś cid vidyate teṣv eva trayo yajamānacaturthā upagāyanti /
11.8.[6]	stutānuśaṃsanāc chastriṇāṃ stotropākaraṇāder adhvaryos stotraprasavād brahmaṇaś cāsti saṃbandhas stotreṇa /
11.8.[7]	tatra svaśākhāyām evādhvaryor upagānaṃ pratiṣidhyate hotuś ca /
11.8.[8]	tatrāpi catura evopagātṝn kurvīteti brāhmaṇād brāhmaṇācchaṃsyacchāvākayor eko na gṛhyate /
11.8.[9]	anyais tribhir upagātavyam yajamānena ca /
11.8.[10]	tasya hi kāmaṃ ha tu yajamāna upagāyet /
11.8.[11]	yajamānasya hi tad bhavatīty asmacchrutāv atha yad yajamāna stotram upagāyati prāṇā vā udgātāraḥ prāṇān eva tad ātman dhatta itītyādeś ca paraśrutau vidher darśanād upagātavyam //
11.9.[1]	athādhvaryus saṃpreṣyati /
11.9.[2]	katham adhvaryuḥ /
11.9.[3]	udgātaiva saṃpreṣyati /
11.9.[4]	na śakyam udgātrā saṃpreṣitum /
11.9.[5]	na hy atra kathyata itthaṃ saṃpreṣyatīti /
11.9.[6]	yadi ca vyākhyāyeta brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstar iti saṃpreṣyatīti tad apy ayuktam /
11.9.[7]	saṃpraiṣo nāma kiñ cit karmoddiśya parasya śāsanam na caivaṃvidhaṃ brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstar ity atra dṛśyate /
11.9.[8]	āheti cākhyātenāsya saṃbandho vakṣyate /
11.9.[9]	anyathā hi kim āhety ākāṅkṣayaivāvatiṣṭheta /
11.9.[10]	tasmād adhvaryur evātra saṃpreṣyati /
11.9.[11]	tasya ca saṃpraiṣeṣu prasiddhe na kṛtam adhvaryugrahaṇam /
11.9.[12]	nanv ittham ity avacane 'dhvaryuṇāpy aśakyam eva saṃpreṣitum /
11.9.[13]	satyam etat /
11.9.[14]	svaśākhāyām eva tu tasyāyaṃ saṃpraiṣo vihita oṃ studhvam iti /
11.9.[15]	evam apy ādhvaryavasya vidher atra vacanam anarthakam /
11.9.[16]	nānarthakaṃ studhvam ity adhvaryuṇā saṃpreṣite brahman stoṣyāma ityādir uttaro vidhir ity etadarthatvāt //
11.11.[1]	prastotā brahmāṇaṃ maitrāvaruṇañ ca brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstar ity āha /
11.11.[2]	kuta āgato maitrāvaruṇaḥ /
11.11.[3]	praśāstar iti liṅgāt /
11.11.[4]	evañ ced brahmann iti liṅgād eva brahmaṇo 'pīti siddher brahmāṇam ity anarthakam /
11.11.[5]	nānarthakaṃ praśāstar ity asyānityatvajñāpanārthatvāt /
11.11.[6]	evaṃ hi bahvṛcabrāhmaṇe śrūyate /
11.11.[7]	atha yat prastotā brahmāṇam āmantrayate brahman stoṣyāma iti mano vā agraṇīr bhavaty eṣāṃ prāṇānāṃ manasaiva prasūtās stomena stuyāmeti /
11.11.[8]	atho apānam eva tan manasā santanotīti //
11.11.[9]	prasave brahmapraśāstṛbhyām ukta upadadhaty udgātāraḥ /
11.11.[10]	upagāyantīty arthaḥ /
11.11.[11]	nanu dadhātir gānan nābhidadhāti /
11.11.[12]	satyam etat /
11.11.[13]	atropadhātavyadravyāśrute stavanaprasavānantaryavidhānāc ca gānārtho dadhātiḥ kalpyeta /
11.11.[14]	kasmāt punar upagāyantīty evānuktam /
11.11.[15]	udgātṛkarmakatvārtham /
11.11.[16]	upagānaṃ hi samākhyayopagātṛbhiḥ kartavyam /
11.11.[17]	tad atra paraśabdena cocyamānaṃ sat samākhyāprāpyaṃ kartāram alabhamānam udgātāra eva kurvantīti yuktaṃ vaktum /
11.11.[18]	kiṃ punar idam upagānan nāma /
11.11.[19]	idam ucyate /
11.11.[20]	pūrvasyā gāyatropaniṣadaṣ ṣaṣṭhasaptamayor anuvākayos sadharmakam upagānan nirūpitam /
11.11.[21]	tatra saptame tad dhaitad eka om ity gāyantīty uktvā tat tathā na gāyed iti tat pratiṣidhya o ity u haike gāyantīti punar uktvā tad api no eva tathā gāyed iti pratiṣidhya punar apy o ity eva gāyed ity upagānasya rūpan nirūpitam /
11.11.[22]	tatra madhyamasya pakṣasya nigītatayā doṣeṇa pratiṣedhāt tasmād aviśeṣe cottamasya pakṣasya vyarthatvaprasaṅgāt kena cid uditena gītiviśeṣeṇa saṃyuktasyāsya okārasya si yau ho huṃ mā tāyā huṃ metivad iha vu vā vu vo vā sākho hā itivac caikasvaryeṇedaṃ grahaṇam iti mantavyam /
11.11.[23]	sa ca gītiviśeṣo gāyatrasya prakṛtatvād tadudgīthasya yo 'vayavo viśeṣeṇoditas tatsadṛśo mantavyaḥ /
11.11.[24]	tasmād ayam okāraḥ kruṣṭādisvaracatuṣṭayaṃ krameṇa prāpya punaḥ prathamam ārūḍhaś caturdaśamātra upagānasaṃjño niścīyate /
11.11.[25]	tad idam upagānam upadadhatīti vihitam ihopagātāraḥ kuryuḥ /
11.11.[26]	kṛte kṛte prastāve kuryuḥ /
11.11.[27]	evaṃ hi śrūyate /
11.11.[28]	etad dha vai sāmno 'ntararaṇyaṃ yat prastutam anabhisvaritam ādīyate /
11.11.[29]	svareṇa saṃpādyodgāyed iti /
11.11.[30]	svara iti copagānasyākhyā tebhyas svaraṃ prāyacchad ityādau granthe samupalakṣyate /
11.11.[31]	tasmāt svareṇa saṃpādyodgāyed ity upagānena saṃpādyodgāyed ity uktaṃ bhavati /
11.11.[32]	vakṣyati ca paryadhyāye /
11.11.[33]	atha khalu prastutaṃ sāma na puropagebhya ādadīta /
11.11.[34]	sahaivopagair ādadīteti /
11.11.[35]	sāmamadhye ye prastāvās teṣu katham /
11.11.[36]	teṣv avikṛteṣv antararaṇyasyānapāyārthaṃ sahaivopagātṛbhir ādadīta //
11.12.[1]	yo 'yaṃ sāmasu bahuśo dṛśyate huṃ iti śabdas sa hiṃkāraḥ /
11.12.[2]	sakṛt kṛto hiṃkāro yasya tat sakṛddhiṃkṛtam /
11.12.[3]	evañ cet sakṛtkṛtahiṃkāram iti prāpnoti /
11.12.[4]	satyam etat /
11.12.[5]	prāmāṇyād ācāryasyāhitāgnyādiṣu paṭhitaṃ hiṃkṛtaśabdaṃ manyāmahe /
11.12.[6]	tasmād adoṣaḥ /
11.12.[7]	ta udgātāras sakṛddhiṃkṛtena parācānāvṛttastotriyeṇa bahiṣpavamānena bahiṣpavamānastotreṇa stuvate /
11.12.[8]	kiṃ punar asya rūpam /
11.12.[9]	atra brūmaḥ /
11.12.[10]	ṛksāmak.lptiḥ prākṛtatantrato brāhmaṇataś cāvagantuṃ śakyā /
11.12.[11]	tato 'yam ācāryo bahiṣpavamānādīni stotrāṇi nātra kalpayati siddhavan nāmnaiva nirdiśati /
11.12.[12]	asmābhis tu prakṛtibhedāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pṛthag eva saptamādhyāyaparisamāptau kalpayiṣyante /
11.12.[13]	āvṛttyavacanād eva parāktvasiddheḥ parācety anarthakam /
11.12.[14]	nānarthakaṃ parāktvaṃ sakṛddhiṃkaraṇe hetur iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
11.12.[15]	tataś ca sandhiśiromānasīneṣu nisargaparākṣu pratitṛcaṃ pratyṛcaṃ hiṃkāraṃ vidhāya punar yaḥ pakṣo bhāllabiparigṛhīto vakṣyata apy u haibhis sakṛddhiṃkṛtair eva bhāllabina stuvata iti /
11.12.[16]	tasyāsmābhir api vikalpena parigrahas sidhyati //
11.13.[1]	bahiṣpavamānasya prathamā stotriyā retasyā /
11.13.[2]	sāhiṃkṛtā bhavati /
11.13.[3]	yo gāyatre hiṃkāro h\.uṃ bhā ity evaṃrūpas tasyāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ //
11.13.[4]	retasyāyā itarāṇi gāyatrāṇi hiṃkṛtāni bhavanti /
11.13.[5]	kim ayan dvitīyo hiṃkāraś codyate /
11.13.[6]	neti brūmaḥ /
11.13.[7]	ya evāsti hiṃkāras tasyedaṃ vacanam /
11.13.[8]	tat kimartham /
11.13.[9]	hiṃkṛtatvam eva retasyayā atulyatvam itareṣāṃ gāyatrāṇām iti jñāpanārtham /
11.13.[10]	tena dhurām agānam uktaṃ bhavati /
11.13.[11]	prastūyamāne gāyatre manasā hiṃkṛtyāpānya vāg iti brūyāt /
11.13.[12]	eṣa gāyatrasya pratihāraś śrutivihita ācāryeṇāpi stuvata iti bahuvacanacodanayā jñāpita eva //
11.14.[1]	stute bahiṣpavamāna idaṃ yajur udgātā yajamānaṃ vācayati //
11.15.[1]	mādhyandine pavamāne stuta idaṃ yajur vācayati //
11.17.[1]	āvartiṣu stuteṣv idaṃ yajur vācayati /
11.17.[2]	eteṣu triṣu vidhāneṣv anu tvārabha ityādir mantrāvayavo 'rthasaṃpattyartham anuṣajyeta /
11.17.[3]	ke cid uttame vidhāna ā mā stutasyetyādim evānuṣaṅgaṃ tāṇḍibhis tathā pratipannatvād icchanti /
11.17.[4]	vayan tu niścinumahe /
11.17.[5]	anu tvārabha ityādir evāvartiyajuṣo 'py anuṣaṅgo bhavitum utsahate saṅgatārthatvāt /
11.17.[6]	tasmāt sarvatrāpi sa evānuṣaṅga iti /
11.17.[7]	mantraikadeśaparityāge hi nātra pramāṇam upalabhāmahe /
11.17.[8]	yas tu tāṇḍināṃ pāṭhas sa tair evāśrayitavyaḥ /
11.17.[9]	na hi sarūpā eva mantrās sarveṣāṃ bhavanti /
11.17.[10]	yajamānavācanānantaraṃ stotrabhūtayor barhiṣor ekam antarvedy upāsyet /
11.17.[11]	atyasyed aparaṃ bahirvedi //
11.18.[1]	adhas stuta ity adhasstuvānaḥ prastotā bhavati /
11.18.[2]	sa pavamāneṣu madhyamāṃ stotriyām eṣā madhyamety adhvaryave prāha /
11.18.[3]	nanu prastotṛgrahaṇam eva kartavyam /
11.18.[4]	kim aprasiddhenādhasstuvānaśabdena /
11.18.[5]	atra brūmaḥ /
11.18.[6]	nāyam adhasstuvānaśabdo nirdeśārtha eva kevalaṃ prastotuḥ /
11.18.[7]	prastāvānantaraṃ prāhety etadartho 'pi /
11.18.[8]	ko 'bhiprāyaḥ /
11.18.[9]	vartamānasāmīpye stuvānaśabdo grāhyaḥ /
11.18.[10]	adhaśśabdena ca prastāvo lakṣyate /
11.18.[11]	tatrāyam artho labhyate /
11.18.[12]	prastutya kiñ cid apy avilambya prāheti /
11.18.[13]	yady ayaṃ stuvānaśabdo 'sya vidheḥ prastāvānantaryāvagamārtho nedānīṃ prastotā nirdiśyate /
11.18.[14]	arthata eva prastotety avagamyate /
11.18.[15]	uktaṃ hy adhaśśabdena prastāvo lakṣyata iti /
11.18.[16]	tatra prastāvaṃ kurvan prāhety asminn arthe labdhe prastotā prāheti na durlabham /
11.18.[17]	prastotraiva hi prastāvaḥ kriyate /
11.18.[18]	nanu prastāvāt pūrvam apy asyāṃ procyamānāyāṃ vartamānasāmīpyan na vihanyate /
11.18.[19]	tasmāt prastāvaṃ kṛtvā kariṣyatā vaiṣā procyā /
11.18.[20]	satyam etat /
11.18.[21]	ubhayathāpi vartamānasāmīpyam anuruddhaṃ bhavati /
11.18.[22]	yadi tu pūrvaṃ prastāvād eṣā procyetottarayos savanayor nidhanaprastāvasandhānāsaṃbhavāt stotravicchedaḥ prasajyeta /
11.18.[23]	tasmāt samyag evāvādiṣma prastutya brūyād iti /
11.18.[24]	yugmastomeṣu pavamāneṣu dve stotriye madhyame /
11.18.[25]	kā tatra procyā /
11.18.[26]	uttareti brūmaḥ /
11.18.[27]	nanu pūrvāpi madhyamaiva /
11.18.[28]	tasyā asati kāraṇe 'tikramaṇam anyāyyam /
11.18.[29]	atra brūmaḥ /
11.18.[30]	madhye bhavā madhyamā /
11.18.[31]	iha caitayos stotriyayor antarālaṃ madhyam /
11.18.[32]	tatra pūrvasyā aparārdho madhyasannikṛṣṭaḥ /
11.18.[33]	uttarasyāḥ pūrvārdhaḥ /
11.18.[34]	pūrvārdhaś cāparārdhāt pradhānam /
11.18.[35]	udgīthaś ca sāmni pradhānaṃ sa ca pūrvasyāḥ pratihāropadravanidhanavyavetatvād viprakṛṣṭo madhyamasya prastāvenaiva tu vyavāyād uttarasyās sannikṛṣṭaḥ /
11.18.[36]	sarvasannikarṣāsaṃbhave ca pradhānasannikarṣo grāhyaḥ /
11.18.[37]	tasmāt pavamānottarabhāgasya yā prathamā saiva yugmastomeṣu procyā //
11.18.[38]	āvartiṣu yottamā stotriyā tām eṣottameti hotre prāha /
11.18.[39]	atra hotṛśabdo hotṛmaitrāvaruṇabrāhmaṇācchaṃsyacchāvākopalakṣaṇārtho grāhyaḥ /
11.18.[40]	tat kimartham /
11.18.[41]	asya vidhes sārthakatvārtham /
11.18.[42]	maitrāvaruṇādīnāṃ hi stotreṣu kim uttamā jānatā hotrā kriyate /
11.18.[43]	āvartiṣu hi stotraśastrayor upasantānaṃ bāhvṛcye vihitam /
11.18.[44]	tat tu śastrī stotrāntam ajānan na śaknuyāt kartum /
11.18.[45]	tatra yaś śastrī hotrādiṣu tasminn eṣottameti jñāpyamāne 'rthavad idaṃ vidhānaṃ bhavati /
11.18.[46]	tasmāt sādhv evoktaṃ hotṛśabdo 'tra hotrādyupalakṣaṇārtha iti /
11.18.[47]	dṛśyate ca maitrāvaruṇādiṣv api hotṛśabdaḥ /
11.18.[48]	yathā sapta hotāra ṛtuśo yajantīti /
11.18.[49]	evañ ca maitrāvaruṇāyaiṣottameti prāhur ity evamādi baudhāyanavacanam upapadyate //
11.19.[1]	athaitat sannihitam udapātram anena yajuṣodgātā cātvāle 'vanayati /
11.19.[2]	nanu prastotā prakṛtaḥ /
11.19.[3]	satyam etat /
11.19.[4]	athaśabdas tv ayaṃ prakṛtād anyam udgātāram adhikaroti /
11.19.[5]	etad ity anarthakam /
11.19.[6]	nānarthakamuttarapavamānāṅgabhūtasyodapātrasyāvanayananivṛttyarthatvāt //
11.20.[1]	yad uttiṣṭhed anyaḥ puruṣa ṛtvig anyo vā tam uttiṣṭhantam ārabhyāvalambya pāṇinā so 'nūttiṣṭhet /
11.20.[2]	sa iti ko 'tra nirdiśyate /
11.20.[3]	anādeśād udgāteti prāptam /
11.20.[4]	sarve tu puruṣasaṃskārarūpatvāt /
11.20.[5]	śrutau te vai tad anṛtaṃ kurvanti ye martyaṃ santam amṛtatvaṃ gamayanti te rūpeṇa varcasā vyṛdhyanta iti bahuvacanopakramāntatvāt sarvair udgātṛbhiḥ kartavyam imaṃ vidhin niścinumaḥ /
11.20.[6]	tasmāt sa iti śabdaḥ prastotrādibhiḥ pratyekaṃ saṃbadhyate /
11.20.[7]	śrutivākyasyaivāsya prakṣepād akṣaragauravam aparihāryam /
11.20.[8]	stutvoddravanti ... bāhūn udgṛhṇantīti /
11.20.[9]	anayor vidhyor ayam avasaraḥ /
11.20.[10]	tasmād utthāyodaṅmukhāḥ kiñ cid uddrutya bāhūn udgṛhṇīyuḥ /
11.20.[11]	bāhūn ity aviśeṣavihitatvād yajamānam eva tat svarge loke samādadhatīty asyāś ca stuter evam evopapannataratvāt sarvān bāhūn udgṛhṇīyuḥ /
11.20.[12]	nanv imau vidhī utthānāt pūrvam eva śrutau vihitau /
11.20.[13]	tasmāt pūrvam eva kartavyau /
11.20.[14]	atra brūmaḥ /
11.20.[15]	nānutthitair uddravaṇaṃ śakyaṃ kartum /
11.20.[16]	taduttarakālañ ca bāhūdgrahaṇam /
11.20.[17]	ato 'rthakrameṇa balavatā pāṭhakramam ullaṅghya parastād evotthānād imau vidhī kartavyau /
11.20.[18]	evam apy utthānānantaryam anayor vidhyor na saṃbhavati yato yajamānavikramaṇam utthānānuvādena vidhāsyate /
11.20.[19]	utthāyottaravedyante yajamānaṃ vikramayatīti /
11.20.[20]	naiṣa doṣaḥ /
11.20.[21]	imau vidhī kṛtvāpi vikramaṇe kriyamāṇe notthānānuvādo na ghaṭate /
11.20.[22]	na hi tasyānantaryāt prayojanam /
11.20.[23]	kin tarhi /
11.20.[24]	tatraiva vakṣyāmaḥ /
11.20.[25]	tasmād utthānoddravaṇabāhūdgrahaṇayajamānavikramaṇāni krameṇa kartavyāni //
11.21-22.[1]	utthāyottarasmin vedyante yajamānaṃ vikramayati /
11.21-22.[2]	utthāyety anarthakam /
11.21-22.[3]	nānarthakaṃ yatrotthānan tatraiva vikramaṇam ity etadarthatvāt /
11.21-22.[4]	tasmād uttarasmin savane na vikramaṇaṃ pravarteta /
11.21-22.[5]	tatra hy uparitanasyāpi karmaṇas sadasy evāsīnaiḥ kartavyatvād utthānasyābhāvaḥ /
11.21-22.[6]	kathaṃ punar vikramayati /
11.21-22.[7]	vakṣyate //
11.21-22.[8]	yajamānasya dakṣiṇaṃ pādam anena mantreṇāntarvedi vikramayati //
11.21-22.[9]	māsmāl lokād avācchaitsīr iti savyaṃ pādaṃ bahirvedi vikramayati /
11.21-22.[10]	liṅgād yajamānena vikramaṇayajuṣī vaktavye /
11.21-22.[11]	asmin kāle kartavyasyābhāvād yathāprapannan niṣkramyāsīran //
12.1.[1]	savanīyasya paśor vapayā yadā caritaṃ vyāpṛtaṃ hutaṃ bhavati /
12.1.[2]	tadanantaram udgātāra ābhiḥ pañcabhir ṛgbhiś cātvāle mārjayante /
12.1.[3]	ādyās tisro gāyatryaś caturthy anuṣṭup pañcamī pratiṣṭhā dvipadā /
12.1.[4]	ittham etāḥ pañca bhavanti /
12.1.[5]	kiṃ punar iha granthagauravaṃ kriyate caritaṃ bhavatīti /
12.1.[6]	carantīty eva vaktavyam /
12.1.[7]	tāvatāpy ayam arthas sidhyati /
12.1.[8]	tathā cānyatra vadati /
12.1.[9]	yadā dvitīyam āpaḥ pariṣiñcati yadā dhiṣṇyān nivapantīti /
12.1.[10]	satyam etat /
12.1.[11]	vacanavairūpyeṇa tv anenāsya vidher viśiṣṭaviṣayatā jñāpyate /
12.1.[12]	tasmāt sattreṣv evaitan mārjanam /
12.1.[13]	uktaṃ hi tāṇḍisūtre cātvāle tu mārjanam pūrvaṃ sattreṣv iti /
12.1.[14]	upapattiñ cātra brūmaḥ /
12.1.[15]	paśvaṅgam etan mārjanam /
12.1.[16]	paratantre hi paśusaṃbandhānām eva rtvijāṃ brahmāgnīdadhvaryupratiprasthātṛhotṛpraśāstṝṇāṃ patnīyajamānayoś ca vihitam /
12.1.[17]	tasmād udgātṝṇāṃ yatra paśusaṃbandhas tatraiva kartavyaṃ manyāmahe /
12.1.[18]	sattre ca teṣāṃ yajamānatvād asti paśusaṃbandho nānyatra /
12.1.[19]	tasmāt sādhūktaṃ sattra evedaṃ mārjanam iti /
12.1.[20]	evañ ced yajamānasyaiva mārjanaṃ vidhātavyam /
12.1.[21]	yajamānatvād evodgātṝṇāṃ sattre sidhyati /
12.1.[22]	yady evaṃ vidhīyeta kiyad yajamānakarmodgātṛbhis sattre kāryaṃ kiyan neti na jñāyeta /
12.1.[23]	iha punaḥ puruṣārthasyāsya yājamānasyodgātṝn prati sattre vidhīyamānatvāt puruṣārthāny udgātāro 'pi kuryuḥ kratvarthāni gṛhapatir evety ayam artho labhyate /
12.1.[24]	tasmād acodyam etat /
12.1.[25]	prakṛtatvād udgātṝṇām udgātṛgrahaṇam anarthakam /
12.1.[26]	nānarthakaṃ sarvodgātṛparigrahārthatvāt /
12.1.[27]	tataś ca subrahmaṇyasyāpi sidhyati //
13.1.[1]	prapadanasya prapatter āvṛtā krameṇa yajñopavītācamanaprapadanamantrātmakena cātvālotkarāv antareṇa prapadya vedyākramaṇenānena mantreṇa vedim ākrāmaty adhitiṣṭhati /
13.1.[2]	ekavacanaprayuktam apy etad vedyākramaṇādy ā samīkṣaṇād dvāror yad asti vidhijātaṃ tat puruṣasaṃskārarūpatvāt sarvaiḥ kartavyaṃ yeṣām antarvedi karmāsti /
13.1.[3]	vedyākramaṇasaṃjñayā tṛtīyasavane saṃvyavahāraḥ kariṣyate /
13.1.[4]	atra pūrvaṃ prastotā gacchati tata udgātā tataḥ pratihartā /
13.1.[5]	eṣa hi sāmagāne kramaḥ //
13.2.[1]	antarvedi tiṣṭhann anena yajuṣādityam upatiṣṭhate //
13.3.[1]	vakṣyamāṇān dhiṣṇyān upatiṣṭhate /
13.3.[2]	idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
13.3.[3]	nānarthakaṃ vakṣyamāṇānām āhavanīyādīnān dakṣiṇavedyantaparyantānān dhiṣṇyatvajñāpanārthatvāt /
13.3.[4]	prayojanaṃ samastadhiṣṇyopasthāna eṣām abhisandhānam //
13.4.[1]	anena yajuṣāhavanīyan tatsamīpe prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhann upatiṣṭhate //
13.5.[1]	bahiṣpavamānasyāstāvaṃ stavanadeśam anena yajuṣopatiṣṭhate /
13.5.[2]	idamādiṣu kavyo 'sītyanteṣu mantreṣu raudreṇetyādiḥ pūrvamantrāvayavo 'nuṣajyeta /
13.5.[3]	nanv agna iti padam anagniṣv āstāvādiṣu virudhyeta /
13.5.[4]	atra brūmaḥ /
13.5.[5]	uktam asmābhis sarveṣām eṣān dhiṣṇyatvam /
13.5.[6]	yasmāc ca samastadhiṣṇyopasthānamantra āgneya eva vidhāsyata agnayas sagarā iti tasmād evaṃ grāhyam /
13.5.[7]	upapanna evānagniṣv apy agniśabdo dhiṣṇyeṣv iti /
13.5.[8]	tasmād ayam anuṣaṅgas sarvān api dhiṣṇyān anūpasarpati //
13.7.[1]	yasminn agnau paśuś śrapyate sa śāmitraḥ /
13.7.[2]	sa bahirvedi tiṣṭhati /
13.7.[3]	tam antarvedy eva tiṣṭhanta upatiṣṭheran //
13.9.[1]	aindrīm ity anena yajuṣā dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anu pradakṣiṇaṃ paryāvṛtyāgnīdhram uttareṇa parītya tasya paścāt prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhann anena yajuṣāgnīdhram upatiṣṭhate /
13.9.[2]	prāṅmukhatvasya smṛtisadācārasiddhes subrahmaṇyādiṣu ca tadavidhānasyaivam evopapadyamānatvāt prāgāvṛtta ity anarthakam /
13.9.[3]	nānarthakam udaṅmukhatvasyāpi smṛtisadācāraprāpitasyaiva nivṛttyarthatvāt /
13.9.[4]	evañ ced udaṅmukhatvaṃ subrahmaṇyādiṣv api vikalpena prāpnoti /
13.9.[5]	satyam etat /
13.9.[6]	vitānaparāṅmukhatvādinā tu doṣeṇa tatra nivāryate /
13.9.[7]	yatra tu doṣo nāsti tatra vikalpena bhavaty eva /
13.9.[8]	parair apy uktaṃ devakarmāṇy adhikṛtya prāṅyāyāny udaṅyāyāni veti /
13.9.[9]	tasmāt sarvatrāpi prāṅmukhagrahaṇan niyamārtham eva //
13.10.[1]	sadasaḥ purastāt pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhann anena yajuṣā hotur dhiṣṇyam upatiṣṭhate //
13.11.[1]	maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyo hotur dhiṣṇyād dakṣiṇataḥ /
13.11.[2]	vakṣyamāṇāś catvāra uttare //
13.16.[1]	mārjālīyo dakṣiṇasmin vedyante tiṣṭhati //
13.19.[1]	sadasi yatra brahmāste tad brahmasadanam //
13.20.[1]	yatra hotāste tad dhotṛṣadanam /
13.20.[2]	yatra sthitair upasthito hotṛdhiṣṇyas tatraiva sthitās sarvān etān maitrāvaruṇadhiṣṇyādīn hotṛṣadanāntān avalokayanta upatiṣṭheran //
13.21.[1]	sadasa uttareṇa parītya sadasaḥ paścāt pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhann anena yajuṣā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate /
13.21.[2]	yaḥ pūrvam āhavanīyas so 'gnipraṇayanād ūrdhvaṃ gārhapatyo bhavati //
13.22.[1]	purāṇagārhapatyānvāhāryapacanayoḥ prājahitasaṃjñā yājñikeṣu prasiddhā //
13.23.[1]	itaraḥ prājahito 'nvāhāryapacanaḥ //
13.24.[1]	anena yajuṣā dakṣiṇaṃ mahāvedyantam upatiṣṭhante /
13.24.[2]	śālāyāṃ hi yā vedis sedānīm apavṛttaprayojanatvād avediḥ /
13.24.[3]	yatra sthitair upasthito gārhapatyas tatraiva sthitāḥ prājahitavedyantān avalokayanta upatiṣṭheran //
13.25.[1]	savyam aṃsam anv apasavyaṃ paryāvṛtya tatraiva tiṣṭhan sarvān dhiṣṇyān abhisandhāya ye draṣṭuṃ śakyās tān avekṣyānena yajuṣopatiṣṭhate //
13.26.[1]	sadaso dvārau dvāram abhitas sthūṇe anena yajuṣā samīkṣate /
13.26.[2]	kim idam ucyate sthūṇe iti /
13.26.[3]	dvārāv eva sadasaḥ pūrvāpare samīkṣitavye /
13.26.[4]	satyam /
13.26.[5]	evam eva prāptam /
13.26.[6]	mantras tv ayaṃ pūrvān dvāram anaṅgabhūtāṃ sadasaḥ prapadanasyāṅgabhūtāñ cāparāṃ sahābhidadhad arthasaṃpadan na labheta /
13.26.[7]	asmin pakṣe tu yayā dvārā sadaḥprapadanaṃ tām abhito ye sthūṇe tayor mantreṇābhidhānam /
13.26.[8]	tatrārthasaṃpad ucyate /
13.26.[9]	dvāśśabda evātra kevalaṃ lakṣaṇayā sthūṇayor gṛhyeta /
13.26.[10]	dṛśyate ca lokavedayor arthavirodhe lakṣaṇā /
13.26.[11]	yathāgnau tiṣṭhatīti śrutvāgnisamīpa iti gṛhṇanti /
13.26.[12]	mārjālīye stuvīrann iti ca mārjālīyasamīpa iti /
13.26.[13]	tasmād atra sthūṇayor eva samīkṣaṇam /
13.26.[14]	asminn eva ca viṣaye baudhāyanasya vacanam evam evopapadyate apare dvārau sadasaḥ pūrve dvārau sadasa iti //
13.27.[1]	sadasas patim ity etaya rcā sadaḥ prapadyaudumbarīn dakṣiṇena parītya tasyā uttarata upaveśanasya krameṇa nirasanādinopaviśanti /
13.27.[2]	dvividham ṛkpāṭhasya prayojanam /mayi varca ity atraiva pratyapādi /
13.27.[3]	paribhāṣayaiva siddhatvād upaveśanasyāvṛtety anarthakam /
13.27.[4]	nānarthakaṃ mādhyandine 'pi savane sadaḥprapadanānantaram upaveśanāvṛtaivopaviśeyur ity etadarthatvāt /
13.27.[5]	vakṣyate hi tatra vedyākramaṇādi sadaḥprapadanāntaṃ savanādāv eva kartavyam iti /
13.27.[6]	upaveśanatadāvṛtau tu tasmin kāla upaviṣṭaiḥ kartavyasyābhāvān na prāpnutaḥ /
13.27.[7]	atas tu vacanād upaveśanāvṛt prāpnoti /
13.27.[8]	tatprāptāv upaveśanam apy arthasiddham /
13.27.[9]	atha vā yad bahiṣpavamāna atra copaveśanasyāvṛteti vacanam tad evaṃ vyākhyeyam /
13.27.[10]	upaveśanasyāvṛtā udagāvṛtta udgātety anantaraṃ vakṣyamāṇayeti /
13.27.[11]	tatra pūrvaṃ vacanaṃ sarvastotreṣūdagāvṛttatvādiṃ prāpayati idañ ca sarvasomabhakṣeṣu //
14.2.[1]	somacamasāṃś camasādhvaryavas sadasy āharanti //
14.3.[1]	abhakṣayitvaiva camasān iḍām upahvayate /
14.3.[2]	tasyām upahūyamānāyāñ camasān udgṛhṇanty uccair dhārayanti /
14.3.[3]	iḍāpātrasamīpa eva camasodgrahaṇaṃ kartavyam /
14.3.[4]	iḍopahvāne hi camasānāṃ kañ cit saṃskārañ janayitum udyamanaṃ kriyata iti mantavyam /
14.3.[5]	sati ca sāmīpye saṃskāro yujyate nāsati /
14.3.[6]	tathā ca paratantre vacanam upodyacchanti camasān iti //
14.4.[1]	hutasya somasyāvayavaṃ bhakṣayanti /
14.4.[2]	na vā somasyety adhyāhāryam /
14.4.[3]	camasagrahaṇam evānuvartayitavyam /
14.4.[4]	tad arthataṣ ṣaṣṭhyantaṃ bhavati /
14.4.[5]	śakyate ca lakṣaṇayā camasaśabdena camasagatas somo nirdeṣṭum /
14.4.[6]	hutānām eva camasānām atrāhriyamāṇatvād uttaratra ca tadbhakṣaṇasya vidhāsyamānatvād idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
14.4.[7]	nānarthakaṃ bhakṣaṇasya pratipattikarmatvāvagamanārthatvāt /
14.4.[8]	dravyasya hi kva cid upayogāt kṛtārthasya sato yad anyad ucyate karma tasya pratipattitvaṃ nyāyyam /
14.4.[9]	tad ācāryeṇa vivriyate /
14.4.[10]	hutasya homenaiva kṛtaprayojanasya somasya śeṣaṃ bhakṣayantīti /
14.4.[11]	tatrāyam artho labhyate /
14.4.[12]	hutaśeṣasya bhakṣyamāṇatvāt pratipattir bhakṣaṇam iti /
14.4.[13]	kiṃ punar asya pratipattitvajñāpane prayojanam /
14.4.[14]	idam ācāryeṇaivocyate //
14.4.[15]	ahutasya somasyāvayavan na bhakṣayanti /
14.4.[16]	yasmāt pratipattikarma bhakṣaṇan tasmād idam uktam /
14.4.[17]	yadi hi bhakṣaṇam arthakarma syāc camasagate some pramādāt sarvasmin huta ekenaiva vā bhakṣite sati śeṣasyābhāve śrutasyābhāve pratinidhir iti nyāyena vrīhyabhāve nīvārair iva yāgasya bhakṣaṇasyāpy anyena somena nivṛttiḥ prāpnoti /
14.4.[18]	tad anena vākyena nivāryate /
14.4.[19]	kim atra bhakṣaṇaṃ lupyate /
14.4.[20]	kas sandehaḥ /
14.4.[21]	asaty etasmin ye dravyārthās saṃskārās te dravyābhāve lupyanta iti /
14.4.[22]	asti [ca] pareṣāṃ vacanaṃ hutaśeṣābhāvam adhikṛtya lupyate sviṣṭakṛd iḍābhakṣaś ceti /
14.4.[23]	pūrveṇa tāvad vākyena pratipattikarmatvaṃ bhakṣaṇasya jñāpitam /
14.4.[24]	anena tatphalam abhihitam /
14.4.[25]	tayor ayam arthas samāsena /
14.4.[26]	yasmād dhutaśeṣasya bhakṣaṇaṃ pratipattis tasmād asati hutaśeṣe lupyata eva bhakṣaṇam /
14.4.[27]	nānyas somo bhakṣayitavya iti /
14.4.[28]	anyathāpi vākyadvayaṃ vyākhyāyate //
14.5.[1]	hotur bhakṣam anu hotari bhakṣitavaty udgātāras sarve bhakṣayanti /
14.5.[2]	svaṃ svañ camasaṃ hotrā bhakṣitaṃ bhakṣayantīty arthaḥ /
14.5.[3]	yad uktam adhastanavidhidvayasya vidhim etaṃ prati hetutvan tad idaṃ vivriyate /
14.5.[4]	yasmād dhutasya camasasya hotrādayo 'vaśyaṃ bhakṣayanty ahutasya codgātrādayo na bhakṣayanti tasmād dhotur udgātrādīnāñ caikasmiṃś camase bhakṣaṇaṃ prāpnoti /
14.5.[5]	tatra kaḥ pūrvaṃ bhakṣayatīti tatkramākāṅkṣāyām idam ucyate hotur bhakṣam anu bhakṣayantīti /
14.5.[6]	nanv anenaiva vidhināsyārthasya siddhatvād dhetudvayam anarthakam /
14.5.[7]	nānarthakaṃ praśāstrādibhir vaṣaṭkṛtāṃś camasāṃs teṣām eva bhakṣaṇam anu bhakṣayantīti nārāśaṃsāṃś cānākāṅkṣyaiva hotṛbhakṣaṃ bhakṣayantīty etadarthatvāt /
14.5.[8]	yasya vā vaṣaṭkāre hūyante camasās so 'tra hotṛśabdebna nirdiśyate havanasya kartā hoteti /
14.5.[9]	tasmād uttaram eva hetudvayasya prayojanam //
14.6.[1]	hutāvaśiṣṭān puroḍāśān iḍopahvānānantaram adhvaryvādayo bhakṣayanti //
14.7.[1]	puroḍāśān bhakṣayitvā tadanantaraṃ somaṃ vakṣyamāṇena camasāvekṣaṇādinā prakrameṇa sarve bhakṣayanti //
14.8.[1]	rājānaṃ bhakṣayitvā vā puroḍāśān bhakṣayanti /
14.8.[2]	ayam apy ekaḥ pakṣaḥ /
14.8.[3]	nanu puroḍāśāḥ pūrvam eva somād ijyante tasmāt pūrvam eva somād bhakṣayitavyāḥ /
14.8.[4]	ato 'yaṃ pakṣo na yujyate /
14.8.[5]	yujyata evāyaṃ pakṣaḥ /
14.8.[6]	na hy ayuktam ācāryo vadati /
14.8.[7]	na caitad ekāntena dṛśyate yāgakrameṇaiva bhakṣaṇam iti /
14.8.[8]	parastād dhi puroḍāśebhyas trayo grahā dvidevatyā ijyante pūrvan tu bhakṣyante /
14.8.[9]	athaitan mataṃ dvidevatyān bhakṣayitveḍām upahvayata iti vacanadarśanād atikramya yāgakramaṃ pūrvam eva puroḍāśebhyo dvidevatyā bhakṣyante /
14.8.[10]	atra tu vacanan na dṛśyata iti /
14.8.[11]	atrāpi śrutivacanam ācāryaprāmāṇyād anumātavyam /
14.8.[12]	atha vā sattraviṣayam evaitad vākyaṃ na bhakṣaṇakramasya vikalpakaṃ rājānaṃ vā bhakṣayitvā puroḍāśān iti /
14.8.[13]	tatrāyaṃ vāśabdas samuccaye rājānaṃ bhakṣayitvā ca sattre puroḍāśān bhakṣayantīti /
14.8.[14]	prasthitabhakṣottarakālaṃ hi sarvayajamānānāṃ sattre puroḍāśabhakṣaḥ /
14.8.[15]	paratantre hi codyate /
14.8.[16]	so 'yam asmākam apy ucyate /
14.8.[17]	tasmād udgātāro 'pi sattre savanamukhīyān bhakṣayitvā puroḍāśān bhakṣayeyuḥ //
14.9.[1]	atrāsmin pradeśe somabhakṣād ūrdhvam asmā udgātre svaryaṃ svarāya hitaṃ yajamānapuruṣā āharanti /
14.9.[2]	vidhānakrameṇaiva somabhakṣoparitanatvam asya vidhes sidhyati /
14.9.[3]	tasmāt sattraviṣayatānivṛttyartham asya vidher atreti prākṛta evaikāho nirdiśyate /
14.9.[4]	pūrvasya hi vākyasya sattraviṣayatvam uktam /
14.9.[5]	tad asyāpi sannidher āśaṅkya tan nivartyate /
14.9.[6]	atha vā pūrvo vidhis sattraviṣaya iti jñāpanārtham idam atreti vacanam //
14.10.[1]	u iti nipāto vākyālaṃkārārthaḥ /
14.10.[2]	yady anyad bhakṣayiṣyan bhavati kṣunnivṛttyartham odanādi tac cāsminn eva kāle 'smā āharanti /
14.10.[3]	vikalpe vāyam uśabdaḥ /
14.10.[4]	tasmād ayaṃ vidhir anityaḥ //
14.11.[1]	yat pūrvaṃ vihitaṃ rājānaṃ bhakṣayantīti tasyeyam itikartavyatā kathyate /
14.11.[2]	athodgātā svañ camasaṃ hotrā bhakṣitam ādāyānena yajuṣāvekṣate /
14.11.[3]	udgātṛgrahaṇam anarthakam /
14.11.[4]	nānarthakaṃ gānakramaprāpitasya prastotṛpūrvatvasya nivṛttyarthatvāt //
14.12.[1]	evam evetare prastotṛpratihartārau subrahmaṇyaś ca yathāpūrvañ camasam avekṣante /
14.12.[2]	prastotā pūrvam avekṣate tataḥ pratihartā tatas subrahmaṇyaḥ /
14.12.[3]	idam eṣām ānupūrvyaṃ varaṇatatpratimantraṇayor dṛṣṭam /
14.12.[4]	tad yathāpūrvam iti vacanād gṛhyate /
14.12.[5]	avekṣaṇopahvānayo rājānaṃ bhakṣayantīti bhakṣaṇaṃ vidhāya vihitatvād bhakṣaṇāṅgatve ca parikalpya prayojanavatvād bhakṣaṇaṃ prati copakartuṃ samarthatvād bhakṣaṇāṅgatā niścīyate /
14.12.[6]	aṅgapradhānayoś caikakālatā naiyāyikair iṣyate /
14.12.[7]	tasmād atra vidhir avekṣaṇasya svarūpaparijñānārtha eva na kālārthaḥ prastotrādīnām /
14.12.[8]	udgātāraṃ prati vihitam avekṣaṇaṃ prasaṅgena teṣām api vidhīyate /
14.12.[9]	evam upahave 'pi draṣṭavyam /
14.12.[10]	tasmāt prastotrādayo 'pi yadā camasaṃ bhakṣaṇārtham ādadīran tadaivāvekṣyopahavam iccheyuḥ //
14.13.[1]	athopahavam anujñānaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ prati hotar upahvayasvetyādibhir vākyair udgātecchate hotuḥ prastotuḥ pratihartus subrahmaṇyāc ca /
14.13.[2]	evaṃ hi hotar ityādi padacatuṣṭayam upapadyate nānyathā /
14.13.[3]	na hi hotar upahvayasvety upahavākāṅkṣaṇam adhvaryutaś śakyaṃ kartum /
14.13.[4]	evam asmai bhakṣaṇaṃ praty anujñām ākāṅkṣamāṇāyāvaśyam anujñā kartavyā /
14.13.[5]	na cātroktam evam anujānīyād iti /
14.13.[6]	tatra laghutvāt samarthatvāt parair api parigṛhītatvād upahūta ity anujānīyuḥ //
14.14.[1]	udgātaiva hotary upahavam icchate na prastotṛpratihartārau subrahmaṇyaś ca /
14.14.[2]	nanūdgātur hotur upahavākāṅkṣaṇasya pūrvavākyasiddhasyāvidheyatvāt prastotrādīnāñ cāvihitasyānivartyatvād idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
14.14.[3]	nānarthakam ekasmiṃś camase yāvatāṃ bhakṣas samavaiti te sarve 'nyo'nyasmād upahavam iccheyur iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
14.14.[4]	idaṃ hi vākyaṃ prastotrādīnāṃ hotur upahavecchānivṛttyartham /
14.14.[5]	nivṛttiś ca satyām eva prāptau yuktā /
14.14.[6]	tasmād eṣāṃ hotāraṃ praty upahavecchaikapātratvāt prāpnotīti mantavyam /
14.14.[7]	uktañ ca mīmāṃsāyāṃ vacanād anujñātabhakṣaṇam ity adhikṛtya tad ekapātrāṇāṃ samavāyād iti /
14.14.[8]	evañ ced anenaiva mārgeṇodgātur api hotrādibhyaḥ prāptatvād upahavecchāyāḥ pūrvaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
14.14.[9]	nānarthakaṃ hotar upahvayasvetyādīnām upahavākāṅkṣaṇanigadānāṃ vidhānārthatvāt /
14.14.[10]	upahavam icchata iti prāptam evānūdyate tatra guṇavidhānārtham //
14.15.[1]	prastotṛpratihartārau subrahmaṇyaś codgātary upahavam iccheyur udgātar upahvayasveti /
14.15.[2]	nanu pūrvavākyoditenaiva mārgeṇāsyārthasya siddhatvād idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
14.15.[3]	nānarthakam udgātar upahvayasvety asya nigadasyotpādanārthatvāt /
14.15.[4]	siddhasya hi punarvacanaṃ viśeṣavidhitsayā kriyate /
14.15.[5]	sarvañ cedaṃ siddham evodgātari prastotṛpratihartārau subrahmaṇyaś ceti /
14.15.[6]	atas sarvo 'yam anuvāda eva /
14.15.[7]	vidhyavayavas tv asya vākyasyārthād adhyāhriyata udgātar upahavyasveti /
14.15.[8]	evaṃ hi śrutasadṛśam evādhyāhṛtaṃ bhavati /
14.15.[9]	subrahmaṇyagrahaṇaṃ sattrārtham /
14.15.[10]	nātra bhakṣas subrahmaṇyasya /
14.15.[11]	evaṃ hi baudhāyanenoktaṃ ke nu khalv ṛtvijām ekāhe soman na bhakṣayantīti /
14.15.[12]	unnetā grāvastut subrahmaṇya ity eva brūyād iti /
14.15.[13]	punaś coktaṃ katham u khalu sattre dīkṣitā bhakṣayeyur iti /
14.15.[14]	neṣṭuś camasa unnetā bhakṣayed acchāvākacamase grāvastud udgātṛcamase subrahmaṇya iti /
14.15.[15]	atha vā bhakṣayaty evātra subrahmaṇyaḥ /
14.15.[16]	na hi dṛśyate pramāṇaṃ sattrārthatve subrahmaṇyagrahaṇasya /
14.15.[17]	nanūktaṃ baudhāyanavacanam /
14.15.[18]	na baudhāyanavacanāśrayeṇaivāsya sattrārthatā niścetuṃ śakyā /
14.15.[19]	asti hi matibhedo 'py ācāryāṇān naikamatyam eva sarvatra /
14.15.[20]	tasmād evaṃ gṛhyatām /
14.15.[21]	bhakṣaṇam eva subrahmaṇyasyāsmadācāryeṇābhipreyate baudhāyanena tv abhakṣaṇam iti /
14.15.[22]	yathānyatrāpy athodgātā [vā] prastotā vā dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya paścād akṣam upasṛpya prāñcaṃ grāvasu droṇakalaśam adhyūhatīti baudhāyanenoktaṃ na vayam anuvartāmahe /
14.15.[23]	udgātraiva droṇakalaśakarma kartavyaṃ niścinumahe /
14.15.[24]	tadvad atrāpi draṣṭavyam /
14.15.[25]	kāmaṃ baudhāyanavacanam abhakṣaṇakāraṇaṃ mā bhūt /
14.15.[26]	asmākam eva ca śrutau subrahmaṇyo bahirvedi karotīti darśanam abhakṣaṇakāraṇaṃ bhavati /
14.15.[27]	idaṃ hi darśanam antarvedi subrahmaṇyasya na kiñcit karmety avagamayati /
14.15.[28]	bhakṣaṇañ ca sadasi bhakṣayantīti vacanam atikramya na bahirvedi kartuṃ yuktam /
14.15.[29]	tasmād asyārthaluptaṃ bhakṣaṇam /
14.15.[30]	nedaṃ darśanam asyābhakṣaṇe kāraṇam /
14.15.[31]	idaṃ hi subrahmaṇyāprakaraṇe dṛśyate /
14.15.[32]	ato bahirvedikāritvaṃ tasyām evāvatiṣṭhate /
14.15.[33]	nāsya sadasi bhakṣaṇaṃ nivārayati /
14.15.[34]	tasmāt sadasy evāsīnas subrahmaṇyo bhakṣayet /
14.15.[35]	atha vā sadasi subrahmaṇyadeśasyāvidhānāt sadasi bhakṣayantīti vacanasya prāyikatvād yathāgnīdhras svaśālāyām evāsīno bhakṣayati tadvat subrahmaṇyo 'pi svasmin deśa utkara evāsīno bhakṣayet /
14.15.[36]	evaṃ hi bahirvedikāritvasya sarvaviṣayatve 'pi na doṣaḥ /
14.15.[37]	mīmāṃsāyāñ ca subrahmaṇyasya bhakṣo 'sti vā na veti vicāro vidyate /
14.15.[38]	tatra śabarasvāminā tāvad bhakṣaṇapakṣa eva siddhāntatvena niścitaḥ /
14.15.[39]	bhavadāsenāpy evam eva niścitya punar vyākhyānāntareṇābhakṣaṇapakṣas sādhitaḥ /
14.15.[40]	punar api saṃśayitam /
14.15.[41]	etāni ca tatra sūtrāṇi /
14.15.[42]	udgātṛcamasam ekaś śrutisaṃyogāt /
14.15.[43]	sarve vā sarvasaṃyogāt /
14.15.[44]	stotrakāriṇo vā tatsaṃyogād bahuśruteḥ /
14.15.[45]	sarve tu vedasaṃyogāt kāraṇād ekadeśe syād iti /
14.15.[46]	avaśyañ caivam avagantavyam /
14.15.[47]	eka eva pakṣas siddhāntatayā sūtreṣu nyasta iti /
14.15.[48]	tan tu pakṣam anavadhārayanto vṛttikārā vipratipadyante /
14.15.[49]	alam atipraṣaṅgena /
14.15.[50]	ko 'nayoḥ pakṣayor asmābhir āśrayaṇīyaḥ /
14.15.[51]	na vayam anujānīmaḥ /
14.15.[52]	saṃśaya evātra śreyān naikapakṣāśrayaṇam /
14.15.[53]	saṃśaye cālopo lopān nyāyya iti kaiś cid uktatvād bhakṣaṇam eva kartuṃ yuktam /
14.15.[54]	tāṇḍinas tv abhakṣaṇam āśrayante /
14.15.[55]	asmābhir api bhagavato baudhāyanasya vacanakriyāyāṃ nāśivam iti bhakṣaṇan nācaryate /
14.15.[56]	na tu sandehas tyajyate /
14.15.[57]	yadi tu bhakṣayed vedyākramaṇādi sarvaṃ kṛtvā sadasy eva yathāvakāśam upaviśya bhakṣayet //
15.1.[1]	iyaṃ paribhāṣā sarvasomabhakṣaviṣayā /
15.1.[2]	upahavam iṣṭvā bhakṣayantīti nāniṣṭvā /
15.1.[3]	camasagate sarvasminn athopahavam icchata ity anenaiva siddhatvāt ṣoḍaśigrahādāv asyopayogaḥ /
15.1.[4]	kasmāt punas tatropahavecchā /
15.1.[5]	yeṣāṃ tatra bhakṣas tebhyo 'dhvaryvādibhyaḥ //
15.1.[6]	atra bhakṣayantīty anuvartate /
15.1.[7]	anena mantreṇa somaṃ bhakṣayanti /
15.1.[8]	atha vā ṣoḍaśigrahādāv apy udgātaiva hotarīty atroktenaiva mārgeṇaikapātre 'ny[o'ny]asmād upahavecchāyās siddhatvād ekam evedaṃ vākyam //
15.2.[1]	evam evottarayor api savanayos savanamukhīyeṣu savanamukhavartiṣu camaseṣu chandassavane upadiśya gaṇavad bhakṣayanti /
15.2.[2]	gāyatracchandasaḥ prātassavanasyeti mantra eva chandassavanayor upadiṣṭatvāc chandassavanopadeśam ity anarthakam /
15.2.[3]	nānarthakaṃ viśiṣṭayoś chandassavanayor grahaṇārthatvāt /
15.2.[4]	tasmād uttarayos savanayor ye nāmanī ye ca cchandasī teṣām ayam upadeśaś codyate /
15.2.[5]	tataś caitat siddham /
15.2.[6]	triṣṭupchandaso mādhyandinasya savanasya jagatīcchandasas tṛtīyasavanasyeti /
15.2.[7]	kasmāt punar etayor ekasyāsamāsenaikasya samāsenābhidhānaṃ kriyate /
15.2.[8]	ācāryeṇaivam eva mādhyandine savane mādhyandinaṃ savanam iti tṛtīyasavane tṛtīyasavanam iti ca tatra tatraikasyāsamāsenaikasya samāsenābhidhīyamānatvāc chrutau ca sarvatraivam eva dṛśyamānatvāt /
15.2.[9]	gaṇavad iti kim ucyate /
15.2.[10]	idaṃ vadāmaḥ /
15.2.[11]	yāv amū sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa iti padaviśeṣau tau gaṇaśabdavatvāt gaṇaśabdenābhidhātuṃ śakyau /
15.2.[12]	tatrāyaṃ matuppratyayas tatpadadvayābhidhāyakād gaṇaśabdād utpannas tadvattāṃ mantrasyābhidadhāti /
15.2.[13]	atha vā gaṇavad vasvādidevatāgaṇavad ity arthaḥ /
15.2.[14]	ime hi pade sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa iti vasvādidevatāgaṇaparigrāhiṇī /
15.2.[15]	tato 'py atra labhyate sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa ity etatpadadvayavatteti /
15.2.[16]	evañ ced gaṇavattāyāḥ pāṭhasiddhatvād gaṇavadgrahaṇam anarthakam /
15.2.[17]	nānarthakaṃ gaṇavattvasya savanamukhīyebhyo 'nyatra nivāraṇārthatvāt /
15.2.[18]	kva nivāryate /
15.2.[19]	ṣoḍaśyādau /
15.2.[20]	tatrāpi hy ayam eva mantro 'nuṣṭupchandasa ityādivikāram āpādya vidhāsyate /
15.2.[21]	nanv anārāśaṃseṣu ca gaṇān iti kariṣyamāṇenaiva yatnena ṣoḍaśyāder gaṇavattā nivartiṣyate /
15.2.[22]	atrānabhividhāya pṛthag abhihitatvād anuṣṭupchandasa ity etāvān eva tatra mantravikāra syāt /
15.2.[23]	atas tu yatnād gaṇavattvan nivartate /
15.2.[24]	atha vā vākyatrayam etat /
15.2.[25]	tat kathaṃ bhavati /
15.2.[26]	idam ucyate //
15.3.[1]	vakṣyante nārāśaṃsās sīdanti nārāśaṃsā iti /
15.3.[2]	teṣu nārāśaṃseṣu gaṇān vicakṣaṇañ ca parihāpya varjayitvā bhakṣayanti /
15.3.[3]	nanu trayāṇām api savanānān nārāśaṃsamantrā āmnāsyante /
15.3.[4]	satyam etat /
15.3.[5]	na tu tatra prauganiṣkevalyānuvartiṣu nārāśaṃseṣu mantravidhiḥ kariṣyate /
15.3.[6]	tadarthaṃ yatnaḥ kriyate /
15.3.[7]	kiṃ punas teṣām indav indrapītasyety anenaivoktamātravikāreṇa bhakṣaṇam /
15.3.[8]	ka evam āha /
15.3.[9]	nāto vākyād ayam artho niṣpannaḥ /
15.3.[10]	kas tarhi vākyārthaḥ /
15.3.[11]	gaṇān vicakṣaṇañ ca parihāpya ye mantrā āmnāsyante tair eva sarvanārāśaṃseṣu bhakṣaṇam iti /
15.3.[12]	tasmād avamair ūrvair ity ābhyām eva prauganiṣkevalyānuvartino 'pi nārāśaṃsān bhakṣayet /
15.3.[13]	evam apy asyārthasya nārāśaṃsādhikāra eva vaktavyasyātra vacanam anarthakam /
15.3.[14]	nānarthakam avekṣaṇāder bhakṣadharmasya cchandassavanopadeśasya ca nārāśaṃseṣu prāpaṇārthatvāt /
15.3.[15]	prāpiteṣu bhakṣadharmeṣu hotur upahavecchā nivartate /
15.3.[16]	na hi tatra hotur bhakṣaṇam //
15.3.[17]	na nārāśaṃsā anārāśaṃsāḥ /
15.3.[18]	anārāśaṃseṣu camaseṣv evam eva bhakṣayanti bhakṣamantre tu gaṇān parihāpya /
15.3.[19]	nanu gaṇavat savanamukhīyeṣv iti vākyena savanamukhīyeṣv eva gaṇavyavasthāpanād gaṇān ity anarthakam /
15.3.[20]	nānarthakaṃ gaṇebhyo 'nyasya savanamukhīyoktasya sarvasya vidher grahaṇārthatvāt /
15.3.[21]	ato 'trāpi cchandassavanopadeśaḥ prāpito bhavati /
15.3.[22]	atha vottarasmin savanadvaye savanamukhīyānām anārāśaṃseṣu ca gaṇān ity asmād vidher gaṇaparihāpaṇaṃ prasaktaṃ gaṇavat savanamukhīyeṣv iti vidhinā nivartyate /
15.3.[23]	atha vānārāśaṃseṣu ca gaṇān ity anena prākṛteṣu stotreṣu gaṇā nivartyante /
15.3.[24]	vaikṛteṣu tu vājapeyasāmādiṣu gaṇavān evāyaṃ mantraḥ prasajati /
15.3.[25]	tannivāraṇārthaṃ gaṇavat savanamukhīyeṣv iti gaṇaniyamaḥ kṛtaḥ /
15.3.[26]	na hy ekaṃ vidhānaṃ prakṛtivikṛtī samenānusarpati //
15.4.[1]	somaṃ bhakṣayitvendriyāṇi cakṣurghrāṇakarṇāsyāny anena mantreṇa saṃmṛśate /
15.4.[2]	atra saṃmarśanasyendriyāṇi prati guṇabhūtatvāt pratīndriyam āvartamānasya saha mantreṇāvṛttiḥ prāpnoti /
15.4.[3]	tannivṛttaye samaḥ prayogaḥ /
15.4.[4]	saṃmṛśate saha mṛśatīty arthaḥ /
15.4.[5]	evañ ca saṃmarśanam indriyāṇāṃ sahakṛtaṃ bhavati yat sakṛduktenaiva mantreṇa sarvāṇy ekavan mṛśyeran /
15.4.[6]	tasmāt sakṛd eva mantram uktvā tadante cakṣurādīni krameṇa saṃmraṣṭavyāni /
15.4.[7]	evañ ca kriyamāṇe gātrā gaṇān iti bahuvacanāntayor mantrapadayor arthasaṃpad bhavati //
15.5.[1]	anena yajuṣātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati //
15.6.[1]	sarvair bhakṣitañ camasam ādāya prastotātmano dakṣiṇasminn ūrau nidhāya tam etayā gāyatryāpyāyayati /
15.6.[2]	āpyāyayatīti pramattapaṭhitaś chāndaso vā /
15.6.[3]	camasaṃ mantreṇābhimṛśati /
15.6.[4]	tad āpyāyanaṃ bhavati /
15.6.[5]	etayety anarthakam /
15.6.[6]	nānarthakam ā pyāyasvety asyā ṛktvapratipādanārthatvāt /
15.6.[7]	kim atas sidhyati /
15.6.[8]	avasānam ardharce /
15.6.[9]	idam itthaṃ bhavatu /
15.6.[10]	gāyatryety ekāntenānarthakam /
15.6.[11]	nānarthakam asyāḥ prātassavanāpyāyanamantratve gāyatrītvasya hetutvapratipādanārthatvāt /
15.6.[12]	yathā devadattena vākyārthas samyaṅ nirūpito medhāvineti śrūyamāṇe samyaṅnirūpaṇasya medhāvitvaṃ hetur ukto 'vagamyate /
15.6.[13]	evam atrāpi draṣṭavyam /
15.6.[14]	iyañ cātra yuktiḥ /gāyatre prātassavane gāyatryāpyāyanam upapannam iti /
15.6.[15]	kiṃ punar asya prayojanam /
15.6.[16]	traiṣṭubhajāgatayoḥ prātassavanayos triṣṭubjagatyor āpyāyanamantratvena parigrahaḥ /
15.6.[17]	vyūḍhacchandasi hi dvādaśāhe caturthādiṣu ṣaṭsv ahassu savanānāñ chandāṃsi vyatiyanti /
15.6.[18]	tatra jāgatāni ca traiṣṭubhāni ca prātassavanāni /
15.6.[19]	ke punas triṣṭubjagatyau yābhyān tatrāpyāyanam /
15.6.[20]	ye uttarayor vakṣyete /
15.6.[21]	na hy etayor agrahaṇe 'nyayoś cānveṣaṇe kāraṇam /
15.6.[22]	tasmād yayā tṛtīyasavane tayā jāgateṣu prātassavaneṣv āpyāyanaṃ bhavati yayā mādhyandine savane tayā traiṣṭubheṣu /
15.6.[23]	adhikāreṇaivārthasiddheḥ prātassavana ity anarthakam /
15.6.[24]	nānarthakam adhastanasya vākyadvayasya savanatrayaviṣayatājñāpanārthatvāt /
15.6.[25]	atha vā bhakṣayitvendriyāṇīti bhakṣaṇānuvādād evāsyārthasya siddhatvād uttaravākyasya savanatrayaviṣayatāsmin vidhau prātassavanagrahaṇena jñāpyate //
15.7.[1]	tad āpyāyanam asarvabhakṣeṣu sarvabhakṣebhyo 'nyeṣu camaseṣu kartavyam /
15.7.[2]	uktam etat savanatrayārthaiṣā paribhāṣeti āpyāyanañ ca prāpitaṃ prātassavane /
15.7.[3]	uttarayoś ca prāpayiṣyate /
15.7.[4]	tat sarvacamaseṣu prasaktam anayā paribhāṣayā sarvabhakṣebhyo nivartyate /
15.7.[5]	te ca sarvabhakṣā ye nārāśaṃsatvāya na pariśeṣyante /
15.7.[6]	tasmāt savanamukhīyānām ājyamarutvatīyānuvartināñ camasānām āpyāyanam /
15.7.[7]	teṣāṃ hi nārāśaṃsatvena sādanam uttaratra vakṣyate //
15.7.[8]	etayā triṣṭubhā mādhyandine savane camasam āpyāyayati /
15.7.[9]	pūrveṇa gāyatrīgrahaṇena samaparihāran triṣṭubgrahaṇam /
15.7.[10]	tasmād gāyatrajāgateṣu mādhyandinasavaneṣu prātassavanatṛtīyasavanābhyām āpyāyanamantrāv ādeyau //
15.8.[1]	etayaiva dviruktayā tṛtīyasavana āpyāyayati //
15.9.[1]	sā dviruktā jagatī saṃpadyate /
15.9.[2]	jagatyāpyāyitaṃ bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ /
15.9.[3]	idaṃ vākyaṃ gāyatrīgrahaṇenaiva samaparihāram /
15.9.[4]	tasmād asya savanasya gāyatratāyān traiṣṭubhatāyāñ ca pūrvasmāt savanadvayād āpyāyanamantrāv ādeyau //
16.1.[1]	āpyāyitāś camasās sīdanti nārāśaṃsāḥ nārāśaṃsanāmāno bhūtvā /
16.1.[2]	camasānāṃ sādanan nārāśaṃsasaṃjñā cobhayam apy anena vākyena kriyate /
16.1.[3]	atha vā dve evaite vākye //
16.2.[1]	ṛtuyājā nāma ke cit somayāgāḥ /
16.2.[2]	tair adhvaryavo vyāpriyante //
16.3-5.[1]	asti śastram ājyan nāma /
16.3-5.[2]	tasmiñ śaste nārāśaṃsān āgatān anena mantreṇa bhakṣayanti //
16.6.[1]	ūrvais te pitṛbhir ity anena mādhyandine savane nārāśaṃsān bhakṣayanti /
16.6.[2]	atrānukto 'pi cchandassavananirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ /
16.6.[3]	tasya kāraṇaṃ pūrvoktam //
16.8.[1]	ṣoḍaśini stotre yo grahaś camaso vā yaś ca rātres somaḥ paryāyeṣu tam anuṣṭupchandasa ity etatpadavikṛtena mantreṇa bhakṣayanti /
16.8.[2]	sannihitasyāpi nārāśaṃsamantrasya liṅgavirodhād yo 'sāv indav indrapītasyeti tārtīyasavaniko mantras sa evāyañ chando vikṛtya vidhīyate /
16.8.[3]	liṅgaṃ hi kramād balavat /
16.8.[4]	evaṃ bhakṣamantropadeśārthaṃ kṛtaprasaṅgasya ṣoḍaśino 'nyad apy aṅgajātam asthāne 'pi granthalāghavārthaṃ vidhāsyate //
16.9.[1]	suvarṇam anyo'nyasmai saṃpradāya saṃpradāya ṣoḍaśinā stuvanti /
16.9.[2]	hiraṇyena ṣoḍaśinam adhvaryur upākaroti /
16.9.[3]	tad yo yadā gāyati sa tadā dhārayet nodgātaiva sarvadety evamartham idam ucyate /
16.9.[4]	nidhane tu prādhānyād udgātaiva dhārayet //
16.10.[1]	ṣoḍaśini gīyamāne 'śva upatiṣṭhate samīpe tiṣṭhati /
16.10.[2]	sāmyekṣyāyety arthavādaḥ /
16.10.[3]	śrutivākyam eva hīdam /
16.10.[4]	kaḥ punar arthavādārthaḥ /
16.10.[5]	ime brūmahe /
16.10.[6]	sāmyenekṣāsya na vaiṣamyeneti vā sāmye 'kṣāṇīndriyāṇy asya tiṣṭhantīti vālukkalpanayā sāmyekṣas sākṣī bhavati /
16.10.[7]	tasya bhāvas sāmyekṣyam /
16.10.[8]	tasya sāmyekṣyāya sākṣitvāyety arthaḥ /
16.10.[9]	atha vā pūrveṇa nirvacanena prajāpatis sāmyekṣaḥ /
16.10.[10]	tasya hi sāmyenaiva sarvabhūteṣv īkṣā buddhir vartate na pakṣapātena /
16.10.[11]	tasmād aśva upatiṣṭhate prajāpatibhāvāyeti kalpyam /
16.10.[12]	dṛśyate cārthavādeṣu prajāpatir aśva iti //
16.11-12.[1]	bhakṣārtham āhṛtaṃ ṣoḍaśigraham anayarcāvekṣate /
16.11-12.[2]	idam avekṣaṇaṃ bhakṣaṇāṅgam bhakṣaṇañ ca sarveṣām uttarasmin vākye vakṣyāmaḥ /
16.11-12.[3]	tasmād idam ekavacanānvitam apy avekṣaṇaṃ sarva eva kuryuḥ /
16.11-12.[4]	bhakṣaṇāṅgatvād eva ca yadā bhakṣaṇārtham ādadīraṃs tadaivāvekṣeran //
16.13-15.[1]	nārāśaṃsavākyād anuvartamānaṃ bhakṣayantīti vidhānaṃ hiraṇyasaṃpradānādividhitrayavicchinnaṃ punar evāthaśabdenādhikriyate /
16.13-15.[2]	harivatīṣv ṛkṣv indra juṣasva pra vahety etāsu ṣoḍaśī yadi syāt tatrānaya rcā ṣoḍaśigrahaṃ bhakṣayanti /
16.13-15.[3]	nanv avekṣaṇa ekavacanadarśanād bhakṣayatīty adhyāhartavyam /
16.13-15.[4]	naitad yuktam /
16.13-15.[5]	prakṛtānuvartanena sidhyati /
16.13-15.[6]	nādhyāhārakāraṇam /
16.13-15.[7]	aṅgenaiva ca pradhānasyānuvṛttir yuktā na pradhānenāṅgasya /
16.13-15.[8]	tasmād atra bhakṣayantīty evānuvartayitavyam /
16.13-15.[9]	avadac ca śaunakaṣ ṣoḍaśibhakṣiṇo gaṇayan trayaś chandogā iti /
16.13-15.[10]	nanu homābhiṣavavaṣaṭkārasamākhyānāṃ bhakṣakāraṇānām atrābhāvāt sattrārtham idam udgātṝṇāṃ ṣoḍaśibhakṣaṇañ codyata iti vaktuṃ ghaṭate /
16.13-15.[11]	naivaṃ ghaṭate /
16.13-15.[12]	yady apy uktāni bhakṣakāraṇāni na santi śrutir evātra kāraṇaṃ bhavati /
16.13-15.[13]	asti hi ṣoḍaśibrāhmaṇe yasmāj jāta ityādi /
16.13-15.[14]	tasmāt prakṛtyartham evedañ codyate na sattrārtham /
16.13-15.[15]	tiṣṭhatu tāvad bhakṣaṇam /
16.13-15.[16]	avekṣaṇasyaiva harivatīnimitto 'yaṃ mantrāntaravidhir iti kuto na gṛhyate /
16.13-15.[17]	asya mantrasyārthavipattir mā bhūd iti /
16.13-15.[18]	na hy avekṣaṇāṅgaṃ śaknoti bhakṣitum /
16.13-15.[19]	asati ca bhakṣaṇavidhāv avekṣaṇam anarthakaṃ bhavet /
16.13-15.[20]	tasmād bhakṣayantīty evānuvartate nāvekṣata iti /
16.13-15.[21]	kva punaṣ ṣoḍaśī harivatīr vyabhicarati /
16.13-15.[22]	śakvarīṣu ṣoḍaśisāma kurvītetyādiṣu kāmyavidhāneṣu prakṛtau vikṛtau ca datvatrirātrādau/ kena mantreṇa tatra grahabhakṣaḥ /
16.13-15.[23]	uktam etad anuṣṭupchandasa iti ṣoḍaśinīti /
16.13-15.[24]	avekṣaṇamantras tu yasmāj jāta ity ayam eva //
16.16.[1]	yas somo rāthantarasya sandhes taṃ bṛhatīcchandasa iti vikṛtacchandaḥpadena tārtīyasavanikena vā mantreṇeṣṭayajuṣas ta ity anena vā bhakṣayanti /
16.16.[2]	na cāyam iyān eva mantra iṣṭayajuṣas ta iti /
16.16.[3]	paraśākhāgatasya mahato mantrasya pratīkam etad gṛhyate /
16.16.[4]	itthaṃ punar grahaṇe ko doṣa uktamātra evāyaṃ mantra iti /
16.16.[5]	eṣa khalu doṣaḥ /
16.16.[6]	aparipūrṇārtham idaṃ mantravākyaṃ bhavet /
16.16.[7]	na hi kaś cid artha iṣṭayajuṣas ta ity etāvatā samāpyate /
16.16.[8]	tatra sākāṅkṣam evedaṃ padadvayam avatiṣṭheta /
16.16.[9]	tasmāt paraśākhāgatasyaivedam ādigrahaṇaṃ kriyate /
16.16.[10]	kutaḥ punaḥ kāraṇāt paraśākhāgatān mahan me 'voca ityādīn mahāmantrān paṭhann imam evācāryo na paṭhati /
16.16.[11]	santi vidhiviśeṣāḥ parato 'py asmābhir grāhyā iti jñāpanārtham /
16.16.[12]	tataś ca prajāpatiṃ manasā dhyāyāt tūṣṇīṃhomeṣu sarvatrety evamādīnāṃ grahaṇaṃ sidhyati //
16.17-19.[1]	mānasasya stotrasya yas somas tam anayor ekena mantreṇa manasā bhakṣayanti /
16.17-19.[2]	manasā mantrañ japtvā manasaiva bhakṣayanti /
16.17-19.[3]	bhakṣyate 'smābhis soma iti smaranti /
16.17-19.[4]	na tatra hi soma eva paramārthena vidyate kva bhakṣaṇam //
16.20.[1]	vājapeyasāmny atiriktoktheṣu ca yas somas tam aticchandasa ity ūhyacchandasā tṛtīyasavanamantreṇa bhakṣayanti //
16.21.[1]	pūrvayor dvayos savanayor dvir nārāśaṃsās sīdanti /
16.21.[2]	katham idam abhipreyate /
16.21.[3]	kim ekasmin savane sakṛd anyasminn api sakṛd ity eva dvis sīdanty utāho dvir ekaikasmin /
16.21.[4]	kutas saṃśayaḥ /
16.21.[5]	ubhayathā loke dṛśyamānatvāt /
16.21.[6]	yathā dviś śivadāso bhuṅkte devarātakṛṣṇarātagṛhayor ity ukte sakṛt sakṛd ekaikasmin bhujyate /
16.21.[7]	dvis sumanaso vāsyantām prāvārakambalayor ity ukte dvir dvir vāsyante /
16.21.[8]	atra brūmaḥ /
16.21.[9]	kāmam ubhayathāpi loke bhavatu /
16.21.[10]	atra tv evam eva gṛhṇīmaḥ /
16.21.[11]	dvir ekasmin dvir evānyasmin sīdanti /
16.21.[12]	yadi sakṛd ekaikasminn iti gṛhyeta dvirgrahaṇam anarthakaṃ syāt /
16.21.[13]	atha vā sīdanti nārāśaṃsā ity ato vākyāt prātassavane tadāvṛdatideśāc ca mādhyandine sakṛtsakṛtsādanasya siddhatvāt sarvam evedaṃ vākyam anarthakaṃ syāt /
16.21.[14]	dviḥ punar ekaikasminn iti gṛhyamāṇe nātra kiñ cid apy anarthakam /
16.21.[15]	nanv asminn api pakṣe savanamukhīyaśeṣāṇāṃ savanadvaye 'pi pūrvoktenaiva prakāreṇa siddhatvāt sādanasyājyamarutvatīyānuvartinām eva vidheyatvād dvirgrahaṇam anarthakam /
16.21.[16]	nānarthakaṃ pūrvayos savanayor nārāśaṃsās sīdantīty ukte savanayor anayor ye bhakṣaśeṣās teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ sādanasya prasajato nivṛttyarthatvāt /
16.21.[17]	tasmāt sādhūktaṃ dvir dvir ekaikasminn iti /
16.21.[18]	nanu punar bahukṛtvas somo bhakṣyate /
16.21.[19]	katithānāṃ bhakṣaśeṣāṇāṃ sādanam etac codyate /
16.21.[20]	prathamadvitīyānām iti brūmaḥ /
16.21.[21]	na hy asati kāraṇe prathamātikramaṇaṃ yujyate /
16.21.[22]	evañ ced anenaiva gatārthatvāt sīdanti nārāśaṃsā iti pūrvaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
16.21.[23]	nānarthakam ṛtuyājebhyaḥ pūrvan nārāśaṃsās sīdantīti kriyākramavidhānārthatvāt /
16.21.[24]	atha vā prathamanārāśaṃsasādanavidhānārtham evedaṃ vākyaṃ bhavatu sīdanti nārāśaṃsā iti /
16.21.[25]	yac cedaṃ vākyaṃ dviḥ pūrvayor iti tad apy asati dviśśabde keṣāñ cin nārāśaṃsānāṃ sādanamātraṃ vidadhyāt /
16.21.[26]	tatra naivedam avagamyetaitāvatithānām iti /
16.21.[27]	tadavagamanārthan dviśśabdaḥ prayujyate /
16.21.[28]	ko 'bhiprāyaḥ /
16.21.[29]	ayam ucyate /
16.21.[30]	ya ete śabdā dvis trir ityādayas teṣām ayaṃ svabhāvo yad ekasminn eva dravye kriyāyā āvṛttim avagamayati /
16.21.[31]	tatrāyan dviśśabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ pūrvan nārāśaṃsībhūya sannānām eva somānān dvitīyaṃ sādanam avagamayatītyartho bhavati /
16.21.[32]	yathā loke prātar eva devadattasya bhojanam ājñāpya bhuktavati tasmin punar gṛhapatir vadati dvir devadatto bhojayitavya iti /
16.21.[33]	na caivaṃ śrutvā punar eva dvir bhojayanti /
16.21.[34]	dvitīyabhojanaparam eva vacanaṃ manyamānās sāyamāśam asmai dadati /
16.21.[35]	evam anenāpi vākyena dvitīyam eva nārāśaṃsānāṃ sādanaṃ vidhīyate nāpūrvaṃ sādanadvayam /
16.21.[36]	tasmāt sādhūktaṃ prathamadvitīyānāṃ sādanam iti //
16.22.[1]	tṛtīyasavane sakṛn nārāśaṃsās sīdanti /
16.22.[2]	prathamata eva //
16.23.[1]	atha nārāśaṃsasādanānantaram imaṃ saṃpraiṣaṃ karmakarān uddiśya prastotāha /
16.23.[2]	kathaṃ prastotā /
16.23.[3]	kim idam idānīm asad anādiṣṭakartṛkam udgāteti /
16.23.[4]	atra brūmaḥ /
16.23.[5]	prastotṛkartṛkastotrāvayavasaṃkhyānakaraṇabhūtaudumbarakhaṇḍopadhānārthavastralābhopāyatvād ayaṃ saṃpraiṣaḥ prastotraiva vaktavyaḥ /
16.23.[6]	yo hi pradhānasya kartā tasyaivāṅgānām apy anādeśe kartṛtvaṃ yuktam /
16.23.[7]	nanv avayavasaṃkhyānam api stotrāṅgam /
16.23.[8]	tataś coktenaiva krameṇa saṃpraiṣo 'py eṣa stotrāṅgaṃ bhavati /
16.23.[9]	tatrāṅgapradhānayor ekakartṛtvāśraye sarvais stotrakāribhir asya saṃpraiṣasya vacanaṃ prapnoti /
16.23.[10]	āheti tv ekavacanaśruter aniyamena trayāṇām ekena niyamahetor vāsamākhyānād udgātraiva /
16.23.[11]	satyam /
16.23.[12]	evaṃ prāpnoti yady eṣa saṃpraiṣa stotrāṅgaṃ bhavet /
16.23.[13]	na caiṣa stotrāvayavasaṃkhyānasyaiva prathamato 'ṅgabhāvād upalabdhaprayojanas stotrāṅgatām ākāṅkṣate /
16.23.[14]	kasmāt punaḥ prastotaiva stotriyāḥ parisañcaṣṭe /
16.23.[15]	yasmād ayaṃ madhyamām adhvaryave hotrādibhyaś cottamāṃ prāha tasmād etaj jñāyate prastotaivāṣāṃ parisaṃkhyāteti /
16.23.[16]	ya eva hi yāni kāni cit saṃkhyātavān sa evaivaṃ vadituṃ śaknoty etāvantīmāny etāvatitham eṣv etad iti /
16.23.[17]	tasmād etan niścetavyam /
16.23.[18]	prastotaiva stotriyāḥ parisañcaṣṭe /
16.23.[19]	sa evātra saṃpreṣyatīti /
16.23.[20]	evaṃ saṃpreṣitāḥ parikarmiṇo vāsa āharanti /
16.23.[21]	tad āstāvamadhye vistṛṇāti yathā vakṣyamāṇā viṣṭutayas tasminn upadhīyeran /
16.23.[22]	evaṃ hi vaiṣṭutam iti vāsaso 'bhidhānaṃ saṃpraiṣadṛṣṭam upapannaṃ bhavati /
16.23.[23]	viṣṭutīnām idaṃ vaiṣṭutam iti //
16.24-26.[1]	ayam arthavādo vāsasa stutyarthaḥ /
16.24-26.[2]	tasyāyam arthaḥ kathyate /
16.24-26.[3]	vistīrṇaṃ punaḥ punas stomapūraṇārtham abhyasyamānaṃ stavanaṃ viṣṭāvaḥ /
16.24-26.[4]	stotrāṇāṃ mahattvajanananimittatvāt sāmnaś śrīr bhavati /
16.24-26.[5]	vāsaś ca śrīr eva bhavati śobhākāritvāt /
16.24-26.[6]	tatraivam arthayojanā /
16.24-26.[7]	yataś śrīr evaiṣā sāmnāṃ yad viṣṭāvaḥ vāsaś ca śrīr eva tasmād viṣṭāvārthaṃ vāso ya āharanti te śriyam eva bhūyasīm asmin sāmni dadhatīti /
16.24-26.[8]	ayam abhiprāyaḥ /
16.24-26.[9]	pṛthag api saṃmatayoḥ parasparasaṃgamo mahīyasīṃ saṃmatiṃ vidadhāti maṇikanakayor iva ca jñānakarmaṇor iva ceti //
16.27-29.[1]	audumbaraviṭapāḥ prādeśapramāṇasaṃmitā viṣṭutayo bhavanti /
16.27-29.[2]	karaṇasādhanaś cātra viṣṭutiśabdaḥ /
16.27-29.[3]	viṣṭūyata ābhir iti /
16.27-29.[4]	nanu sāmabhir viṣṭūyate /
16.27-29.[5]	satyam etat /
16.27-29.[6]	yady api tu paramārthato nāsāṃ viṣṭāvakaraṇatvam asti viṣṭāvasaṃkhyābhiḥ paricchidyata ity aupacārikam asty eva /
16.27-29.[7]	tad atrāśrīyate /
16.27-29.[8]	nanu viṣṭutiśabdasya strīliṅgatvād audumbaryaḥ prādeśamātrya iti prāpnoti /
16.27-29.[9]	na prāpnoti /
16.27-29.[10]	udumbarakhaṇḍānāṃ hi prādeśamātrāṇāṃ satāṃ viṣṭutibhāvo 'tra vidhīyate /
16.27-29.[11]	tasmād ittham eva sādhu /
16.27-29.[12]	arthavādo vākyaśeṣaḥ /
16.27-29.[13]	tasyāyam arthaḥ /
16.27-29.[14]	ūrg ity ayaṃ śabdo rasavacanaḥ /
16.27-29.[15]	atra lakṣaṇayā rasavad vacanaṃ kalpyate /
16.27-29.[16]	vai iti nipāto hetau /
16.27-29.[17]	tatraivaṃ yojanā /
16.27-29.[18]	yato rasavad annam udumbaras tasmād udumbarāvayavā viṣṭutitvenopādīyante /
16.27-29.[19]	tasya rasavata evānnādyasyāvarodhāyeti //
16.30-31.[1]	sarvastotreṣu tṛṇadvayam anyad vā stotram adhvaryur āharati /
16.30-31.[2]	tat tasya svasminn eva tantre vihitam /
16.30-31.[3]	ācāryeṇa ca stotraṃ pratigṛhya ... japatīti vidadhatā sarveṣv āvartipavamāneṣu stotram astīty avagamitam /
16.30-31.[4]	tasyaivaṃ siddhasyāstāvaṃ praty āhriyamāṇasya stotrasya prapadanamārgo 'yaṃ vidhīyate /
16.30-31.[5]	stotrāharaṇan tv anūdyate /
16.30-31.[6]	stotram adhvaryur dakṣiṇena hotur dhiṣṇyan dvir āharati /
16.30-31.[7]	idānīm eva vakṣyati catvāri stotrāṇi /
16.30-31.[8]	teṣu dvayor ayaṃ stotrāharaṇamārgaḥ kathitaḥ /
16.30-31.[9]	dvayos tu vakṣyate //
16.30-31.[10]	uttareṇa hotur dhiṣṇyan dvis stotram āharati pratiprasthātā /
16.30-31.[11]	sa hi tatrādhvaryur iṣyate /
16.30-31.[12]	ājyeṣv ayaṃ mārgo bhavatu pṛṣṭheṣu ca /
16.30-31.[13]	katham anyeṣu stotreṣu /
16.30-31.[14]	idaṃ vadāmaḥ /
16.30-31.[15]	dvāv etau sañcārau sadasaḥ /
16.30-31.[16]	dakṣiṇena hotur dhiṣṇyam eka uttareṇaikaḥ /
16.30-31.[17]	ekeṣāṃ hi vacanam antareṇa hotur maitrāvaruṇasya ca dhiṣṇyāv adhiṣṇyānāṃ visaṃsthitasañcāra iti /
16.30-31.[18]	anyeṣāṃ punar athaiṣāṃ visaṃsthitasañcāro 'ntareṇa hotuś ca dhiṣṇyaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaś ca ye dhiṣṇyā iti /
16.30-31.[19]	tatrāsmākam avacane 'pi dvayor ekas sañcāraḥ pratistotram aniyamena prasajati /
16.30-31.[20]	tatra pūrvayor ājyayor adhvaryukartṛkatvāt stotrāharaṇasya dvāraś ca dakṣiṇabhāgenādhvaryoḥ prapannatvād dakṣiṇam eva sañcāram ṛjutvāt pūrvaṃ vākyan niyacchati /
16.30-31.[21]	uttarayoś ca pratiprasthātṛkartṛkatvād uttarabhāgena ca tasya prapannatvād uttaram api vākyam ṛjutvād evottaraṃ sañcāran niyacchati /
16.30-31.[22]	dṛṣṭārthapravartitatvāc cāyaṃ sañcāraniyamas sarveṣv api stotreṣūpādīyate /
16.30-31.[23]	tasmāt sarvatrāpi yad adhvaryus stotram āharati tad dakṣiṇena hotur dhiṣṇyam āharati yat pratiprasthātā tad uttareṇa /
16.30-31.[24]	evam avakraṃ vartma bhavati //
16.32.[1]	ta udgātāraḥ pañcadaśastomenāgnidevatākenājyena stuvate /
16.32.[2]	yathāstomaṃ vā /
16.32.[3]	vāśabdo hetau /
16.32.[4]	yathāstomaṃ hi stotavyam ity arthaḥ /
16.32.[5]	pañcadaśāny ājyāni bhavantītyevamādibhiś śrutivākyair eva stomā vihitāḥ /
16.32.[6]	tadapekṣayā yathāstomam ity uktam /
16.32.[7]	ayam abhiprāyaḥ /
16.32.[8]	śrutivihitastomaparigrahārtham anenājyena pañcadaśena stuvata iti /
16.32.[9]	tata idam uktaṃ bhavati /
16.32.[10]	sarvastotreṣu śrautā eva stomā grāhyā iti /
16.32.[11]	pratistotraṃ hi stomavacane granthasya garimā prasajati /
16.32.[12]	atha vā te pañcadaśenāgneyenājyena stuvata ity etāvataiva vākyena sarvatra śrautā eva stomā ity upalakṣyante /
16.32.[13]	nāgneyasyaiva pañcadaśatvaṃ vivakṣyate /
16.32.[14]	na hy asti kāraṇam asyaiva stomo vidheyo nānyeṣām iti /
16.32.[15]	nanv asminn anyeṣu ca stotreṣu śrutitas stomāḥ prāptāḥ /
16.32.[16]	kim ataḥ /
16.32.[17]	ata etad bhavati /
16.32.[18]	anyebhyaś śrautastomanivartanārtham etad vacanam iti /
16.32.[19]	atra vadāmaḥ /
16.32.[20]	asty eveyaṃ parisaṃkhyā nāma /
16.32.[21]	iha tu sā pañcadaśāny ājyāni bhavantīty evamādiśrutivirodhaprasaṅgān na gṛhyate /
16.32.[22]	tasmād upalakṣaṇārtham evedaṃ vacanan na parisaṃkhyānārtham /
16.32.[23]	nanu śrutisiddhānāṃ stomānām upalakṣaṇāpy anarthikaiva /
16.32.[24]	yady evaṃ sarveyam anarthikā daśādhyāyī saṃvṛttā /
16.32.[25]	asyāṃ hi śrutisiddham eva kathyate /
16.32.[26]	vyākhyānādāv eva cedam uditaṃ śrautā eva vidhayas sūtrair anukramyanta iti /
16.32.[27]	yadi ca kalpasūtrāṇi śrutyasiddham arthaṃ vidadhyuḥ na prāmāṇyam upalabheran /
16.32.[28]	ataś śrutisiddhakathanam atra na doṣāya /
16.32.[29]	guṇāyaiva tad bhavati /
16.32.[30]	evam anena vākyena śrutita eva stomānāṃ grahaṇam avagamitam /
16.32.[31]	stomaprasa:gena tu kva cit saṃśaye stomasya niścayopāyaḥ kathyate yathāstomaṃ veti /
16.32.[32]	stomaśabdo 'tra stomakalpam upalakṣayati /
16.32.[33]	vāśabdo 'vadhāraṇāyām /
16.32.[34]	ayam arthaḥ /
16.32.[35]	yathā stomakalpam eva stomā grāhyā iti /
16.32.[36]	stomakalpasya śrutyā virodhaśaṅkāyām idam ucyate /
16.32.[37]	yathāmuṣya vyomna ekāhasya śrutau stomavidhiḥ sa saptadaśo bhavatīti tasyaikaviṃśa ārbhavaḥ pavamāno bhavaty agniṣṭomasāma veti ca /
16.32.[38]	stomakalpe tu saptadaśasyaikaviṃśam agniṣṭomasāmeti /
16.32.[39]	nanv atra yathā stomakalpam eva gṛhyamāṇe śruteḥ prāmāṇyaṃ hīyeta /
16.32.[40]	atra brūmaḥ /
16.32.[41]	śrutyarthasyaiva parigrahārtham idaṃ yathāstomam ity ucyate /
16.32.[42]	ayam abhiprāyaḥ /
16.32.[43]	pūrvoktām ārbhavasyaikaviṃśatāṃ vāśabdena nivartyāgniṣṭomasāmna ekaviṃśatvaṃ siddhāntatvena śrutāv apy upāttam iti /
16.32.[44]	na hi śrutiviruddham ācāryaḥ kalpayati /
16.32.[45]	atha vā śrutivihitānāṃ stomānām anyathābhāvo 'pi prakṛtāv evāsti /
16.32.[46]	vakṣyati hy āgnicitike saptadaśo madhyandinaḥ pañcadaśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭham iti /
16.32.[47]	tasyāpi parigrahārthaṃ yathāstomaṃ vety ucyate //
16.33.[1]	apavamāneṣv ayaṃ kramaḥ /
16.33.[2]	yad uta stotrānantaraṃ śastraṃ tatas somejyā tatas somabhakṣaṇam iti /
16.33.[3]	tad etad api bhakṣaṇānantaram ucyate /
16.33.[4]	atha mitrāvaruṇadevatākenājyena stuvate /
16.33.[5]	athaindreṇa /
16.33.[6]	athaindrāgnena //
16.34.[1]	savanaśabdas somābhiṣavam abhidadhat tatsahacaritaṃ kriyākalāpaṃ sakalam api lakṣaṇayāvagamayati /
16.34.[2]	sūyate 'smin soma iti vādhikaraṇasādhanas san saṃjñātvenāsmin karmakalāpe pravartate /
16.34.[3]	tasyātra prātaśśabdo viśeṣakaḥ /
16.34.[4]	tat prātassavanam itthaṃ santiṣṭhate /
16.34.[5]	savanāntarārambhād evaitatsavanasamāptijñāpananiṣpatter idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
16.34.[6]	nānarthakaṃ yadarthan devayajanabhūmiḥ prapannā tat prātassavanaṃ yatas santiṣṭhate tasmāt tato niṣkrāmeyur ity etadarthatvāt /
16.34.[7]	nanūttarasavanādau prapadanam api prātassavanataḥ prāpnoti /
16.34.[8]	kim ataḥ /
16.34.[9]	ata etad bhavati /
16.34.[10]	niṣkramaṇam arthasiddham iti /
16.34.[11]	satyam etat /
16.34.[12]	kin tv arthagate niṣkramaṇa āśrīyamāṇe yena kena cit pathā niṣkrāmeyuḥ /
16.34.[13]	vacanāvagamite punar yad vācanikaṃ sadaḥprapadane vartma tenaiva niṣkramaṇam api sidhyati /
16.34.[14]	tasmāt pradakṣiṇam audumbarīṃ parītya sadaso 'parayā dvārā niṣkramyāgnīdhrīyam uttareṇa gatvā cātvālotkarāv antareṇa vrajitvā tato yathārthaṃ gaccheyuḥ //
17.1.[1]	etayaiva prātassavane vihitayaivāvṛtā krameṇa mādhyandinam api savanaṃ prasiddham /
17.1.[2]	yā prātassavanasyetikartavyatā saivāsyāpi savanasyātidiśyate /
17.1.[3]	uttarais tu vākyair viśeṣo vakṣyate /
17.1.[4]	kimartham idam etayaivāvṛteti vacanam /
17.1.[5]	prātassavanadharmāṇām atra prāpaṇārtham evam idamartham evaitat /
17.1.[6]	evañ ced evam eveti vaktavyam /
17.1.[7]	tāvatāpy ayam arthas sidhyati yathānyatrāpy atidiśyata evam eva prāg vartamāna evam evāparāhṇa upasadi saṃsthitāyām iti /
17.1.[8]	atra brūmaḥ /
17.1.[9]	yady evam evety avakṣyata yad atra vacanena nāpavadiṣyate tat sarvam avikṛtam eva prātassavanikaṃ karmātrāpi prāsaṅkṣyat /
17.1.[10]	iṣyate tv atra keṣāñ cit karmaṇāṃ kramavikāraḥ keṣāñ cid akaraṇañ ca /
17.1.[11]	tatsiddhyartham etayaivāvṛtety uktam /
17.1.[12]	kin tat sarvam iyatā sidhyati /
17.1.[13]	kas sandehaḥ /
17.1.[14]	itthaṃ hi gṛhyate /
17.1.[15]	āvṛtā krameṇa nyāyeneti /
17.1.[16]	tatra nyāyāvalambanena kāni cit karmāṇi na kriyante kriyate ca keṣāñcit kramaḥ /
17.1.[17]	kathaṃ punar atra prayogaḥ /
17.1.[18]	ime vadāmaḥ /
17.1.[19]	ādita eva kṛtayajñopavītācamanakā vediṃ prapadyerann asminn eva cāvasare vedyākramaṇādi sada..upaveśanāntaṃ karma kuryuḥ /
17.1.[20]	kuta idam evaṃ kriyate /
17.1.[21]	nyāyād iti brūmaḥ /
17.1.[22]	idaṃ hi karma yasmin kāle prātassavane kṛtan na tasmin kāle 'tra kartuṃ śakyate /
17.1.[23]	pavamānena stutvā kṛtam etat prātassavane /
17.1.[24]	atra tu stute dadhigharmeṇa carantīti vakṣyamāṇatvāt tasmāt sthānād avagacchati /
17.1.[25]	evañ caivābhipremo vayam /
17.1.[26]	kṛtavedyākramaṇādipadārthajātair eva prātassavanavad atrāpi sadaḥ praveṣṭavyam iti /
17.1.[27]	tathā parair apy uktaṃ dhiṣṇyān upasthāya sadaḥ prasarpantīti /
17.1.[28]	vakṣyate ca sadasi pavamānena stuvata iti /
17.1.[29]	tata idam arthasiddham /
17.1.[30]	prāk pavamānād avaśyam atra vedyākramaṇādi kāryam iti /
17.1.[31]	evañ ced dhavirdhānaprapadanād ūrdhvam etat kartavyaṃ prātassavanakālasyāsattaye /
17.1.[32]	satyam /
17.1.[33]	evam api prāpnoti /
17.1.[34]	ittham eva sahakāribhis tv ādita evāsyeṣyamāṇatvād asmākam api tṛtīyasavane tathaiva vakṣyamāṇatvād ittham eva niścinumahe /
17.1.[35]	ādāv eva vedyākramaṇādi kṛtvā sadasy upaviśeyur iti /
17.1.[36]	tato 'bhiṣavakāle dakṣiṇena hotur dhiṣṇyaṃ sadaso niṣkramyādhvaryupathena gatvā havirdhānaṃ prapadyeran /
17.1.[37]	tato havirdhānābhimarśanādiḥ pravṛtahomāntaḥ karmakalāpaḥ pratāyate /
17.1.[38]	na tv atra viśvarūpāṇāṃ vacanaṃ pravartate /
17.1.[39]	tasya kāraṇaṃ pūrvam evoktaṃ na cātra viśvarūpāgānaṃ kartavyam /
17.1.[40]	yat pūrvoktaṃ devasomabhakṣaṇādivad idaṃ mantavyam iti tasyedaṃ phalam /
17.1.[41]	devasomabhakṣaṇādivad asmin savane viśvarūpāgānasyāpy akaraṇam /
17.1.[42]	kutaḥ punar devasomabhakṣaṇādīnām atrākaraṇam /
17.1.[43]	yasmād etāni śrutāv eva coditāni na sūtre tasmād atraitāni nātidiśyante /
17.1.[44]	yad eva hi prātassavane vihitavān ācāryas tad eva sannidhānād etayety atideṣṭuṃ śakyate na sarvaṃ prātassavanāṅgam /
17.1.[45]	idamartham eva ca devasomabhakṣaṇādīnām ācāryeṇākalpanaṃ yad eṣām atrākaraṇam /
17.1.[46]	tasmād itthaṃ mantavyam /
17.1.[47]	yāni śrutita āgatāni prātassavanāṅgāni tāny atra na pravarteran /
17.1.[48]	tadvad bhāvapratipādanād viśvarūpāgānañ ceti /
17.1.[49]	kiñ ca viśvarūpāgānasyātrābhāvaṃ sahakāripratyayo 'py avagamayati /
17.1.[50]	kva u khalu vāsatīvarasya stotrabhaktir bhavati śastrabhaktiś ceti /
17.1.[51]	viśvarūpā u hāsya stotrabhaktir bhavati prātaranuvāka u śastrabhaktir iti /
17.1.[52]	tatra grahatvena śastratayā copāttayor vāsatīvaragrahaprātaranuvākayor anāvartamānatvād asyāpi stotratvenopāttasya tathātvam eva ghaṭate /
17.1.[53]	tasmād avasthitam etat /
17.1.[54]	nātra viśvarūpāṇāṃ pravṛttir iti /
17.1.[55]	atra ca sadasi pavamānagānasya vidhāsyamānatvāt pravṛtahomānantaraṃ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya pratyaṇcas sarpanti tadā cādhvaryum anumantrayeta //
17.2.[1]	saṃgatās santatā vā prasṛpya sadasi mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvate /
17.2.[2]	saṃprasṛpyeti bhavitavye saṃprasarpyeti cchāndaso guṇaḥ /
17.2.[3]	ācāryeṇa vā saṃprasṛpyety eva kathitaṃ pramādād adhyetṛbhir evaṃ kṛtam /
17.2.[4]	atha vā ṇijantād dhātor ayaṃ pratyayaḥ /
17.2.[5]	udgātṝṇām evedam ucyate /
17.2.[6]	ātmabhis samam adhvaryvādīn prasarpyeti /
17.2.[7]	evañ ca sarpaṇastavanayos samānakartṛkatā śrūyamāṇā kiñ cid api na vihanyate /
17.2.[8]	itarathā hi ye sarpanti tais sarvais stūyamānatvād vihanyeta //
17.3.[1]	sāmārthaṃ sāmārthaṃ hiṃkurvanti /
17.3.[2]	sāmnas sāmnaḥ purastād dhiṃkurvantīty arthaḥ /
17.3.[3]	atra śrutāv āmahīyave vaṣaṭkāro vihitaḥ prathamastotriyāyām eva cāvadhāritaḥ /
17.3.[4]	vaṣaṭkuryād vauṣāḍ bhūmī o dadā itīti /
17.3.[5]	tasmād o vauṣāḍ bhū iti gāyet //
17.4.[1]	pavamānena stute dadhigharmasamākhyena haviṣādhvaryvādayo vyāpriyante //
17.5.[1]	dadhigharmānantaraṃ pāśukasavanīyaiḥ puroḍāśaiś caranti //
17.5.[2]	atha somena caranti //
17.6.[1]	some bhakṣite sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu dakṣiṇāsaṃbaddhāni yajūṃṣy adhvaryur juhoti //
17.7.[1]	dvādaśaṃ śataṃ gavān dadyād ekaviṃśatiprabhṛti vā yathopapādam iti jyotiṣṭomasya dakṣiṇāś śākhāntare vihitāḥ /
17.7.[2]	tā gāḥ parikarmiṇo dakṣiṇāpathena nayanty upājanti //
17.8.[1]	tāsāṃ gavān dakṣiṇāpathena nīyamānānāṃ yā gauḥ prathamā purastāt prasthitā tām ātreyāya dattvā tato brahmaṇe dakṣiṇā nayanti dadati /
17.8.[2]	brahmārthāṃ vā dakṣiṇān tatpradiṣṭan deśan nayanti /
17.8.[3]	hiraṇyadānam ātreyāya śrutau dṛśyate sarveṣu lokeṣu jyotir dhatte ya evaṃ vidvān atrihiraṇyan dadātīti /
17.8.[4]	tasmād gor anantaraṃ hiraṇyam apy ātreyāya dātavyam /
17.8.[5]	idam eva vā hiraṇyam apekṣya goḥ prāthamyavacanam //
17.8.[6]	atha hotre dakṣiṇān nayanti //
17.8.[7]	ṛtvijān nāma hotrakā iti /
17.8.[8]	mahartvigbhyo 'nye ya ṛtvijas te hotrakāḥ /
17.8.[9]	tebhyas sarvebhyas sahaiva dakṣiṇā nayanti //
17.8.[10]	ye brāhmaṇā yajamānenāhūtā yajñaṃ vā draṣṭum āga[c]chanti te prasarpakāḥ /
17.8.[11]	tebhyo dakṣiṇādānam /
17.8.[12]	idam adṛṣṭārtham eva codyate nānamanārtham /
17.8.[13]	na hi tair ānatair ṛtvigbhir ivāsti prayojanam /
17.8.[14]	yāś ca dakṣiṇāḥ kratuṃ prati śrutau vihitās tāsām ṛtvigānamanārthataiva nyāyavidbhir niścitā /
17.8.[15]	tasmāt parisaṃkhyātadakṣiṇānapekṣayā yathotsāham anyad dravyaṃ prasarpakebhyo dātavyam /
17.8.[16]	evañ ced ātreyadakṣiṇāyā apy evaṃbhāvaḥ prāpnoti /
17.8.[17]	ko nety āha /
17.8.[18]	nanu pūrvam uktaṃ prathamāṃ gām ātreyāya dattveti /
17.8.[19]	tad anyasyāṃ gavi dīyamānāyāṃ virudhyeta /
17.8.[20]	nāyaṃ virodha āpadyate /
17.8.[21]	evaṃ hi tatrābhipremaḥ /
17.8.[22]	yā gaur ātreyāya dīyate sāpi parisaṃkhyātābhis saha dakṣiṇāpathena nīyata iti /
17.8.[23]	santi dakṣiṇādānārthā mantrāś śrutivihitā brahman manas ta ityādayaḥ /
17.8.[24]	tair etā dakṣiṇā dātavyāḥ /
17.8.[25]	tatrānenedam iti mantraliṅgasyāvirodhāya dakṣiṇādravyaṃ sannidhāv avasthāpya pratyakṣīkṛtya dadyāt /
17.8.[26]	sthāvarasya tu dravyasya pūrvavijñāpanena pratyakṣīkaraṇam /
17.8.[27]	evan dattā dakṣiṇāḥ prasannena manasa rtvijaḥ pratigṛhṇīyuḥ /
17.8.[28]	pratyagrahaiṣam iti brūyuḥ hotrakās tu pratyagrahaiṣmeti /
17.8.[29]	yad anyena vidhinā dakṣiṇā dīyeran tatrāpi yathārtham eva pratigṛhṇīyuḥ /
17.8.[30]	tūṣṇīṃbhāvenaiva vā pratigrahaṇam avagamayeyuḥ /
17.8.[31]	ke cit paravihitena vidhinā pratigrahaṇam icchanti na tu tad asmābhir mṛṣyate //
17.9-10.[1]	dakṣiṇāsu dakṣiṇāpathena nīyamānāsūtkare tiṣṭhann aniruktāṃ subrahmaṇyāṃ subrahmaṇyas trir āhvayati /
17.9-10.[2]	stutyartho vākyaśeṣaḥ /
17.9-10.[3]	tasyāyam arthaḥ /
17.9-10.[4]	yat prāyaṇam upakramaṇaṃ subrahmaṇyāyān tad evodayanaṃ samāpanaṃ syād iti /
17.9-10.[5]	evamartham aniruktām evātrāhvayatīti //
18.1.[1]	asti marutvatīyan nāma śastram /
18.1.[2]	tasmiñ śaste nārāśaṃsān bhakṣayanti /
18.1.[3]	dviḥ pūrvayor iti vacanād āpyāyya sādayanti /
18.1.[4]	asminn avasare vaiṣṭutaṃ vāsa āharateti saṃpraiṣasya vacanaṃ prātassavanataḥ prāptam api pūrvasminn eva vāsasi viṣṭutyupadhāne śakye 'nyopādānasyānyāyyatvād arthato nivartate /
18.1.[5]	na hy asti vastralābhād anyad asya prayojanam //
18.2-4.[1]	bhakṣiteṣu nārāśaṃseṣūdgātā dakṣiṇena hotur dhiṣṇyaṃ gatvā sadaso 'dhi pūrvayā dvārā niṣkramyāparayā dvārāgnīdhragṛhaṃ prapadyāgnīdhre 'gnau vakṣyamāṇe pṛṣṭhāhutī juhoti /
18.2-4.[2]	sadasa iti yo 'rthas sa eva sadaso 'dhīti /
18.2-4.[3]	adhiniṣkramyeti vā vyākhyeyam /
18.2-4.[4]	pṛṣṭhāhutī ity anarthakam /
18.2-4.[5]	nānarthakaṃ brahmasāmāgniṣṭomasāmavājapeyasāmasandhiṣāmatvāpattau bṛhadrathantarayor etadāhutyabhāvārthatvāt /
18.2-4.[6]	pṛṣṭhāhutyoḥ prayojakaṃ pṛṣṭham eva na bṛhadrathantare ity abhiprāyaḥ //
18.5.[1]	uttarām āhutin tūṣṇīñ juhoti /
18.5.[2]	amantrañ juhotīty arthaḥ /
18.5.[3]	nanu pṛṣṭhāhutī iti dvivacanād evottarasyā āhutyās sadbhāvasiddher mantrasya ca tasyām aprasaktasyānivartyatvād idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
18.5.[4]	nānarthakaṃ pūrvasyaiva mantrasyottarasyām api prasaktasya nivṛttyarthatvāt /
18.5.[5]	asati hy asmin vākya āhutidvayena mantras saṃbadhyeta /
18.5.[6]	nanu homasyedaṃ rūpaṃ yad uta kasya cid dravyasya kāñ cid devatām uddiśyāgnau prakṣepaḥ /
18.5.[7]	atra punar devatā na kīrtyate na cāsti mantro yenāsāv avagamyeta /
18.5.[8]	tasmād ayam ahomaḥ /
18.5.[9]	satyam etat /
18.5.[10]	na vinā devatayā homas saṃbhavati /
18.5.[11]	kin tu homavidhānānyathānupapattyaivātra kā cid devatā kalpanīyā /
18.5.[12]	tatrāpi mukhyatvāt prajāpater eva niyamanan nyāyyam /
18.5.[13]	tasmād anyatrāpi vidhāv īdṛśe prajāpatir devatātvena dhyātavyaḥ /
18.5.[14]	paravacanam apy etam artham upodbalayati prajāpatiṃ manasā dhyāyāt tūṣṇīṃhomeṣu sarvatreti //
18.6.[1]	bṛhat pibatu somyaṃ madhv ity evaṃ vā pūrvāhutir hotavyā /
18.6.[2]	vakṣyati sa rathantareṇa stute bṛhatā veti /
18.6.[3]	tatra rathantare pṛṣṭhe sati pṛṣṭhāhutimantraḥ pūrvavihitaḥ /
18.6.[4]	bṛhati tv ayam ucyate /
18.6.[5]	arthato hi vyavasthā yuktā na caivaṃ mantavyaṃ rāthantara evāyam mantro bṛhadartham ūhyata iti /
18.6.[6]	asty evāyam mantro bhedena bṛhadarthaḥ /
18.6.[7]	tasya tu pūrvasmān mantrād bhedamātraṃ granthalāghavāya kīrtyate /
18.6.[8]	na hi bṛhato rathantaraṃ prakṛtir yato 'yam ūha ity ucyeta //
18.7.[1]	idaṃ vikṛtyartham ucyate /
18.7.[2]	yat pṛṣṭhaṃ syād vairūpādi tat pṛṣṭhāhutimantre bṛhadrathantaraśabdayos sthāna ādiśet /
18.7.[3]	bṛhaty apy anenaiva siddhatvād bṛhad iti veti pūrvaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
18.7.[4]	nānarthakam anyatra bahuviṣayeṇa vacanena rathantaraśabdavato mantrasya bṛhaty aprāpaṇārthatvāt /
18.7.[5]	tena kiṃ sidhyati /
18.7.[6]	idaṃ sidhyati /
18.7.[7]	samānaṃ param iti bahvarthena vacanena mahimasaṃbharaṇamantro 'pi bṛhati prasakto rathantaraśabdavattvān nivartate /
18.7.[8]	nanu pṛṣṭhaprayuktatvād evāyaṃ mantro vairūpādiṣv api gacchati /
18.7.[9]	tatra vairūpādyādeśasyārthasiddhatvād idaṃ vākyam anarthakam /
18.7.[10]	nānarthakaṃ pṛṣṭhāṅgeṣu dharmeṣu yasya vacanan tasyaiva vairūpādiṣu gamanan nānyasyeti jñāpanārthatvāt /
18.7.[11]	tasmād vakṣyamāṇā bṛhadrathantaradharmā vairūpādiṣu na pravarteran /
18.7.[12]	nanu mahimasaṃbharaṇādi dharmacatuṣṭayan dṛśyate mahāvrate /
18.7.[13]	kāman dṛśyatām /
18.7.[14]	na tadanyatraiṣāṃ pravṛttau kāraṇaṃ bhavati //
18.8.[1]	hutvā pṛṣṭhāhutī savyam āvṛtya niṣkramaṇavartmanaiva sadaḥ prapadyāstāvaṃ bhajeta /
18.8.[2]	tato rathantarasya stotram adhvaryur āharati //
18.9.[1]	tat stotraṃ pratigṛhyānena yajuṣā pṛthivīm abhimṛśati //
18.10.[1]	atha rathantarasya mahimno jvalanajalarathāśanipavaneṣu saṃkīrṇān anena yajuṣā saṃbharati /
18.10.[2]	saṃbharāmīty abhisandhāya mantravacanaṃ saṃbharaṇam //
18.11.[1]	athemaṃ mantraṃ vāmadevyaṃ purastācchāntim abhivyāharati /
18.11.[2]	purastācchāntir vāmadevyam iti mantrasyaivāsya nāmanī /
18.11.[3]	atha vā vāmadevyam ity eva mantrasya nāma /
18.11.[4]	purastāc chāntim matvā vāmadevyam abhivyāharati /
18.11.[5]	abhyananaṃ hi vakṣyate /
18.11.[6]	tac cāthābhyaniti prāṇo vai śāntir iti śrutivacanāc chāntir bhavati /
18.11.[7]	tadapekṣayedaṃ vāmadevyaṃ yajuḥ purastācchāntir bhavati //
18.12-13.[1]	athaitāḥ pañcāmṛtavyāhṛtīr abhivyāharati /
18.12-13.[2]	ādyās tisraḥ padavyāhṛtaya uttare vākyavyāhṛtī //
18.12-13.[3]	etat pṛthivyabhimarśanamantrādy amṛtavyāhṛtyantaṃ sarvam uktvā stotram abhyaniti /
18.12-13.[4]	anavānam etad vidhicatuṣṭayam anuṣṭhāya tadante stotram abhyanyād ity arthaḥ /
18.12-13.[5]	yathā śvāsavāyus stotre nipatati tathābhyanitavyam //
18.14.[1]	bṛhatpṛṣṭhas somo yadi syād bṛhatas stotraṃ pratigṛhyedaṃ yajur japet //
18.15.[1]	stotrapratigrahaṇasaṃbaddhād vidheḥ paran dharmajātaṃ rathantarasya bṛhataś ca samānam /
18.15.[2]	vāmadevyābhivyāharaṇādi dharmatrayam ato vacanād bṛhati pravartate na tu mahimānas saṃbhāryāḥ /
18.15.[3]	pūrvoktam apy akaraṇam /
18.15.[4]	paravacanaṃ hy ekaṃ kāraṇaṃ rathantara eva rcaṃ yas te goṣu mahimeti /
18.15.[5]	mīmāṃsakaiś caivam avirodho bhavati yeṣām ayaṃ rāddhānto nohaḥ prakṛtāv iti /
18.15.[6]	kiṃ punar ime pṛthivyabhimarśanādayo dharmā brahmasāmādibhāve 'pi bṛhadrathantarayor iṣyante /
18.15.[7]	atra brūmaḥ /
18.15.[8]	bṛhatas tāvad itthaṃbhūtād ācāryeṇaiveme nivartitāḥ /
18.15.[9]	evaṃ hi tenoktaṃ bṛhaddharmopakrame yadi bārhatas somas syād iti /
18.15.[10]	na ca bṛhato brahmasāmādibhāvena bārhatas somo bhavati /
18.15.[11]	tasmād bṛhati tāvad apṛṣṭhe na prasaṅgo dharmāṇām /
18.15.[12]	tattulyanyāyatvāc ca rathantaradharmāṇām api sandhāv aprasaṅgas sidhyati /
18.15.[13]	atha vā śrutita evāyam arthas sāmadvaye 'pi sidhyati /
18.15.[14]	eṣāṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ sannidhau śrūyate yadi rāthantaras somas syād yadi bārhatas somas syād iti /
18.15.[15]	na pṛṣṭham eṣān dharmāṇāṃ hetus somaś ca kevalam /
18.15.[16]	saṃyuktam ubhayaṃ hetur āhutyoḥ pṛṣṭham eva tu //
18.15.[17]	yadā te bṛhadrathantarayor vaiśeṣikā dharmā ebhyaḥ /
18.15.[18]	paścāt sāmānyadharmāṇām āvartijapādīnāṃ prayogaḥ //
18.16.[1]	udgātā rathantareṇa vā bṛhatā vodgāyati /
18.16.[2]	nanu bahubhis stūyamānatvāt te stuvata iti prayoktuṃ yuktam /
18.16.[3]	satyam etat /
18.16.[4]	udgātṛprādhānyāvagamārthas tv ekavacanaprayogaḥ /
18.16.[5]	evam api vacanavairūpyakaraṇe hetur vaktavyo yad idaṃ pṛṣṭhayajñāyajñīyānām ekavacanena stutir vidhīyate bahuvacanenānyeṣām /
18.16.[6]	ayam atra hetur yat pūrvokte stotrapañcake nāsti gāyatram asti cānyeṣu /
18.16.[7]	śrutivihitagāyatrapratihāraparigrahārtho bahuvacanaprayoga ity arthaḥ /
18.16.[8]	kiṃ punar ayaṃ pṛṣṭhabhāve sāmnos tulyo vikalpaḥ /
18.16.[9]	kas sandehaḥ /
18.16.[10]	saty asmin vacane 'tha rathantaraṃ vā bṛhad vā pṛṣṭham iti /
18.16.[11]	nanu prākṛte samāmnāye bṛhacchyaitayor ṛcaś śyaitañ ca na dṛśyate rathantaranaudhase tu sārdham ṛgbhir dṛśyete /
18.16.[12]	tatra tulyavikalpāśrayaṇan na yujyate /
18.16.[13]	atra vadāmaḥ /
18.16.[14]	itthaṃ gṛhṇanto vayam imam āmnāyam anuvartemahi /
18.16.[15]	prathamasomasya rathantaram eva pṛṣṭham kāryam iti //
18.17.[1]	rathantare prastute ho ity uktvā tata udgīthādim ādadīta /
18.17.[2]	prastuta ity anarthakam /
18.17.[3]	nānarthakaṃ prastāvāntahovacanayos sandhānārthatvāt /
18.17.[4]	itarathā hi prastāvakālāntarbhāvenaiva hośabdam uktvodgīthādir eva prastāvena sandhīyeta /
18.17.[5]	tad anena nivartyate /
18.17.[6]	kiṃ punar idam ādyāyām eva stotriyāyāṃ kāryam āho svit sarvāsu /
18.17.[7]	sarvāsv iti brūmaḥ /
18.17.[8]	kutaḥ /
18.17.[9]	rathantare prastuta idaṃ vidhīyate bahukṛtvaś ca rathantaraṃ prastūyate /
18.17.[10]	tasmād ayaṃ vidhiḥ pratistotriyaṃ kāryaḥ /
18.17.[11]	kiñ cāṅgam etad rathantarasya yad dhovacanam /
18.17.[12]	rathantaran tāvad atrāvartata āvartamānañ ca tat svāṅgaṃ hośabdam apy āvartayati bhuktir iva pādanirṇejanādīni /
18.17.[13]	nanv asya stotrāṅgatā yuktā /
18.17.[14]	neti brūmaḥ /
18.17.[15]	rathantaram iti hi sāmno nāma na stotrasya /
18.17.[16]	kāmaṃ vā kayā cit kalpanayā stotre 'py asmin rathantaraśabdo vartatām /
18.17.[17]	tathāpi tu bhavadabhipretā hośabdānāvṛttir na sidhyati /
18.17.[18]	stotram api hīdaṃ bahukṛtvaḥ prastūyate /
18.17.[19]	atha vā na sakṛd api stotraṃ prastūyate /
18.17.[20]	sāmāvayavā hi prastāvādayo na stotram eṣāṃ viśeṣaṇatvenāvakalpate /
18.17.[21]	yady api kathañ cid avakalpeta tathāpi ho iti brūyād ity etāvatārthasiddhau ho ity uktvādim ādadītety ādisanbandhena vidhānād āder idam aṅgaṃ bhavati /
18.17.[22]	tadāvṛtter āvartetaiva /
18.17.[23]	nanu cāsyāṅgāni na stotrasya /
18.17.[24]	kim ataḥ /
18.17.[25]	idam ato bhavati /
18.17.[26]	tair api hośabdenevāvartitavyam iti /
18.17.[27]	atra brūmaḥ /
18.17.[28]	pṛṣṭhāhutyādayas sāmāṅgatve 'pi nāvartante /
18.17.[29]	sakṛdanuṣṭhitair eva taiḥ pratistotram upakriyate /
18.17.[30]	na hi te prathamastotriyāntarbhāvena prayujyante yatas tasyādāv evopakuryuḥ /
