18.17.[31]	hośabdavacanan tu prastute sāmni kriyamāṇaṃ svāśrayasyaiva stotriyāviśeṣasyopakartuṃ śaktaṃ nānyasya /
18.17.[32]	tasmād idam āvartate na pṛṣṭhāhutyādayaḥ /
18.17.[33]	dadyāt kanakaviṣāṇaṃ gośatam iti śrutvā kanakaśṛṅgatā sarvagavāṃ kriyate /
18.17.[34]	tatas stotrāṅgatve 'pi niścitāsyāvṛttiḥ //
18.18.[1]	idam adhastanād abhinnavyākhyam //
18.19.[1]	rathantare prastūyamāne cakṣuṣī saṃmīlayet /
18.19.[2]	atrāpi pūrvasyevāvṛttim eva niścinumahe /
18.19.[3]	kiṃ punar idaṃ prastāvāṅgam /
18.19.[4]	neti brūmaḥ /
18.19.[5]	yadi hy asya prastāvāṅgataiṣiṣyata rathantaraṃ prastuvan saṃmīlayed ity avakṣyata /
18.19.[6]	prastāvāṅgaṃ hi prastotraiva kartavyam /
18.19.[7]	yatas tv evam anuktan tasmād udgātraiva kartavyam //
18.20.[1]	ayam akṣṇoḥ prastāvakāle saṃmīlitayor unmīlanakālaḥ kathyate /
18.20.[2]	svar dṛśam iti prati vipaśyet /
18.20.[3]	vivṛṇuyād unmīlayed ity arthaḥ /
18.20.[4]	yatra punas svar dṛśam iti śabdo 'yan na śrūyate tatra katham /
18.20.[5]	tatrāpi yāni svar dṛśam ity anena tulyasthānāny udgīthāntyākṣaracatuṣṭayāni tāni vaktum upakramamāṇo vidhim etam anutiṣṭhet /
18.20.[6]	na hi svar dṛśam iti śabdenātra prayojanam /
18.20.[7]	kena tarhi /
18.20.[8]	tallakṣitena kālena /
18.20.[9]	sa ca kālas tadabhāve 'pi vidyata eva /
18.20.[10]	yathā pūrvāṃ sandhyāñ japaṃs tiṣṭhet sāvitrīm ārkadarśanād iti vidhim etam anutiṣṭhan hi meghādicchinnam arkam adṛṣṭvāpy arkadarśanalakṣite kāla uparamati tadvad atrāpi //
18.21.[1]	yāvatkālaṃ stobhet tāvatkālam udgātur hastau pṛthivyāṃ syātām /
18.21.[2]	arthavādo vākyaśeṣaḥ /
18.21.[3]	tasyāyam arthaḥ /
18.21.[4]	rathantaran devarathaḥ /
18.21.[5]	tam idānīm udgātārūḍhaḥ /
18.21.[6]	kṣipraṃ gāyed iti vacanam anuvartamānam udgātāram āśu dhāvann apavidhyed api /
18.21.[7]	tatparijihīrṣayā pṛthivī hastābhyām ālambyate /
18.21.[8]	tad ucyate devarathasyānapavyādhāyeti /
18.21.[9]	ṣaṣṭhī kartari /
18.21.[10]	devarathenodgātur anapavyādhāyety arthaḥ /
18.21.[11]	asvayonirathantaran daśama evāhni stubhyate /
18.21.[12]	tatrāgniṣṭudādau ca kim ayaṃ vidhir na gacchati /
18.21.[13]	atra brūmaḥ /
18.21.[14]	yady ayaṃ vidhis stobhāśrayo 'bhaviṣyan nāgamiṣyad agniṣṭudādau /
18.21.[15]	rathantaraṇimitta eva tv ayaṃ vidhir na stobhanimittaḥ /
18.21.[16]	evaṃ hi śrūyate /
18.21.[17]	eṣa vāva devaratho yad rathantaram /
18.21.[18]	rathantare prastute pṛthivīṃ hastābhyāṃ gacched devarathasyānapavyādhāyeti /
18.21.[19]	tasmād agniṣṭudādāv api rathantaraṃ gāyan yo 'sya vidheḥ prakṛtau stobhopalakṣitaḥ kālas tasmin kāle pṛthivīm ālambeta /
18.21.[20]	eṣām api dharmāṇām adhikāre yadi rāthantaras somas syād yadi bārhatas somas syād iti śrutau dṛśyamānatvād brahmasāmādibhāve bṛhadrathantarayor eṣām apravṛttiḥ /
18.21.[21]	asminn arthe vacanam eva tāṇḍisūtre vidyate tasyāpṛṣṭhasya sato nivarteran dharmā iti /
18.21.[22]	pṛṣṭhena stute māhendran nāma śastram śasyate /
18.21.[23]	atha hūyate māhendro grahaḥ /
18.21.[24]	tam anuvartante nārāśaṃsāḥ /
18.21.[25]	tadbhakṣaṇānantaraṃ vakṣyamāṇasyāvasaraḥ //
18.23.[1]	tat stotraṃ pratigṛhya etāṣ ṣaḍ vyāhṛtīr abhivyāharati /
18.23.[2]	itikaraṇādhyāhāreṇedaṃ vākyaṃ vyākhyeyam //
18.23.[3]	idañ ca yajur abhivyāharati /
18.23.[4]	atha vaikam evedaṃ vākyam //
18.24.[1]	sa udgātā madhyamayā vācānejann akampamāno vāmadevyena stute /
18.24.[2]	madhyamayā vāceti savanasvarāpavādaḥ //
18.25.[1]	ā pratihārād vāmadevyam anavānaṃ gāyet /
18.25.[2]	udgīthamadhye nāramed ity arthaḥ //
18.26.[1]	pratihāre pratihriyamāṇa eva vāg iti brūyād udgātā /
18.26.[2]	nanv āmnāyato 'pi vākchabdo vāmadevye sidhyati /
18.26.[3]	satyam /
18.26.[4]	sidhyati /
18.26.[5]	ūrdhvan tu pratihārād āmnāyataḥ prāptaḥ pratihāratulyakālatām anena vidhinā nīyate /
18.26.[6]	iyaṃ hi vacanavyaktiḥ /
18.26.[7]	yad vāg ity udgātā brūyāt tat pratihāre pratihriyamāṇa eveti /
18.26.[8]	nanv evam ācāryasyāmnāyaviruddhavāditvan doṣaḥ prasajati /
18.26.[9]	atra brūmaḥ /
18.26.[10]	śrutāv api vidyate /
18.26.[11]	pratihāra eva pratihriyamāṇe vāg ity udgātā brūyād iti /
18.26.[12]	tasmād ittham mantavyam /
18.26.[13]	sahaiva pratihāreṇāyam āmnāto vākchabdas sahoccāraṇasya dvayor abhāvāt pratihārād ūrdhvam āmnāyata iti /
18.26.[14]	udgātṛgrahaṇam anarthakam /
18.26.[15]	nānarthakam anejanamadhyamasvarayor ekavacanasaṃyogād udgātur eva prāptayoḥ prastotṛpratihartror api prāpaṇārthatvāt /
18.26.[16]	atha vā śrutivākyasyaivātra prakṣepād aparihāryam udgātṛgrahaṇam /
18.26.[17]	kiṃ punar ime dharmās sthānacyutam api vāmadevyam upasarpanti /
18.26.[18]	atra brūmaḥ /
18.26.[19]	bṛhadrathantarayos sthānacyutau dharmābhāvaḥ pratyapādi /
18.26.[20]	idaṃ kila tatra kāraṇam /
18.26.[21]	rāthantaras somo bārhatas soma iti dharmavidhisannidhau dṛśyata iti /
18.26.[22]	tatraitasmād darśanād ayan nyāya upalabhyate /
18.26.[23]	sthānacyutis sāmno dharmābhāve nimittam iti /
18.26.[24]	tenaiva nyāyena vāmadevyasyāpi sthānacyutasya dharmābhāvo niścīyate /
18.26.[25]	nyāyo hi kasmiṃś cid upalabdhas tatsadṛśe 'nyasminn api bhavati /
18.26.[26]	vākchabdas tv āmnāyamūlatvād yatrāmnāyate tatraivāvatiṣṭhate /
18.26.[27]	sthānād apāyam anapāyaṃ vā nāpekṣate /
18.26.[28]	tasmād ayam āgniṣṭute vāmadevye na pravarteta trairātrike tu pravartetaiva /
18.26.[29]	tatra ke cid vadanti /
18.26.[30]	sāmno dharmābhāvasya sthānacyutir yonicyutiś ca dvayaṃ saṃyuktaṃ nimittaṃ bhavati /
18.26.[31]	tataś ca yathā cyutam api yones svasthānavarti sāma dharmān labhate tathaiva cyutam api sthānāt svayonyavasthitaṃ labhetaiva dharmān iti /
18.26.[32]	tathā sati bṛhati brahmasāmni vāmadevye ca trairātrike pravarterann eva dharmāḥ //
18.27.[1]	atha naudhasena stute /
18.27.[2]	rathantarapṛṣṭhābhiprāyam etad vacanam /
18.27.[3]	bṛhatpṛṣṭhe tu śyaitena brahmasāmnā bhavitavyam /
18.27.[4]	evaṃ hi śrutir āha rathantareṇa stuvantīdaṃ vai rathantaram /
18.27.[5]	atha vāmadevyenedaṃ vā antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyam /
18.27.[6]	atha naudhasenādo vai naudhasam /
18.27.[7]	anantarhitān eveta ūrdhvān lokāñ jayati /
18.27.[8]	bṛhatā stuvanty ado vai bṛhat /
18.27.[9]	atha vāmadevyenedaṃ vā antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyam /
18.27.[10]	atha śyaitenedaṃ vai śyaitam /
18.27.[11]	anantarhitān evāmuto 'rvāco lokān jayatīti /
18.27.[12]	yac cādo vacanam atha naudhasaṃ vā śyaitaṃ vā brahmasāmeti tad apy uktavacanānurodhena pṛṣṭhavyavasthayaiva sāmno vikalpa iti mantavyam /
18.27.[13]	tasmād ayaṃ rāddhāntaḥ /
18.27.[14]	rathantare pṛṣṭhe sati naudhasaṃ brahmasāma bṛhati śyaitam iti /
18.27.[15]	kimarthaṃ punar ācāryeṇa śyaitena vety atra noktam /
18.27.[16]	yat pūrvam ṛksāmāmnāyadarśanavaśenopalabdhaṃ prathamasomasya rathantaram eva pṛṣṭham iti tasya dārḍhyārtham //
18.28.[1]	dinasya madhyamo bhāgo madhyandinaḥ /
18.28.[2]	tasmin bhavam mādhyandinaṃ savanam itthaṃ santiṣṭhate //
19.1.[1]	anantaran tṛtīyasavane kriyākramaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ //
19.1.[2]	prapadanasyāvṛtā yajñopavīty ācānto dhā asīti vediṃ prapadya vedyākramaṇena mṛdā śithirety anena vedim ākramyādhvanām adhvapata ity etenaiva yajuṣādityam upatiṣṭhate //
19.2.[1]	athānena yajuṣā dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anu paryāvṛtyāgnīdhrañ ca sadaś cottareṇa parītya paścāt sadasas tiṣṭhan samastān dhiṣṇyān āhavanīyādīn dakṣiṇavedyantaparyantān īkṣamāṇo 'gnayas sagarā ity etenaiva yajuṣopatiṣṭhate //
19.3.[1]	atha sadaḥ prapadya dakṣiṇenaudumbarīṃ parītya tayaiva prātassavanoktayaivāvṛtāstāva upaviśya hotur dhiṣṇyan dakṣiṇena gatvā sadaso 'dhi pūrvayā dvārā niṣkramyādhvaryupathena gatvā pūrvayā dvārā havirdhānagṛhaṃ prapadyottarasmin havirdhāne śakaṭe sannaṃ pūtabhṛtan nāma mṛnmayam mahat pātraṃ vasavas tvā punantv ity etenaiva mantratrayeṇa daśāpavitreṇa pavayati /
19.3.[2]	śakaṭopari sannasya pūtabhṛta upaviṣṭena pavanāsaukaryād upaveśanāvidhānāc ca tiṣṭhataiva pavayitavyam /
19.3.[3]	etenaiva pavitreṇeti vā vyākhyātavyam //
19.4.[1]	dvayor ambhṛṇayor uttarahavirdhānāvasthitayoḥ pūrva eva pūtabhṛd bhavati /
19.4.[2]	evakāro gaur eva rathantaram iyam eva prācī dik prathamam ahar ityādiṣv api vākyālaṃkārārthaḥ //
19.4.[3]	tayor evāpara ādhavanīyasaṃjño bhavati /
19.4.[4]	idaṃ prasaṅgena jñānārtham uktam //
19.5.[1]	pūtabhṛto mukhe pavitran ta ity etenaiva tṛcena pavitraṃ vitanoti //
19.6.[1]	tatra yathāvacanaṃ śukrasya pavitāra udgātāro 'dhvaryuprabhṛtayaś ca kurvanti /
19.6.[2]	rājānayanādīnām ātmābhimarśanāntānāṃ prātassavanikānāṃ vidhīnāṃ sarveṣām api parigraho yathādeśam iti kriyate //
19.7.[1]	tathā kṛte tayaiva prātassavanoktayaivāvṛtā saṃprasarpya sadasi pavamānenārbhavena stuvate //
19.9.[1]	uṣṇikkakubhyān tadāśraye sāmanī lakṣyete /
19.9.[2]	uṣṇikkakubhāv anavānam ā pratihārād gāyet /
19.9.[3]	sabhapauṣkale ity avacanaṃ śaṅkusujñānādiṣv api prāpaṇārtham //
19.10.[1]	pavamānena stute paśunādhvaryavaś caranti //
19.11.[1]	atha savanīyaiḥ puroḍāśaiś caranti //
19.12.[1]	rājani bhakṣite nārāśaṃsās sīdanti /
19.12.[2]	nanv ayam arthas sakṛt tṛtīyasavana iti pūrvam eva vyadhāyi /
19.12.[3]	satyam etat /
19.12.[4]	tatsiddhasyaivāyam anuvādaḥ kriyate kramāvagamanārtham anyavivakṣayā ca /
19.12.[5]	tasmād adoṣaḥ //
19.13-15.[1]	atha sadaso niṣkramyāparayā dvārā havirdhānaṃ prapadya tatra sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu tryāvṛd yathā tribhir uptānān tisro rājayo bhaveyus tathā puroḍāśaśakalāni trīṇi trīṇi tribhir ebhir mantrair upāsyanti /
19.13-15.[2]	mādayadhvam ityādir anuṣaṅgaḥ /
19.13-15.[3]	atrāsaṃsparśanaṃ sarvatrājyalepena somasyeti vacanād ājyalepasya ca puroḍāśeṣv ekāntasannipatanān nārāśaṃseṣv iti sāmīpyalakṣaṇā saptamī grāhyā /
19.13-15.[4]	yathā gaṅgāyāṃ gāvo 'vaṭe bhuñjata iti /
19.13-15.[5]	tato nārāśaṃsānāṃ samīpe dakṣiṇata upāsyeyuḥ /
19.13-15.[6]	upaśabdenaiva vā sāmīpyaṃ lakṣyate /
19.13-15.[7]	asminn anyeṣu ca pitṛkarmasu prācīnāvītinā bhavitavyam /
19.13-15.[8]	tasya manvādivacanasiddhatvād atrāvacanam //
20.1.[1]	vaiśvadevan nāmāsti śastram /
20.1.[2]	tasmiñ śaste nārāśaṃsān bhakṣayanti //
20.2.[1]	teṣu bhakṣiteṣv āgnīdhraś śālākān nāmāgnīn upakalpayate /
20.2.[2]	śālākāsu prajvalayya dhiṣṇyāgnīnām asmin savane viharaṇam /
20.2.[3]	tad idam uktañ śālākān upakalpayata iti /
20.2.[4]	ke cid asminn api savane pavamānānantaram eva dhiṣṇyān viharanti //
20.3.[1]	somadevatyena caruṇādhvaryavo 'smin kāle vyāpriyante //
20.4.[1]	caritvaitañ caruṃ sadasy āharanti //
20.5-6.[1]	tañ carum ābhyām ṛgyajurbhyām udgātāvekṣate //
20.7.[1]	tasmiṃs tu carau svāñ chāyām api paryavekṣeta /
20.7.[2]	ātmano 'praṇāśāyety arthavādaḥ /
20.7.[3]	ātmana iti vā chāyāviśeṣanam /
20.7.[4]	apraṇāśāyety etāvān evārthavādaḥ /
20.7.[5]	tatrāpy arthād ātmana ity eva kalpyam /
20.7.[6]	caruś cāyam āsiktabahvājyatvād ādarśa iva cchāyān darśayati //
20.8.[1]	athāpi carusthāt sarpiṣaḥ kiñ cid gṛhītvākṣṇor ādadhīta /
20.8.[2]	arthavādasyāyam arthaḥ /
20.8.[3]	cakṣurindriyasya vardhanārtham iti //
20.9-10.[1]	tatra caror avekṣaṇe vijñānam apy etat syāt /
20.9-10.[2]	ya ātmānam ātmanaś chāyāñ carāv asminn avekṣamāṇo na paripaśyet so 'cirād apetāsus syād iti //
20.11.[1]	yad idam uktaṃ vijñānan tasmāt satyāt kāraṇād ājyaṃ bhūyaś ca carāv ānīyāpi parididṛkṣetaivātmānam /
20.11.[2]	chāyān draṣṭuṃ prayatetaivety arthaḥ /
20.11.[3]	didṛkṣaiva hi śakyā /
20.11.[4]	darśanam atra daivādhīnam /
20.11.[5]	arthavādasyāyam arthaḥ /
20.11.[6]	sarvasya svāyuṣaḥ parigrahāyeti //
20.12.[1]	saumyasyeti ṣaṣṭhī pañcamyarthe /
20.12.[2]	saumyāc caroḥ kiñ cid upahatya tad anaya rcākṣṇor ādadhīta /
20.12.[3]	savye 'py akṣṇi mantro vaktavyaḥ /
20.12.[4]	yathā cedam udgātrā saumye carau vyāpṛtan tathaiva prastotṛpratihartārāv api vyāpriyeyātām /
20.12.[5]	uktaṃ hi puruṣasaṃskārāṇām ekavacanavihitānām api sarvārthatvam /
20.12.[6]	yac ca kiñ cid akṣaragauravam asmin saumyasaṃbandhe granthe tad asya śrautatvād eva mṛṣyatām //
20.13-14.[1]	tañ carum avekṣya dakṣiṇenaudumbarīṃ paryāhṛtyāparabhāge sadaso 'nena yajuṣā sādayati /
20.13-14.[2]	avekṣyety anarthakam /
20.13-14.[3]	nānarthakaṃ nyāyasiddhasya prastotṛpratihartror avekṣaṇādes sadbhāvajñāpanārthatvāt /
20.13-14.[4]	evañ ced avekṣya ... sādayatīti samānakartṛkatvena śravaṇāt prastotṛpratihartror anyatareṇa caros sādanaṃ prāpnoti /
20.13-14.[5]	na prāpnoti /
20.13-14.[6]	avekṣyeti ṇijantād ayaṃ pratyayaḥ /
20.13-14.[7]	tatrāyam arthaḥ /
20.13-14.[8]	prastotṛpratihartṛbhyām avekṣaṇaṃ kārayitvā sādayaty udgāteti //
20.15.[1]	yathetaṃ prativrajyopaviṣṭa udgātari yajñāyajñīyasya stotram adhvaryur āharati //
20.16.[1]	tena yajñāyajñīyenāprāvṛta udgāyet /
20.16.[2]	dvau pakṣau śrutau yajñāyajñīyādhikāre prāvaraṇam aprāvaraṇañ ca /
20.16.[3]	tayor ayam ācāryeṇeṣṭaḥ pakṣaḥ parigṛhyate /
20.16.[4]	nanu śrutāv eva pūrvaṃ prāvaraṇapakṣam uktvā tasmin doṣam udbhāvya paścād aprāvaraṇapakṣa evāvadhāritaḥ /
20.16.[5]	satyam etat /
20.16.[6]	śrutyavadhāritānān tu keṣāñ cid anityatvajñāpanārtham atrāprāvṛta ity ucyate /
20.16.[7]	kim etasya jñāpane prayojanam /
20.16.[8]	idam ucyate /
20.16.[9]	daśame 'hni brahmasāmnaḥ pañcadaśatvaṃ śrutir avadhārayati brahmasāmna eva nava stotriyā upādāyātropadadhyād iti /
20.16.[10]	tasyānityatvaṃ sidhyati /
20.16.[11]	iṣyate hi saṃvatsaram upagatasya caturviṃśam evāsyāhno brahmasāma /
20.16.[12]	tat kasmād iti cet kāraṇaṃ kalpavṛttau kathayiṣyāmaḥ //
20.17.[1]	yajñāyajñīyam eva tad gāyatram iva prastuyād ityādivacanānusāreṇa svasyām evoharahasye gīyate /
20.17.[2]	yat tatra saptamaṃ sāma tasya rathantaravarṇeti nāma /
20.17.[3]	rathantaravarṇām asya stotrasya dvitīyāṃ karoti //
20.18.[1]	rathantaravarṇāyā nidhanam anu nidhanam uktvānena mantreṇottarata āsīnāṃ patnīṃ samīkṣate /
20.18.[2]	nanu vāmī nāmetyāde[r] retāṃsi dhīmahītyantasyaikatvaṃ madhya itikaraṇābhāvād uktam /
20.18.[3]	tasmād ayaṃ vidhis samantrakaṃ kartavya uttaras tūṣṇīṃ viparyayo vā /
20.18.[4]	atra brūmaḥ /
20.18.[5]	yady api madhye netikaraṇaṃ vṛṣṇas ta ityādeḥ patnīkartṛkapratisamīkṣaṇāṅgatvam eva liṅgasaṃpattaye grāhyam /
20.18.[6]	kiñ ca tad āhur ā vā etat patny udgātuḥ prajān datta ityādi brāhmaṇam atra mantrabhedam avagamayati /
20.18.[7]	tasmād itikaraṇādhyāhāreṇedaṃ vākyaṃ vyākhyeyam /
20.18.[8]	kim punar idaṃ rathantaravarṇayaiva nidhanaṃ viśeṣyate na punar yajñāyajñīyena /
20.18.[9]	atra brūmaḥ /
20.18.[10]	ānantaryavihitatvād rathantaravarṇāyās tayaiva nidhanaṃ viśeṣyate /
20.18.[11]	yadi ca yajñāyajñīyena nidhanaṃ viśeṣyeta prāg api rathantaravarṇāyāḥ prathamastotriyānidhane patnī samīkṣyeta /
20.18.[12]	tatra pūrvavākyavihitarathantaravarṇāgānam aṅgīkṛtyottaravākyavihite patnīsamīkṣaṇe kriyamāṇe vidhānakramo bādhyeta /
20.18.[13]	tasmād api rathantaravarṇayaiva nidhanasya niścinumahe viśeṣaṇam //
20.19.[1]	anena yajuṣodgātāram itarā pratisamīkṣate /
20.19.[2]	itaraśabdaḥ pūrvasya vidheḥ karmabhāvena sadasi sannihitān tasyaiva kartur udgātur itarāṃ patnīm atropalakṣayati /
20.19.[3]	patnīty avacanaṃ śrutyanukaraṇārtham /
20.19.[4]	patnyaśaktau yajamāno mantraṃ vadet //
20.20.[1]	yajñāyajñīyasya someṣu bhakṣiteṣu sadaso 'dhy aparayā dvārā niṣkramyāparayaiva dvārāgnīdhragṛhaṃ prapadyāgnīdhre 'gnau vakṣyamāṇe sruvāhutī juhoti /
20.20.[2]	ke cid āgnīdhraśālāyā ekām eva dvāran dakṣiṇataḥ kurvanti /
20.20.[3]	nanv atra bhakṣyamāṇānāṃ sarvasomānām api yajñāyajñīyasaṃbandhāviśeṣe viśeṣaṇānarthakyād yajñāyajñīyasyety anarthakam /
20.20.[4]	nānarthakaṃ prathamasome rājanyasya ṣoḍaśino nivāraṇārthatvāt /
20.20.[5]	vakṣyate hi ṣoḍaśinam adhikṛtya tad ekastotraṃ syāt ṣoḍaśī yajñāyajñīyañ ceti /
20.20.[6]	tatra caiṣāṃ ṣoḍaśiyajñāyajñīyayos somānāṃ yajñāyajñīyenaiva viśeṣaṇam ubhayasāmnas somasya rathantareṇevaindreṇeva caindrāgnasyānupapannam /
20.20.[7]	evam asya yajñāyajñīyagrahaṇasya rājanyayajñe viruddhārthavāditvād anyatra bhūtārthānuvāditvāt prasakte nairarthakye prathamasomād rājanyasya ṣoḍaśinam asya sārthakatvāya nivartayāmaḥ /
20.20.[8]	ke cid idaṃ somabhakṣaṇasya sāmnā viśeṣaṇaṃ somasaṃbandhinām eva cchandogānāṃ somabhakṣaṇañ jñāpayatīti kalpayitvā subrahmaṇyaṃ somabhakṣān niṣedhayanti /
20.20.[9]	kiṃ punar anagniṣṭome 'pi kratāv etatkāle evaite āhutī /
20.20.[10]	neti brūmaḥ /
20.20.[11]	savanasamāptāv evaite āhutī hotavye ity aparayā dvārā niṣkramaṇavidhānād avagamyate /
20.20.[12]	yatra hi savanam asamāptaṃ tatra pṛṣṭhāhutyādau pūrvayaiva dvārā niṣkramaṇavidhir dṛṣṭaḥ /
20.20.[13]	avadac ca kauṣītakiḥ nāsaṃsthite savane 'parayā dvārā nissarpatīti /
20.20.[14]	tasmād uttarāsv api saṃsthāsu yad antyaṃ stotran tasya someṣu bhakṣiteṣu sruvāhutyoḥ kālaḥ /
20.20.[15]	kiṃ punar atra sruveṇāhutyor viśeṣaṇāt pravṛtahomādiṣu juhvā homaḥ /
20.20.[16]	naitad avakalpayate /
20.20.[17]	yady evan tatraiṣiṣyatātra sruveṇāhutī ity avakṣyata /
20.20.[18]	siddhenaiva tu sruvasaṃbandhenānayor āhutyos sruvāhutī iti saṃjñā yājñikaprasiddhā /
20.20.[19]	asti ca bahusādhāraṇaguṇāvalambiny api saṃjñā /
20.20.[20]	yathā paṅkajaṃ phalguno manobhava iti /
20.20.[21]	atha vā sruvaparimite dravye sruvaśabdo 'tra vartata agnihotre yathā sa yaṃ prathamaṃ sruvam unnayatīti /
20.20.[22]	tasmāt pūrṇena sruveṇaite āhutī hotavye //
21.1.[1]	anūyājā nāma yāgaviśeṣāḥ /
21.1.[2]	tair idānīm adhvaryavaś caranti //
21.2.[1]	anūyājaiś caritvā hāryojananāmadheyena dhānāmiśreṇa graheṇa caranti //
21.3-4.[1]	hutasya hāryojanasyoccheṣaṇād avaśiṣṭād avayavād iyatīr veyatīr vā dhānā ādāya tā āhavanīyasya samīpa anena yajuṣā nidadhati /
21.3-4.[2]	kiyatyaḥ punar iyatyo bhavanti /
21.3-4.[3]	ime brūmahe /
21.3-4.[4]	iyatīr veyatīr veti nedaṃ vacanaṃ parimāṇadvayasyaiva dhānānāṃ vikalpakam /
21.3-4.[5]	sarvaparimāṇāpekṣo 'yaṃ vikalpaḥ /
21.3-4.[6]	dṛśyate hi bahuviṣayā dviruktiḥ /
21.3-4.[7]	yathāyām ayām itīdaṃ brahmedaṃ brahmetīyad itīyad itīti ca /
21.3-4.[8]	tasmād yathālābham atra dhānā ādeyāḥ /
21.3-4.[9]	ke cid vyācakṣate /
21.3-4.[10]	aṅgulīnām agrāt prabhṛty uttamaparvadvayāntasya parimāṇadvayasyaivāyaṃ vikalpa iti /
21.3-4.[11]	idañ ca karma dhānānidhānādy upariṣṭājjapāntaṃ subrahmaṇyenāpi kartavyam /
21.3-4.[12]	yat tv asya neṣyate tad uttaratrāsmābhir apavadiṣyate //
21.5.[1]	saptabhir ebhir mantrair enāṃsy avamoktuṃ yajante /
21.5.[2]	kim anādeśād ājyena /
21.5.[3]	atra brūmaḥ /
21.5.[4]	mantrāṇāṃ śākalatvavacanād evādiṣṭam atra dravyam /
21.5.[5]	yadi hi śakalair hūyeta tato mantrāś śākalās syuḥ /
21.5.[6]	tasmāt palāśādīnāṃ śakalair atra hotavyam /
21.5.[7]	atha vā dravyam eva śākalaśabdenābhidhīyate /
21.5.[8]	śākalaiś śakalair ity arthaḥ /
21.5.[9]	svārthe taddhitaḥ /
21.5.[10]	atha vā nāyan taddhitārthaḥ /
21.5.[11]	tadbhinnam evedaṃ prātipadikaṃ śakalaśabdenaikārtham /
21.5.[12]	dṛśyate hi khaḍgaḥ khāḍgaḥ talas tāla iti /
21.5.[13]	svāhākāreṇa vinā homasyādarśanād eṣām api mantrāṇāṃ svāhākārāntānām eva śaunakenāmnātatvād atrāpi svāhākārāntair eva homo niścīyate //
21.6-7.[1]	appūrṇāś camasā apsuṣomā nāma bhavanti /
21.6-7.[2]	tān apsuṣomān dakṣiṇena cātvālam upaviśya somabhakṣakrameṇa pṛthag upahavanigadān abhivyāhṛtya vā samupahūtā sma iti yugapad abhivyāhṛtya vānena yajuṣāvaghreṇa bhakṣayanti /
21.6-7.[3]	avajighrantīty arthaḥ //
21.8.[1]	bhakṣaṇānantaram anena yajuṣā dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anu paryāvartate /
21.8.[2]	bhakṣanimitto 'yam ātmasaṃskāraḥ /
21.8.[3]	tasmād ekavacanavihito 'pi sarvaiḥ kartavyaḥ //
21.9.[1]	savyaṃ bāhum anu punas tūṣṇīṃ paryāvṛtyānena yajuṣā dvitīyaṃ bhakṣayanti /
21.9.[2]	dvitīyam ity anarthakam /
21.9.[3]	nānarthakam avaghreṇa bhakṣayantīty asyāvabodhanārthatvāt /
21.9.[4]	dvitīyādayo hi śabdās tulyajātīyāpekṣayaiva pravartante //
21.10.[1]	bhakṣayitvā sarveṣāṃ bhakṣaṇād ūrdhvan tān apsuṣomān udgātā samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomīty etenaiva mantreṇa cātvāle 'vanayati //
21.11.[1]	dadhīty eva dadhiṣomāḥ /
21.11.[2]	tān āgnīdhra upaviśya camasena vā yathāpūrvaṃ paryayeṇa pāṇibhir eva vā yugapad etaya rcā bhakṣayanti /
21.11.[3]	yadi subrahmaṇyas soman na bhakṣayed apsuṣomadadhiṣomān api na bhakṣayet //
22.1.[1]	patnīsaṃyājair nāma yāgair antaśśālam adhvaryavaś caranti //
22.2.[1]	patnīsaṃyājaiś caritvāvabhṛtham apravṛttaprayojanaṃ yajñam agreṇāgnīdhram adhvaryavas saha sādayanti //
22.3.[1]	tasminn avabhṛthe viṣṭutīś caudumbarīñ cāsandīñ cāpyajati prakṣipati /
22.3.[2]	kim iyaṃ somāsandī codyata āho svid gharmāsandī /
22.3.[3]	na somāsandī nāpi gharmāsandī /
22.3.[4]	tayor hi nāsmākaṃ vyāpāraḥ /
22.3.[5]	nanu nāto 'nyātrāsty āsandī /
22.3.[6]	satyam etat /
22.3.[7]	asti tu mahāvrate /
22.3.[8]	tadartham āsandīgrahaṇam //
22.4.[1]	anena mārgeṇa niṣkrāmann imaṃ saṃpraiṣam adhvaryur āha //
22.15.[1]	eṣāṃ lokānām āptyai //
22.16.[1]	asty avabhṛtheṣṭir nāmeṣṭiḥ /
22.16.[2]	tayādhvaryavaś caranti //
22.17.[1]	samāptāyām avabhṛtheṣṭyām upāvasṛpya tīrtham ebhir mantrais trir apa ācāmati /
22.17.[2]	mantrāṇāṃ liṅgāt sa yad evātra rjīṣa iti cārthavādāt somabhakṣasaṃbandhibhis sarvair evācamanaṃ kartavyam /
22.17.[3]	tatra nedam abhakṣaṇapakṣe subrahmaṇyasya //
22.18.[1]	atha nivṛttās tīrthād udumbaramayīr ārdrāḥ parṇavatīs samidho 'nena mantreṇādadate /
22.18.[2]	ekaikā samit sarvair ādeyā //
22.19.[1]	yo yas samidham ādattavān sa sarvo gatvāhavanīye 'nena yajuṣā samidham abhyādadhāti //
22.20.[1]	abhyādhāya samidham anena yajuṣāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate //
22.21.[1]	athaitad yajur japati //
22.22.[1]	somābhiṣave sutyāśabdaḥ prathamaṃ pravartate /
22.22.[2]	yasminn ahani sutyā sa ca divasas sutyāśabdenābhidhīyate /
22.22.[3]	atra tu sutyādivase kriyamāṇaṃ karmakalāpam upalakṣayati /
22.22.[4]	santiṣṭhate sutyā /
22.22.[5]	yat kartavyaṃ sutyādivase tat sarvam atrāvasīyata ity arthaḥ /
22.22.[6]	samāptatvāt karmaṇo niṣkrāmeyuḥ //
22.23.[1]	yathāyathaṃ yathā svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ praty udgātāro visṛjyante yajamānena /
22.23.[2]	parigāṇagānapakṣe nedānīṃ prastotā visṛjyate //
22.24.[1]	yo 'yañ jyotiṣṭomas sa ekāha ity ucyate /
22.24.[2]	tasyāṅgabhūtaṃ yat karma tad aikāhikam ity arthaḥ /
22.24.[3]	mahan me 'voca ityāder upariṣṭājjapāntasyaikāhikasya karmaṇaḥ kriyākramo vyākhyātas sarvañ ca vikṛtijātam ayam vidhir asmād evaikāhād āskandati /
22.24.[4]	ye tu vaikṛtā viśeṣās teṣāṃ kaiś cid atrāpi kalpitāḥ pariśiṣṭāḥ paryadhyāye kalpayiṣyante //
23.1.[1]	yena karmaṇāgnayo gārhapatyādaya ādhīyante tad agnyādheyam /
23.1.[2]	tasya somāt pūrvasyāpi sataḥ pūrvam avacane pūrvam eva kāraṇaṃ pratyapādi /
23.1.[3]	iha tūcyate /
23.1.[4]	agnyādheye liṅgaśākhāntarīyavacanaprāpitānāṃ sāmnāṃ gānasya kālam upadekṣyāmaḥ /
23.1.[5]	atha gānan tatkālañ ceti kalpyam //
23.2-3.[1]	yajñopavīty ācānto 'gnīnāṃ viharaṇadeśam uttareṇa parītya gārhapatyasyāyatanam apareṇa prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhann araṇyor ity asyām ṛci ghṛtācer āṅgirasasya sāmādharottarayor araṇyos saṃyojyamānayor gāyati //
23.4.[1]	asyām ṛci rāśivairājam mathyamāne gāyati //
23.5.[1]	asyām ṛci kaunmudam udyati dhūme gāyati //
23.6.[1]	asyām ṛci gāthinaḥ kauśikasya sāma ca yac cādo 'gneś śraiṣṭhyam iti tac ca jāte 'gnau gāyati /
23.6.[2]	agneś śraiṣṭhyāt pūrvasmin sāmacatuṣṭaya ṛgādigrahaṇam anarthakam /
23.6.[3]	nānarthakam ṛggataliṅgaparijighṛkṣayaiṣāṃ sāmnāṃ gānam iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
23.6.[4]	kim etasya jñāpane prayojanam /
23.6.[5]	vakṣyamāṇabrahmasāmagānagrahaṇapakṣe sāmacatuṣṭayam idam anādṛtya rcām evāsāṃ vacanam /
23.6.[6]	udgātur eva hi gānaprādhānyan na brahmaṇaḥ /
23.6.[7]	atha vedaṃ vijñānam ṛggrahaṇasya prayojanam /
23.6.[8]	ṛggatāl liṅgāt sāmacatuṣṭayam idaṃ pravṛttan na vacanād iti //
23.7.[1]	gārhapatye 'gnāv ādhīyamāne rathantaraṃ gāyati /
23.7.[2]	rathantaravāmadevyabṛhadvāravantīyaśyaiteṣu ke cit saṃpreṣyanti ke cin na /
23.7.[3]	tat pūrvam eva pṛṣṭvādhvaryun tadvaśam iyāt //
23.8.[1]	gārhapatyād āhavanīyārtham agnāv uddhriyamāṇe vāmadevyaṃ gāyet //
23.9.[1]	ke cid anuddhṛtyaivāhavanīyārtham agnim anvāhāryapacanam ādadhati /
23.9.[2]	tatra siddhā yajñāyajñīyād ūrdhvavartitā vāmadevyasya //
23.10.[1]	āhavanīyārtham uddhṛtan tam agniṃ prāñcaṃ praṇīyāhavanīyasya sthāne nidadhaty adhvaryavaḥ /
23.10.[2]	parasya vidher viṣayak.lptir iyam //
23.11.[1]	tad iti tadārthe /
23.11.[2]	atha vā tacchabdadarśanād yacchabdam apy adhyāhṛtyaikavākyatayaivedaṃ yojyam /
23.11.[3]	yadā nidadhati tadā gāyati //
23.13.[1]	ādhita āhavanīye vāravantīyaṃ śyaitañ ca gāyati /
23.13.[2]	ādhita ity ācāryaprāmāṇyād dadhāter hīty asya vidheḥ kva cid abhāve lakṣaṇam anumeyam /
23.13.[3]	atha vādhita i ity evaṃ padacchedaḥ kāryaḥ /
23.13.[4]	iśabdo 'sti nipātaḥ /
23.13.[5]	sa ihetiśabdasyārthe vartate /
23.13.[6]	ādhita i āhitavān iti /
23.13.[7]	asyāṃ velāyāṃ gāyatīti kalpyam //
23.14.[1]	yāv agnī sabhāyām āvasathe ca nidhīyete tau sabhyāvasathyau /
23.14.[2]	tāv āhitau sabhapauṣkalābhyām upatiṣṭheta /
23.14.[3]	sabhena sabhyaṃ pauṣkalenāvasathīyam //
23.15.[1]	sarvān agnīn āhitāñ śyaitenopatiṣṭhetety eka ācāryā bruvate /
23.15.[2]	asmin pakṣe vāravantīyānantaraṃ śyaitam agītvā sabhyāvasathyau svasāmabhyām upasthāya tataḥ pañcāgnīn sahaiva śyaitenopatiṣṭheta /
23.15.[3]	sabhyāvasathyayos tu vaikalpikam ādhānam /
23.15.[4]	tato 'nayor anādhānapakṣe na śyaitasya kālaḥ pakṣadvaye 'pi bhidyate //
23.16-18.[1]	tāny etāni sāmāny udgātā gāyed ebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ /
23.16-18.[2]	tatra gānasaṃyogād iti gānenodgātus saṃyogāt /
23.16-18.[3]	kuto 'sya gānasaṃyogaḥ /
23.16-18.[4]	yato 'yaṃ gānakartṛvacanenodgātṛśabdenābhidhīyate /
23.16-18.[5]	atha vedādhikṛtatvād iti sāmavedenodgātuḥ kartṛtvenādhikṛtatvād upāttatvāt /
23.16-18.[6]	anyārthe hi vākye śrūyate /
23.16-18.[7]	tad āhur yad ṛcā hotṛtvaṃ kriyate yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnodgītha iti /
23.16-18.[8]	tatra sāmavedenodgīthakriyāyām udgīthasya kartur udgātṛtve sāmavedenodgātā karotīty ayam artho labhyate /
23.16-18.[9]	atha vā sāmavedenodgātur adhikṛtatvam asya vedasya samākhyānād avagamyate /
23.16-18.[10]	loke hy audgātro veda ity ayaṃ vedas samākhyāyate /
23.16-18.[11]	atha brahmaudane ca liṅgadarśanād iti /
23.16-18.[12]	yena śrutena dṛṣṭena vā kaś cit pratyakṣeṇāgṛhyamāṇo 'rtho niścīyate tat tasya liṅgaṃ bhavati /
23.16-18.[13]	yathā dhūmo 'gnisadbhāvasya /
23.16-18.[14]	yathā ca kamalodbodho divākarodayasya /
23.16-18.[15]	evam atrāpi tāny udgātā gāyed ity asyārthasya niścayo brahmaudana āgnyādheyike liṅgadarśanāt kriyate /
23.16-18.[16]	yena tal liṅgam ācāryeṇa paraśākhāyān dṛṣṭaṃ tena nehedam iti nirdiṣṭaṃ śabdena /
23.16-18.[17]	sāmānyaśabdenaivoktaṃ liṅgadarśanād iti /
23.16-18.[18]	tat khalu liṅgam /
23.16-18.[19]	mahartvijo brahmaudanaṃ prāśnīyur iti paravacanam /
23.16-18.[20]	ete ca mahartvijo yad dhotādhvaryur brahmodgāteti /
23.16-18.[21]	yadi cāgnyādheyasāmāny udgātur anyo gāyen niṣprayojanasyāgnyādheye tadarthe brahmaudane darśanam udgātur nāvakalpeta /
23.16-18.[22]	tasmāt kāraṇatrayād udgātaiva sāmāni gāyet /
23.16-18.[23]	kiñ ca yo 'yaṃ madhyamo hetuḥ sa sarvatrāpi sāmavede vihitam /
23.16-18.[24]	anirdiṣṭakartṛkaṃ karmodgātā kuryād ity avagamayati //
23.19.[1]	teṣāṃ sāmnāṃ yāni tṛcasthāni tṛceṣv api vidyante tāni tṛceṣu gāyet /
23.19.[2]	na stotrabhūtānīti vakṣyati /
23.19.[3]	tasmād imaṃ vidhiṃ bṛhadrathantaravāmadevyāni prayojayanti na yajñāyajñīyaprabhṛtīni //
23.20.[1]	yāny ekarc[eṣ]u bhajante tāni tris trir gāyet /
23.20.[2]	na stotrabhūtānīti /
23.20.[3]	ata eva kāraṇād yajñāyajñīyaprabhṛtīny apīmaṃ vidhiṃ prayojayanti na kevalaṃ pañcādyāny agner nidhi ca /
23.20.[4]	kiṃ punar bṛhadrathantaravāmadevyāni nemaṃ vidhiṃ prayojayanti /
23.20.[5]	kutas saṃśayaḥ /
23.20.[6]	yatas tāny ekarceṣv api santi tṛceṣv api /
23.20.[7]	atra brūmaḥ /
23.20.[8]	yady ekarceṣu sattāmātram āśritya trirgānam aiṣiṣyata tris sarvāṇīty avakṣyata /
23.20.[9]	na hy atra vihitaṃ sāmāsti yad ekarcan na spṛśati /
23.20.[10]	yatas tv ekarcena viśinaṣṭi tata eva labhyate /
23.20.[11]	yāny ekarceṣv eva na tṛceṣv iti /
23.20.[12]	tasmād bṛhadrathantaravāmadevyāni sakṛt sakṛd eva gāyet //
23.21.[1]	tāni sarvāṇi sāmāni tiṣṭhan gāyet /
23.21.[2]	nanv ādāv uktam apareṇa gārhapatyāyatanaṃ prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhann iti /
23.21.[3]	tad adhikārarūpeṇa sarveṣv apy eṣu bhavituṃ śaknoti /
23.21.[4]	tato 'yaṃ vidhir anarthakaḥ /
23.21.[5]	nānarthakas sthānaviśeṣapratipādanārthatvāt /
23.21.[6]	tato yajñāyajñīyādīni tasya tasyāgneḥ paścāt tiṣṭhan gāyet //
23.22.[1]	stotreṣu bhūtāni pravṛttāni na gāyet /
23.22.[2]	yena rūpeṇa stotreṣu bhūtāny etāni tāni tena rūpeṇa na gāyed ity arthaḥ /
23.22.[3]	atha vāstotrabhūtānīti kṛtvaivan neyam /
23.22.[4]	stotreṣu bhūtā utpannā ye viśeṣās te stotrabhūtāḥ /
23.22.[5]	te yeṣu na santi tāny astotrabhūtānīti /
23.22.[6]	ubhayathāpi ye rathantarādīnāṃ stotrārthāḥ pāṭhās teṣām ihāgrahaṇaṃ sidhyati /
23.22.[7]	athānyathā vyākhyāsyāmaḥ //
23.23.[1]	madhyamayāmandrayānuccayā vācāgnyādheyasāmāni gāyet /
23.23.[2]	atha vāstotraparibhāṣāvākyāntabhūtam evedaṃ na vākyāntaram /
23.23.[3]	tiṣṭhann astotrabhūtāni madhyamayā vāceti /
23.23.[4]	tataḥ pravargyādiṣv api madhyamayaiva vācā geyam /
23.23.[5]	asmin vyākhyāne parisāmasu madhyamayā vācā gāyed iti vidhir anarthakaḥ /
23.23.[6]	nānarthakas savanāntarbhūtaparigāṇārthatvāt /
23.23.[7]	pūrvayor hi savanayor antarbhūteṣu parigāṇeṣu tatsvarau mandroccau paribhāṣām imāṃ bādhitvā prasajataḥ /
23.23.[8]	tannivṛttaye tatra madhyamayā vāceti vidhāsyati /
23.23.[9]	katarat punar vyākhyānayor garīyaḥ /
23.23.[10]	yataḥ pūrvasmin vyākhyāne pravargyādiṣv aniyatas svaro bhavati niyato 'smin tata idaṃ garīyaḥ //
23.24-25.[1]	manasā vācā vā brahmā sāmāni gāyed ity eka ācāryā bruvate /
23.24-25.[2]	kimarthaṃ manasā vety asya brahmaṇaiva sambandhaḥ kriyate nodgātrā /
23.24-25.[3]	atra brūmaḥ /
23.24-25.[4]	itthan naḥ pratibhāti /
23.24-25.[5]	brahmodgātror anyatareṇāgnyādheyasāmāni geyānīti vacanam ācāryeṇa dṛṣṭam /
23.24-25.[6]	idañ ca dṛṣṭaṃ bahvṛcaśrutau /
23.24-25.[7]	dve vai yajñasya vartanī /
23.24-25.[8]	vācānyā saṃskriyate manasānyā /
23.24-25.[9]	sā yā vācā saṃskriyate tām anya ṛtvijas saṃskurvanti /
23.24-25.[10]	atha yā manasā tāṃ brahmā /
23.24-25.[11]	tasmād yāvad ṛcā yajuṣā sāmnā ca kuryus tūṣṇīn tāvad brahmāsīta /
23.24-25.[12]	ardhaṃ hi tad yajñasya saṃskarotīti /
23.24-25.[13]	asmadupaniṣadgranthaś cāyaṃ vāva yajño yo 'yaṃ pavata ityādis tasmāt sa tūṣṇīm āsta ityantas samupalakṣitaḥ /
23.24-25.[14]	tato 'gnyādheyakarmaṇi brahmaṇas tūṣṇīmāsanārtham manasāgānaṃ vihitavān /
23.24-25.[15]	manasāpi hi gītaṃ gītam eva bhavatīti /
23.24-25.[16]	atha caivaṃ paśyan vāpakṣam api brahmaṇo 'bhyupagatavān /
23.24-25.[17]	yato vacanād brahmaṇas sāmagānam āgataṃ tata eva vāpakṣo 'py āgata iti /
23.24-25.[18]	udgātus tu manasāgānaṃ kva cid api na dṛśyate /
23.24-25.[19]	na cāsya brahmaṇa iva tūṣṇīmāsane kāraṇam upalakṣyate /
23.24-25.[20]	tasmād evam eva vyavadhātavyam /
23.24-25.[21]	udgātā ced vācaiva brahmā ced vācā vā manasā veti //
23.26.[1]	nityam agnihotre ete geye /
23.26.[2]	vikalpāprasaṅgāt sadety anarthakam /
23.26.[3]	nānarthakam anasmadīyenāpi vidhināgnihotre hūyamāne sāmadvayasya prāpaṇārthatvāt /
23.26.[4]	yadi hi sadeti nāvakṣyata kam aham asmi kam mamety etad uktvā veti vakṣyamāṇatvād asmadagnihotravidhāv eva sāmadvayaṃ prāvartiṣyata /
23.26.[5]	sadeti vacanāt sarvatrāpi siddhāsya pravṛttiḥ /
23.26.[6]	kaḥ punar atra gātā /
23.26.[7]	yajamānaḥ /
23.26.[8]	na hy udgātāgnihotre 'sti na ca sāmāny adhvaryur avagacchati /
23.26.[9]	uttaratra ca kāraṇaṃ vakṣyāmo yajamānageyatve /
23.26.[10]	apara āha //
23.27.[1]	yathāsaṃkhyanyāyenaiva pūrvasminn agnihotre gauṣūktasya parasminn āśvasūktasya siddher vākyadvayam anarthakam /
23.27.[2]	nānarthakam ekaikasmin sāmadvayaprasaṅganivṛttyarthatvāt /
23.27.[3]	atha vā yathāsaṃkhyanyāyenaiva sāmadvayam agnihotrābhyāṃ kāmaṃ saṃbadhyatām /
23.27.[4]	agnihotrayos tu sāyaṃprātaḥkālatvaṃ vākyadvayam idaṃ vijñāpayati /
23.27.[5]	naivaṃ vacanavyaktiḥ kāryā yat sāyaṃ hūyate tasmin gauṣūktam iti /
23.27.[6]	kathan tarhi /
23.27.[7]	yad gauṣūktavad agnihotran tat sāyaṃ hotavyam iti //
23.28-29.[1]	ayam ubhayos sāmnor gānakālaviśeṣaḥ kathyate /
23.28-29.[2]	pūrvasyām āhutau hutāyāṃ vaitadyajurvacanānantaraṃ vā geye /
23.28-29.[3]	atra yadi sāmnor hāvakenaiva gānam aiṣiṣyata pūrvām āhutiṃ hutvety avadiṣyata /
23.28-29.[4]	yatas tv anyakartṛkam iva codyate tasmād yajamāno gāyet /
23.28-29.[5]	na hy anyo hāvakād agnihotrasya rtvig asti /
23.28-29.[6]	itthaṃ hi śrūyate /
23.28-29.[7]	agnihotrasya yajñakrator eka ṛtvig iti /
23.28-29.[8]	yac cedaṃ yajuḥ kam aham asmi kaṃ mameti tad yājamānam iti niścetuṃ yuktam /
23.28-29.[9]	tatraitad yajur uktvā geye iti samānakartṛkatvaśravaṇād eva sāmagānasya yājamānatvaṃ sidhyati /
23.28-29.[10]	asya sāmagānakālavikalpasya vyavasthayā grahaṇaṃ yuktam /
23.28-29.[11]	anyasmin hotari pūrvaḥ kālas svayaṃhome para iti /
23.28-29.[12]	asti hi kadā cit svayaṃhomo 'pi /
23.28-29.[13]	svayaṃ parvaṇi juhuyād iti svayam ahatavāsā yajamāno 'gnihotrañ juhuyād iti ca /
23.28-29.[14]	kimartham agnyādheyasya dakṣiṇā vidhāsyaṃs tābhyaḥ pūrvam eva saśeṣam agnyādheyam avasthāpyāgnihotraṃ sasāmagānakrameṇa vihitavān iti cet saśeṣe 'py agnyādheye saty apratīkṣya pavamāneṣṭim agnihotraṃ hotavyam iti jñāpanārtham //
23.30.[1]	ṣaḍ dvādaśa vā caturviṃśatir vā gāvo 'gnyādheyasya dakṣiṇās syuḥ /
23.30.[2]	kathan na samuccayo gṛhyate /
23.30.[3]	pṛthak pṛthag āsāṃ vacanāt /
23.30.[4]	samuccaye 'bhīṣṭe sati dvicatvāriṃśad ity ucyeta /
23.30.[5]	agnyādheyagrahaṇam agnihotraprasaṅganivṛttyartham //
23.30.[6]	aśvaś ca vānaḍvāṃś ca vā ṣaḍādibhis samuccīyeta //
23.31.[1]	bahuvidhan dravyaṃ gavāśvamahiṣamaṇisuvarṇavrīhiyavabhūmyādi deyam /
23.31.[2]	pūrvoktā dakṣiṇā nityāḥ /
23.31.[3]	ayam āḍhyaviṣayo vidhiḥ /
23.31.[4]	yady āḍhyas syān na pūrvoktābhir eva tuṣyet /
23.31.[5]	bahuvidhan dravyam anyad api phalasamṛddhaye dadyād ity arthaḥ //
23.32.[1]	aparimitasaṃkhyātaṃ dravyan deyam /
23.32.[2]	bahusaṃkhyasya dravyasya dānārtham idam uktam /
23.32.[3]	tad dhi dussaṃkhyānatvād aparimitam iti vaktuṃ śakyam /
23.32.[4]	adhastanād vidher asya ko bhedaḥ /
23.32.[5]	taj jātiviṣayam idaṃ vyaktiviṣayam iti //
23.32.[6]	atha vaikavākyatayaiva vyākhyeyam /
23.32.[7]	bahu dravyan deyan dātuśakyaṃ yuktaṃ yasya vidyeta tena pūrvoktās saṃkhyā anādṛtyāparimitaṃ bahusaṃkhyan dravyan deyam iti /
23.32.[8]	asminn api vyākhyāne napuṃsakaliṅgopādānād evādyagavām api dānaṃ sidhyati //
23.33.[1]	yāvatīs tāvatīr iti cchāndasau śabdau /
23.33.[2]	yāvatyas saṃvatsarasya rātrayas tāvatyo deyāḥ /
23.33.[3]	śaktaś cet pūrvaṃ pakṣatrayam atikramyemam āśrayeta //
23.34.[1]	āgnyādheyikasyāgneyasya puroḍāśasyeḍānta iḍāsaṃbaddhe karmaṇi samāpte sahasram api gavān dadyād ity eke yājñikās samāmananti /
23.34.[2]	atha vā //
23.35.[1]	yo daridraṣ ṣaḍ api gā dātun na śaknoti tasyāgnyādheyābhāvaprasaṅga idam ucyate /
23.35.[2]	anāḍhyas sann agnīn ādadhāna ekām api gān dadyād iti paiṅgakaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vidadhāti /
23.35.[3]	tasmād ekayāpi gavāgnīn ādadhīta /
23.35.[4]	naiva daridratāṃ vyapadiśya nādadhīta //
23.36.[1]	anāḍhyatāhetukaṃ dakṣiṇāhrāsaṃ pūrvasmād vākyād upalabhya mīmāṃsakānāñ ca mukhād asamartho 'pi sarvāṅgopasaṃhāre nityaṃ karmānutiṣṭhed iti śrutvāgnyādheyādīni karmāṇy adakṣiṇāny api prayuyukṣamānānān daridratarāṇān nirbhartsanam idaṃ kriyate /
23.36.[2]	atra cāgnyādheyaśabdo gośabdaś ca viśeṣavācināv api santau pratipādyārthānurodhāya sāmānyasyopalakṣakau gṛhyete /
23.36.[3]	tatrāgnyādheyaśabdas sarveṣāṃ vaidikānāṃ karmaṇām upalakṣakas sarvadakṣiṇānāñ ca gośabdaḥ /
23.36.[4]	evaṃ yojyam /
23.36.[5]	anagnyādheyam eva ca tad bhavati yasmin karmaṇi gaur na dīyate dakṣiṇā na dīyate /
23.36.[6]	na hi dakṣiṇānyair aṅgais tulyā pravartata ṛtvigānamanārthatvāt /
23.36.[7]	manuś ca bhagavān avocat /
23.36.[8]	indriyāṇi yaśas svargam āyuḥ kīrtiṃ prajāṃ paśūn /
23.36.[9]	hanty alpadakṣiṇo yajñas tasmān nālpadhano yajed //
23.36.[10]	iti /
23.36.[11]	liṅgañ ca dṛśyate /
23.36.[12]	dakṣiṇās svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayantīti //
24.1.[1]	pravargyo nāma somāṅgabhūtaḥ kaś cit kriyāviśeṣaḥ /
24.1.[2]	tasya tāvat pūrvam eva codanā kṛtā pravargyopasadbhyāñ carantīti /
24.1.[3]	prathame some tu tasyānityatvaṃ śrutyantarasiddham avagamayitun tadaṅgabhūtāni sāmāni tatrāvihitāni /
24.1.[4]	tāni vidhitsur ācāryaḥ pratijānāti /
24.1.[5]	pravargye sāmnāṃ liṅgataḥ paravacanataś ca samupasthitānāṃ gānasya kālam upadekṣyāmaḥ //
24.2.[1]	pravargyam ārabhamāṇeṣu yajñopavīty ācānto vedyutkarāv antareṇāsīnaṃ hotāram apareṇa parītya gharmam abhimukho gharmasyaiva dakṣiṇata upaviśya madantībhir nāma gārhapatye taptābhir adbhir vāmadevyena mārjanaṃ kurute /
24.2.[2]	kim anādeśād udgātā /
24.2.[3]	naivam /
24.2.[4]	uttarasmād vākyāt prastotety avagamyatām //
24.3.[1]	taṃ kṛtaśāntikaṃ yadādhvaryur evaṃ saṃpreṣyati tat tadāprabhṛti vakṣyamāṇāni sāmāni gāyati /
24.3.[2]	hotṛbrahmasaṃpraiṣavacanam atrānarthakam /
24.3.[3]	nānarthakaṃ brahmaṇā prasave kṛte hotrā copakrānte 'bhīṣṭave gānārambha iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
24.3.[4]	atha vā pravargyacodanāyām avidhānāt sāmnām anityatvaṃ kaś cid āśaṅketa /
24.3.[5]	tannirāsārtham asaṃśayanityābhyāṃ brahmahotṛpraiṣābhyāṃ prastotṛsaṃpraiṣasya sahavacanam //
24.3.[6]	brahma jajñānam ity ṛcy etayos sāmnoḥ pūrvaṃ sāma trir gāyati //
24.4.[1]	mahāvīre prathamam ājyenājyamāne śārṅgaṃ gāyati /
24.4.[2]	trīṇi śārṅgāṇi /
24.4.[3]	teṣām anyatamaṃ gāyati /
24.4.[4]	nanv asati kāraṇe prathamātikramaṇam anyāyyam /
24.4.[5]	satyam etat /
24.4.[6]	asti tv iha kāraṇaṃ yat brahma jajñānam prattāyām iti vākyayoḥ pūrvagrahaṇam uttaranivṛttyarthaṃ karoti /
24.4.[7]	tena śārṅgāṇām aniyamas sidhyati /
24.4.[8]	atha vā triṣu pravargyadivaseṣu trīṇi krameṇa geyāni /
24.4.[9]	punar apy evam eva caturthādiṣv api vidyamāneṣv āvarteran /
24.4.[10]	evaṃ yātayāmadoṣaparihāras saṃbhavataḥ kṛto 'pi bhavati /
24.4.[11]	atha vā yāvantaḥ pravargyās tāṃs tredhā vibhajyaikaikasmin bhāge krameṇaikaikaṃ gāyet /
24.4.[12]	evaṃ saṃbhavato yathāsaṃkhyam anugṛhītaṃ bhavati //
24.5.[1]	rukmaśabdas suvarṇe cāsti rajate ca /
24.5.[2]	rukme mahāvīrasyādhastād upadhīyamāne śukraṃ gāyati /
24.5.[3]	upadhāya rukmaṃ vādhūlakās saṃpreṣyanti /
24.5.[4]	tathā sati pūrvam eva saṃpraiṣāc chukraṃ geyam /
24.5.[5]	tatra kiṃ prāthamyāc chukran trir geyam uta prāthamyañ jahad api brahmajajñānīyam eva trir geyam /
24.5.[6]	taddharma trirgānam iti /
24.5.[7]	atra brūmaḥ /
24.5.[8]	na śukram avidhes trir geyan nāprathamaṃ brahmajajñānīyan trirgānasyeha prathamottamadharmatvāvagamāt /
24.5.[9]	kiṃ punas sakṛd eva dve api /
24.5.[10]	naivam /
24.5.[11]	trirgāne vihite sakṛd gātum ayuktatvāt /
24.5.[12]	kā punar gatiḥ /
24.5.[13]	iyaṃ gatiḥ /
24.5.[14]	yathā śukran tathā brahmajajñānīyam api pūrvam eva saṃpraiṣād geyam iti /
24.5.[15]	asya hi śārṅgādivad avayavakarmabhir na saṃbandho 'sti /
24.5.[16]	evaṃ kṛte na bhūyān vidhyatikramaḥ kṛto bhavati /
24.5.[17]	iyad eva hy atra vihitād bhidyate yad asaṃpraiṣaṃ sāmadvayaṃ gīyata iti /
24.5.[18]	vidhikramaś ca sāmnāṃ saṃbhavann evam anugṛhīto bhavati /
24.5.[19]	prāthamyañ ca brahmajajñānīyasyātyaktaṃ bhavati /
24.5.[20]	anaṅgam asya prāthamyaṃ śukratṛtīyavat tyajyatām apīti cen na /
24.5.[21]	aṅgam evāsya prāthamyaṃ prathamavihitatvāc chukrādivac ca karmaviśeṣasaṃbandhenāvidhānāt /
24.5.[22]	nanu saṃpraiṣapūrvakatvam asyaivan tyaktaṃ bhavati /
24.5.[23]	na saṃpraiṣapūrvakatvaṃ prāthamyavad asyaiva viśeṣadharmaḥ /
24.5.[24]	sādhāraṇo 'yam eṣāṃ sarveṣām api /
24.5.[25]	saugatyā tyajyata iti nāyuktaṃ śukrasyeva //
24.6.[1]	abhir atroparibhāktve vartate /
24.6.[2]	uttarasmin rukme mahāvīrasyopari dhīyamāne candraṃ gāyati //
24.7.[1]	gharmo mahāvīraḥ /
24.7.[2]	tasyendhane dīpane kriyamāṇe gharmasya tanū ca gharmavrate ca gāyati /
24.7.[3]	nanv anyatra samuccaye caśabdo dṛśyate /
24.7.[4]	yathāgneś ca śraiṣṭhyaṃ somasya ca vratam iti /
24.7.[5]	iha caśabdābhāvān na samuccayo yujyate /
24.7.[6]	kathaṃ punar bhavān manyate /
24.7.[7]	uttaraṃ sāmadvayaṃ pūrveṇa vikalpyata iti /
24.7.[8]	yady evaṃ bhavatāpi nānanditavyam adoṣo me pakṣa iti /
24.7.[9]	anyatra hi vikalpe vāśabdo dṛśyate /
24.7.[10]	yathā kakubhaṃ vā kāvaṃ veti /
24.7.[11]	tad atra vāśabdādarśanād vikalpo 'pi na yujyate /
24.7.[12]	kiñ ca na prāyeṇa vāśabdādibhir lakṣaṇair vinā vikalpo dṛṣṭaḥ /
24.7.[13]	dṛṣṭas tu samuccayo vinā caśabdādibhiḥ /
24.7.[14]	yathā rathantaran dairghaśravasan naudhasaṃ samantam ābhīśavaṃ yaudhājayam iti hotur brahmaṇa ājye iti ca /
24.7.[15]	tasmāt samuccaya evātra niścitaḥ //
24.8.[1]	rucite gharme gharmasya rocanaṃ gāyati /
24.8.[2]	kadā punar ayaṃ rucito bhavati /
24.8.[3]	yadā vadanti rucito gharma iti //
24.9.[1]	rauhiṇau nāma dvau puroḍāśau /
24.9.[2]	tayoḥ pūrvasmin hūyamāne rājanaṃ gāyati //
24.10.[1]	gavi vatsenopasṛṣṭāyān dhenu vā kakubhaṃ vā gāyati //
24.11.[1]	prattāyāṃ gavi gaur dhayatīty asyām ṛci ye dve śyāvāśve tayoḥ pūrvaṃ gāyati //
24.12.[1]	payasi duhyamāne dohādohīyaṃ gāyati /
24.12.[2]	kiṃ śārṅgavad dohādohīyayor apy aniyamaḥ /
24.12.[3]	nainayor aniyamaḥ /
24.12.[4]	na hi śārṅgavad enayor liṅgatas sāmyam asti /
24.12.[5]	viśeṣaviniyoge hi liṅgaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhavati tac cottarasminn evāsti /
24.12.[6]	uttarayor vidhānayoḥ payograhaṇaṃ kariṣyati /
24.12.[7]	atraiva na karoti /
24.12.[8]	yasmād āharaṇam āsecanañ ca bahūnām api dravyāṇāṃ saṃbhavati /
24.12.[9]	dohanan tu payasa eva nānyasya saṃbhavati /
24.12.[10]	agnivāyuravibhyaś ca trayaṃ brahma sanātanam /
24.12.[11]	dudoha yajñasiddhyartham ṛgyajussāmalakṣaṇam //
24.12.[12]	ityādidarśanād aparihāro 'yam iti cen na tasya prayogasya gauṇatvāt /
24.12.[13]	mukhyo hi dohaśabdaḥ payoviṣaya eva vijñātavyo 'viśiṣṭāyān dohanacodanāyāṃ paya iti lokavedayoḥ pratīyamānatvāt //
2.4.13.[1]	yasmin kāle paya āhriyamāṇaṃ bhavati sa kālaḥ payaāhriyamāṇaḥ /
2.4.13.[2]	nanv evam āhriyamāṇapaya iti prāpnoti /
2.4.13.[3]	satyam etat /
2.4.13.[4]	viśeṣaṇaṃ bahuvrīhau pūrvan nipatati /
2.4.13.[5]	vivakṣāvaśena tu viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvasyāniyamo dṛśyate /
2.4.13.[6]	yathā loke brāhmaṇagṛhastho gṛhasthabrāhmaṇas taskaravṛṣalo vṛṣalataskara iti /
2.4.13.[7]	yathā ca vede taruṇadarbhā darbhataruṇāś [śrotriyamahārājā] mahārājaśrotriyā iti /
2.4.13.[8]	tadvad atrāpi payaāhriyamāṇenājyan dadhi vety anayā vivakṣayā payo viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati /
2.4.13.[9]	payaāhriyamāṇe kāle payo gāyati /
2.4.13.[10]	aparam matam /
2.4.13.[11]	nāyaṃ samāsaḥ /
2.4.13.[12]	payo 'trāharatikarma /
2.4.13.[13]	tataḥ paya iti dvitīyā /
2.4.13.[14]	nanv anabhihiteṣu karmādiṣu dvitīyādayo bhavanti /
2.4.13.[15]	satyam etat /
2.4.13.[16]	na tv iha kārakam abhihitaṃ mantavyam /
2.4.13.[17]	bhāva evāhriyamāṇaśabdenābhihita iti kalpyam /
2.4.13.[18]	ayan tv atra doṣaḥ /
2.4.13.[19]	sakarmakasya dhātor bhāvotpattir abhyupagatā bhavati /
2.4.13.[20]	aparam matam /
2.4.13.[21]	paya iti saptamyantaś śabdaś chandovad iti /
2.4.13.[22]	ayam arthaḥ /
2.4.13.[23]	payasy āhriyamāṇe payo gāyatīti /
2.4.13.[24]	atrāpy ayan doṣaḥ /
2.4.13.[25]	yathā prattāyām iti vākye pūrvavākyāvasthitasyaiva gośabdasyānuvartanenārthas siddha evam etadvākyāvasthitasyaiva payaśśabdasyānuvartanenārthasiddhāv uttarasmin vākye payograhaṇaṃ vyarthaṃ bhavet /
2.4.13.[26]	tasmād uktas samāsapakṣa eva sādhīyān /
2.4.13.[27]	kiñ ca gharmotsādyamāna iti vakṣyati /
2.4.13.[28]	tatra tāvad avaśyam abhyupagantavyas samāsa iti /
2.4.13.[29]	yat tatra lakṣaṇaṃ tad evātrāpi bhavati //
24.14.[1]	mahāvīre payasy āsicyamāne sindhu gāyati /
24.14.[2]	sindhuṣāma sindhu /
24.14.[3]	triḥ paya āsicyate /
24.14.[4]	sāmāpi kin trir geyam /
24.14.[5]	atra brūmaḥ /
24.14.[6]	gavy upasṛṣṭāyām iti gavādhikāre vihitāni sāmāni gavyenaiva payasā saṃbanddhum arhanti /
24.14.[7]	prathamam eva hi gavyam āsicyate dvitīyam ājan tṛtīyam ubhayaṃ saṃsṛṣṭam /
24.14.[8]	iti sakṛd eva gānaṃ siddham //
24.15.[1]	śaphābhyāṃ mahāvīre parigṛhyamāṇe vasiṣṭhasya śaphau gāyati //
24.16.[1]	āhavanīyaṃ prati mahāvīre hriyamāṇe brāhmaṇaspatyaṃ vā vratapakṣau vā gāyati /
24.16.[2]	vratapakṣapakṣe dvau pakṣau /
24.16.[3]	ubhe prātar ubhe sāyam ity ekaḥ pakṣaḥ /
24.16.[4]	pūrvaṃ prātar uttaraṃ sāyam ity ekaḥ /
24.16.[5]	uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ kimavalambanaḥ /
24.16.[6]	ekena dvayor vikalpas satyāṃ gatau na yuktataraḥ /
24.16.[7]	śakyate cainayoḥ kālāpekṣayā vyavasthā kartuṃ sā ceha viśeṣato yuktā /
24.16.[8]	yataḥ pūrvam ahnas sāma rātrer uttaram /
24.16.[9]	ahar vai pūrvāhṇo rātrir aparāhṇa iti śrūyata ity etad avalambanam /
24.16.[10]	yā prāṇāpānayor ṛk sā tayā gītyā yuktā vratapakṣāv apy anusarpati /
24.16.[11]	ke cit tu vratapakṣāv anṛcāv evecchanti /
24.16.[12]	tatra yuktataram āstheyam /
24.16.[13]	kiṃ vā saṃśayitasevanayeti brāhmaṇaspatyam eva geyam //
24.17.[1]	pravargye hute 'śvinor vrate gāyati //
24.18.[1]	uttarasmin rauhiṇe puroḍāśe hūyamāne rauhiṇakaṃ gāyati //
24.19.[1]	gharmotsādyamāne kāla ārūḍhavad āṅgirasaṃ vā kāvaṃ vā trir gāyati /
24.19.[2]	dve kāve /
24.19.[3]	tayoḥ katarad geyam /
24.19.[4]	uttaraṃ geyaṃ kāvaśabdenānyatropāttatvāt /
24.19.[5]	tāsu kāvaṃ kāvam antyam iti /
24.19.[6]	sāmānyacodanāyāṃ hi prasiddhagrahaṇan nyāyyam /
24.19.[7]	ayam eva nyāya aukṣṇorandhrādiṣv api //
24.20.[1]	pūrvavac chāntiṃ kṛtvā prapadanavartmanā niṣkramyopasadi saṃsthitāyām utkare tiṣṭhan subrahmaṇyām āhūya yathārthaṃ yathāprayojanam eti /
24.20.[2]	prayojanavaśena gacchatīty arthaḥ /
24.20.[3]	atraiva kartavyasyottarasyāpi karmaṇo vidyamānatvāt tadavirodhena dūragamanābhāvārthaṃ yathā[rtha]grahaṇam /
24.20.[4]	nanūpasadante subrahmaṇyāhvānaṃ subrahmaṇyakartṛkaṃ pūrvam eva vihitam /
24.20.[5]	tasyaiva kim idaṃ subrahmaṇyāhvānasya prastotṛkartṛkatvaṃ vikalpena vidhīyata utānyad idaṃ prastotus subrahmaṇyāhvānaṃ vidhīyate /
24.20.[6]	atra brūmaḥ /
24.20.[7]	nedam ubhayam apy avakalpate /
24.20.[8]	pūrvasya samākhyāprāptakartṛparityāgo doṣaḥ /
24.20.[9]	uttarasya niruktām aniruktām ity avacane 'nyataraniścayāśakteḥ prayogo 'prasiddhiḥ /
24.20.[10]	kaḥ punar adoṣaḥ pakṣaḥ /
24.20.[11]	ime brūmahe /
24.20.[12]	ṣoḍaśa rtvijas somasya vihitāḥ /
24.20.[13]	teṣāṃ yo yasmin karmaṇi śrutyādibhiḥ kāraṇair viniyujyate sa tan nirvartayati /
24.20.[14]	tatra yaṣ ṣoḍaśa puruṣān ṛtvigguṇayuktān nopalabdhuṃ śaknoti tenāpy āvaśyako mā hāyi somayāga ity evamartham eko 'pi bahūny ārtvijyāni kartuṃ śakyāni kuryād iti yājñikair niścitam /
24.20.[15]	tasmin viṣaye prastotur asyaiva subrahmaṇyayā samānakartṛkatvaṃ syāt /
24.20.[16]	mā bhūd anyasyeti jñāpanārthaṃ prastotradhikāre subrahmaṇyāhvānam idaṃ kīrtitam /
24.20.[17]	evañ cet saṃsthitāyām ityādi padacatuṣṭayam anarthakam /
24.20.[18]	nānarthakaṃ pūrvavihitam evedaṃ subrahmaṇyāhvānam anūdyate nāparaṃ vidhīyata ity etadavabodhanārthatvāt /
24.20.[19]	yau hi deśakālau pūrvavihitayā subrahmaṇyayā saha vihitau tāv evātrāpy ucyete /
24.20.[20]	tatra deśakālānanyatvāt saiveyaṃ subrahmaṇyeti prajñāyate //
25.1.[1]	athānantaraṃ parigāṇāni vakṣyāma upadekṣyāma iti vānuvartayitavyam /
25.1.[2]	yataś caitāni stotrāntarbhāvena na pravartante tataḥ paritas stotrāṇi vartanta iti parigāṇāni bhavanti //
25.2.[1]	prathamam eva tāvat parigāṇāni geyāny ageyānīti vicāryante /
25.2.[2]	yadi hi geyāni syus tadaiva hi vidheyāni /
25.2.[3]	yataś caitāni geyāny ageyānīti saṃśayyante tato vayam manyāmahe /
25.2.[4]	liṅgata evaiṣān dīkṣaṇīyādiṣu pravṛttir na vacanād iti /
25.2.[5]	vacanaprāptau hi satyān na yuktaṃ saṃśayitum /
25.2.[6]	na tāvat parigāṇāni geyāni /
25.2.[7]	kuta iti cen naitāny adhvaryus saṃpreṣyati /
25.2.[8]	yac cādhvaryur geyāni pravargyasāmādīni saṃpreṣyatītītaḥ kāraṇād ity arthaḥ /
25.2.[9]	hetāv api hi dṛṣṭa itiśabdaḥ /
25.2.[10]	yathābhirūpa iti kanyān dadāti /
25.2.[11]	dhanavān iti kanyān dadātīti /
25.2.[12]	idañ cāsya vākyasya dṛṣṭāntatvena laukikaṃ vākyam anūdyate /
25.2.[13]	varṣāsu sūrya udito neti saṃśaye vadanti noditas sūryaḥ kamalāni hi na vikasanti /
25.2.[14]	yatas tāni vikasanty uditas sūrya iti /
25.2.[15]	tadvad idan draṣṭavyam /
25.2.[16]	atraivam arthayogaḥ /
25.2.[17]	yasmād geyāni sāmāny agnyādheyapravargyāgnicayagharmodvāsanāvabhṛtheṣv adhvaryus saṃpreṣyati na ca tārkṣyasāmādīni saṃpreṣyati tasmād etāni na geyānīti /
25.2.[18]	nanv araṇisannidhānādau nādhvaryus saṃpreṣyati gīyanta eva ca sāmāni /
25.2.[19]	tato vipakṣe sadbhāvād ayukto hetur nādhvaryus saṃpreṣyatīti /
25.2.[20]	atra brūmaḥ /
25.2.[21]	yeṣv adhvaryusaṃpraiṣo nāsti tāni sarvāṇi sapakṣabhūtāny evātrābhipreyante /
25.2.[22]	yad dhi gānam astotrāntarbhūtaṃ tat sarvaṃ parigāṇam iti śakyaṃ vaktum /
25.2.[23]	tasmād ghṛtācer āṅgirasasya sāmety evamādīny api tārkṣyasāmādīni vedānīm ageyāny eva saṃvṛttāni /
25.2.[24]	atha vā vācanikam araṇisannidhānādau sāmagānaṃ mantavyam /
25.2.[25]	yas tv ayaṃ vicāro geyāny ageyānīti sa liṅgataḥ pravṛtteṣu tārkṣyasāmādiṣv iti vyākhyāyāṃ vipakṣam ayaṃ hetur nopasarpati //
25.3.[1]	svasmin vā yajñe gāyet /
25.3.[2]	sattre vā gāyed ity arthaḥ /
25.3.[3]	tatra hi yajamānair evārtvijyaṃ kriyate /
25.3.[4]	tataḥ prastotur api sva eva sa yajño bhavati /
25.3.[5]	pūrvam eva hi prastotṛgeyatvaṃ parisāmnām avocāma /
25.3.[6]	vāśabdaḥ pakṣavyāvṛttyarthaḥ /
25.3.[7]	adhastane vākye pratiṣiddhatvāt parisāmnāṃ sattre 'py agānam eva prāptam /
25.3.[8]	sa pakṣo vāśabdena nivartyate /
25.3.[9]	kiṃ punar ayaṃ vikalpārtho na gṛhyate /
25.3.[10]	sattre gāyed vā na veti /
25.3.[11]	atra brūmaḥ /
25.3.[12]	vikalpārthe 'py asmin sati na mahān doṣaḥ /
25.3.[13]	kin tūttarasmin vākye dvau vāśabdau staḥ /
25.3.[14]	tatraikena vikalpe samuccaye vā siddha itarasyāvaśyaṃ pakṣavyāvṛttyarthatā grāhyā /
25.3.[15]	tattulyatvam ṛjv āgatam asya notsraṣṭavyam iti kṛtvā pakṣavyāvṛttyartho 'yan niścitaḥ /
25.3.[16]	tatas sattre nityāni parigāṇāni /
25.3.[17]	apara āha /
25.3.[18]	sva ity agniṣṭomasya prākṛtasyākhyā /
25.3.[19]	evaṃ hi śrūyate /
25.3.[20]	tad āhur na prathamaṃ yajamāno 'tirātreṇa yajeteti /
25.3.[21]	svañ ca hy atimanyate dvau ca yajñakratū /
25.3.[22]	brahma vā agniṣṭomaḥ /
25.3.[23]	brahma vai brāhmaṇasya svam /
25.3.[24]	agniṣṭomañ ca hy atimanyata ukthyañ ca ṣoḍaśinañ ceti /
25.3.[25]	ayaṃ granthas svaśabdam agniṣṭomābhidhāyinam avagamayati /
25.3.[26]	tasmāt sve yajñe gāyed agniṣṭome gāyed ity arthaḥ /
25.3.[27]	evañ ced gāyed ity evāstu na sve yajña iti /
25.3.[28]	prakaraṇād eva hy agniṣṭomasaṃbandhas sidhyati /
25.3.[29]	satyam etat /
25.3.[30]	avadhāraṇārthan tu sve yajña ity uktam /
25.3.[31]	sva eva yajñe gāyen nānyatreti /
25.3.[32]	tatas siddham /
25.3.[33]	nātyagniṣṭomādiṣu na ca vikṛtiṣv iti /
25.3.[34]	iyam anayor jyāyasī vyākhyā //
25.3.[35]	evaṃ sthitam /
25.3.[36]	yas svo yajñas tato 'nyatra na geyānīti /
25.3.[37]	sa pakṣo vāśabdenaikena nivartyate vidhis tv ayam ekena vikalpyate /
25.3.[38]	yaṃ vā puruṣaṃ śreyāṃsaṃ kāmayeta prastotā tasya yajñe gāyed vā na veti /
25.3.[39]	nanv ṛtvijo yajamānasya śreyastvan nityam eva kāmayante /
25.3.[40]	kimarthaṃ viśeṣyate yaṃ ... śreyāṃsaṃ kāmayeteti /
25.3.[41]	atra brūmaḥ /
25.3.[42]	dvividhā yaṣṭāraḥ ye ca phalam abhisandhāya pravartante ye ca kiñ cid anabhisandhāya vihitam avaśyaṃ kartavyam ity eva śuddhena manasā pravartante /
25.3.[43]	tatra ye phalam anabhisandhāya pravartante te 'nyebhyaś śreyāṃso bhavanti /
25.3.[44]	tathā ca bhagavadgītāsu śrūyate /
25.3.[45]	karmaṇy evādhikāras te mā phaleṣu kadā cana /
25.3.[46]	mā karmaphalahetur bhūr mā te saṅgo 'stv akarmaṇi //
25.3.[47]	iti /
25.3.[48]	anāśritaḥ karmaphalaṃ kāryaṃ karma karoti yaḥ /
25.3.[49]	sa sannyāsī ca yogī ca na niragnir na cākriyaḥ //
25.3.[50]	iti ca /
25.3.[51]	tato 'yaṃ vākyārthaḥ /
25.3.[52]	yaṃ śreyāṃsaṃ phalākāṅkṣiṇaṃ kāmayeta manyeta tasyeti /
25.3.[53]	yaṃ lokaś śreyāṃsaṃ kāmayeteti vā yojyam /
25.3.[54]	evan tāvad imāni parigāṇāni sve yajñe nityāni /
25.3.[55]	yas tu śreyān kāmyate tasya yajñe vaikalpikāni bhavanti /
25.3.[56]	tatra punar evaṃ brūmaḥ /
25.3.[57]	ubhayatrāpi nityāny eveti /
25.3.[58]	tata idaṃ varṇyate /
25.3.[59]	samuccaye vāśabdo na vikalpa iti /
25.3.[60]	samuccayaḥ pūrvaṃ vidhim apekṣya kriyate /
25.3.[61]	ayam arthaḥ /
25.3.[62]	yaṃ viśeṣeṇa śreyāṃsaṃ kāmayeta tasya ca yajñe gāyen na kevalaṃ sve yajña eveti /
25.3.[63]	evañ ca sati yad yajñasya śrutaṃ phalaṃ tasyotkarṣakarāṇi parigāṇānīti mantavyam /
25.3.[64]	tataḥ phalotkarṣād yajamānaś śreyān bhavati //
25.4.[1]	dīkṣaṇīyāyām iṣṭau tārkṣyasāmanī gāyet //
25.5.[1]	prāyaṇīyāyām iṣṭau pravad bhārgavaṃ gāyet //
25.6.[1]	ātithyāyām iṣṭau preṣṭhaṃ va ity asyāṃ yad auśanan tad gāyet /
25.6.[2]	auśanam ity ukte prasiddham auśanan tat syād iti matvedam ṛcā viśeṣyate /
25.6.[3]	tatas sabhavāmadevyakāvādiṣu siddhaṃ prasiddhagrahaṇam //
25.7.[1]	pravargye ca yathāliṅgaṃ yāni liṅgavanti sāmāni tair upatiṣṭheta /
25.7.[2]	kāni punar atra liṅgavanti /
25.7.[3]	yāni gharmaśabdavanti navānugānādīni trīṇy uttaraṃ vaiśvānaravratam udyan lokān ityādīni /
25.7.[4]	kadā punar imāni gātavyāni /
25.7.[5]	ūrdhvaṃ gharmavratābhyāṃ prāg gharmasya rocanāt /
25.7.[6]	tadaiva hy eṣām asty avasaraḥ /
25.7.[7]	yady eṣām apariniṣṭhite gāne rucito gharma syād gīyamānaṃ sāma samāpyaiva gharmasya rocanaṃ gāyet /
25.7.[8]	tatra trirabhyāso gātuḥ prāṅmukhatvaṃ sthānāsanayor aniyamaś ca parigāṇadharmā vakṣyante /
25.7.[9]	pravargyasāmāny udaṅmukhenāsīnena sakṛd geyāni /
25.7.[10]	prathamottamayor eva hi trirabhyāsaḥ /
25.7.[11]	tatraiṣāṃ liṅgād gīyamānān navānugānādīnāṃ parigāṇatvāviśeṣāt trirabhyāsādayo dharmāḥ prāpnuvanti /
25.7.[12]	teṣān nivartanārthaṃ gāyed ity anuvartamānenaivārthasiddhau satyām apy upatiṣṭheteti śabdāntareṇa vidhiḥ kriyate /
25.7.[13]	tataś śabdāntaracoditatvād dharmāntaragrahaṇam eṣāṃ siddham /
25.7.[14]	tasmān nityaiḥ pravargyasāmabhis tulyadharmataiṣāṃ bhavati /
25.7.[15]	asminn arthe 'nyad api jñāpakam udvāsanādhikāre 'vādiṣma /
25.7.[16]	iha gharmasyādityasaṃskṛtatvād asmadbrāhmaṇe tad yat tad yajñasya śiro 'cchidyateti so 'sāv ādityas sa u eva pravargya iti darśanād vrataśukriyāṇy api liṅgavanti bhavanti //
25.8.[1]	itikaraṇas samuccayārthaḥ /
25.8.[2]	trīṇy etāny upasatsu gāyet /
25.8.[3]	yad uktaṃ śārṅgeṣu tat somavrateṣv api tulyam /
25.8.[4]	kiñ ca tṛtīyasya somavratasyāgnīṣomapraṇayane vidhāsyamānasya yātayāmadoṣas sati saṃbhave parihārya iti kṛtvā dve eveha somavrate upādāya tayoḥ pūrvaṃ paurvāhṇikyām upasadi geyam uttaram aparāhṇikyām ity ayam apy atraikaḥ pakṣaḥ /
25.8.[5]	ayam eva ca tebhyo 'bhimatataraḥ //
25.9.[1]	sadas sadasopatiṣṭheta /
25.9.[2]	kasmin kāle /
25.9.[3]	mīyamāne tasmin /
25.9.[4]	mīyamāna iti vikaraṇavyatyayaś chāndasaḥ /
25.9.[5]	bahusthūṇaṃ sadaḥ /
25.9.[6]	tatra yā sthūṇā prathamam mīyate tasyāṃ sāma gāyet /
25.9.[7]	audumbarī kaiś cit prathamam mīyate kaiś cin na /
25.9.[8]	tatra ke cid vadanti /
25.9.[9]	yady apy anyā sthūṇā prathamaṃ mīyeta tām atikramyaudumbaryām eva sāma geyam /
25.9.[10]	saiva hi sthūṇānām abhyarhiteti /
25.9.[11]	guravas tu bruvate /
25.9.[12]	sado'ṅgam etat sāma na tatsthūṇāṅgam /
25.9.[13]	yadā ca sado mīyate so 'sya kāla ity uktam /
25.9.[14]	tatra yathā loke śālāyāṃ mīyamānāyāṃ maṅgalaṃ giro viprān vācayatety ukte prathamasthūṇāyām eva mīyamānāyāṃ vācayanti śālā mīyata iti cāvagacchanti tadvad atrāpi sadasaḥ prathamāyām eva sthūṇāyāṃ mīyamānāyāṃ sado mīyata ity avagamya sāmaitad geyam iti //
25.10.[1]	havirdhāne anasī havirdhānābhyām upatiṣṭheta /
25.10.[2]	kadeti ced yadaite svasthānaṃ prāpte tadopatiṣṭheta //
25.11.[1]	yadāgniṃ praṇayanti tadāgner vrataṃ gāyet /
25.11.[2]	praṇīyamāne gāyed ity arthaḥ /
25.11.[3]	ke cid agniṃ praṇīya havirdhāne pravartya sado minvanti /
25.11.[4]	tatra sāmnāṃ siddhakramavighātaḥ /
25.11.[5]	evam anyatrāpy upalakṣya karmakramānurodhaḥ kāryaḥ //
25.12.[1]	yadāgnīdhrīyam agniñ ca somañ ca praṇayanti tadāgner vratañ caiva yat tṛtīyaṃ somavrataṃ tac ca gāyet /
25.12.[2]	praṇīyamānayor gāyed ity arthaḥ /
25.12.[3]	aparaṃ vyākhyānam //
25.13.[1]	pavitre soma āsicyamāne somaḥ pavata ity asyām ṛci yāni prathamād ūrdhvan trīṇi somasāmāni tāni gāyet /
25.13.[2]	anuvartamānena siddhe gāyed ity anarthakam /
25.13.[3]	nānarthakam asya sāmatrayasya nityatvāvagamanārthatvāt //
25.14-16.[1]	ahar ahas sattre saṃsthite 'hani paścād gārhapatyaṃ gārhapatyasya paścād vartamānas sattrasya rddhi gāyet /
25.14-16.[2]	gāyed ity asyāpi nityatvārtham //
25.14-16.[3]	ahīneṣv ekāheṣu ca prāk chvassutyāyās subrahmaṇyāyāḥ paścād eva gārhapatyasya vartamāno yajñasārathi gāyet /
25.14-16.[4]	atha vā vākyadvaye 'pi gārhapatyasyeti vaktavye dvitīyaprayogād gārhapatyam īkṣamāṇas tasyaiva paścād iti vyākhyeyam /
25.14-16.[5]	nanu yajñasārathi vidhāya somasāmāni vidhātavyāni kriyākramānurodhāya /
25.14-16.[6]	satyam etat /
25.14-16.[7]	kin tv ahīnaikāheṣv iti vacanam asya sattreṣv abhāvārtham /
25.14-16.[8]	tatra yadi kriyākramānurodhenāyaṃ vidhir akariṣyata somasāmnām apy abhāvas sattreṣv āśaṅkyeta /
25.14-16.[9]	tatparihārārtham atrāyaṃ vidhiḥ kṛtaḥ /
25.14-16.[10]	evam api sattrārthaṃ sattrasya rddhinaḥ pūrvam ahīnaikāhārthaṃ yajñasārathi vidhātavyam /
25.14-16.[11]	satyam etad api /
25.14-16.[12]	prāk chvassutyām iti tu yajñasārathinaḥ kālo vihitaḥ /
25.14-16.[13]	sa eva vakṣyamāṇānāṃ rākṣoghnānām apīṣyate na tu sa yas sattrasya rddhinaḥ kālas saṃsthite 'hanīti /
25.14-16.[14]	tatsiddhyarthaṃ rākṣoghnasannikarṣeṇa yajñasārathi vidhīyate //
25.14-16.[15]	itiśabdas samuccayārthaḥ /
25.14-16.[16]	eteṣām ṛṣīṇāṃ rākṣoghnāny etair dṛṣṭāni prāk chvassutyāyā gāyet /
25.14-16.[17]	dvayor anayor vākyayor ahar ahar ity anuvartate /
25.14-16.[18]	kiṃ punar asmin vākye paścād gārhapatyam ity anuvartate /
25.14-16.[19]	nānuvartate /
25.14-16.[20]	yadi hy anuvarteta pūrvasmin vākye paścād [eva] gārhapatyam iti vacanam anarthakaṃ bhavet /
25.14-16.[21]	tatrāpi hi sattrasyarddhivākyād evānuvarteta /
25.14-16.[22]	tathā sidhyati /
25.14-16.[23]	yat tatra paścād eva gārhapatyam iti vadati taj jñāpayati /
25.14-16.[24]	nānuvṛttir asyeti /
25.14-16.[25]	tasmād aniyatadeśāni rākṣoghnāni /
25.14-16.[26]	kiṃ punas sarveṣāṃ rākṣoghnānām etadṛṣidṛṣṭānām atra gānam āho svit trayāṇām eva /
25.14-16.[27]	sarveṣām iti brūmaḥ /
25.14-16.[28]	yadi hi trayāṇām evaiṣiṣyata trīṇīty avakṣyata somasāmasv iva /
25.14-16.[29]	sattrārthāni caitāni /
25.14-16.[30]	tad uttarasmin vākye vivariṣyate /
25.14-16.[31]	aparo mārgaḥ //
25.17.[1]	tāni rākṣoghnāni gīyamānāni sarvān yajamānān sapatnīkān sañśrāvayet sārdhaṃ śrāvayet /
25.17.[2]	yajamānabahutvasaṃbandhād vartata eva rākṣoghnāni /
25.17.[3]	sattrādhikārasya ca sattrasyarddhivākyād anuvṛtter abhāvānavagamād yajamānān ity etāvatā siddhe sarvān ity anarthakam /
25.17.[4]	nānarthakaṃ sarvān samīpam ānīya gāyed ity etadarthatvāt /
25.17.[5]	sarvaśabdas saṃbhūyavartiṣv api hi saṃbhavati //
25.18.[1]	anūbandhyeṣu ca vakṣyamāṇeṣu yathāliṅgaṃ sāmāni gāyet /
25.18.[2]	katham atra liṅgopādānam iti ced idam ucyate //
25.19.[1]	aukṣṇorandhraṃ gāyed ukṣaṇy anūbandhye sati /
25.19.[2]	anūbandhyadravyāṇāṃ sāmnāñ cābhidhānasārūpyaṃ liṅgatvenopādīyate /
25.19.[3]	prathamam aukṣṇorandhraṃ gāyet /
25.19.[4]	kāraṇam iha kāvavidhāv avādi //
25.20.[1]	trayāṇām anyatamaṃ gāyet /
25.20.[2]	prasiddhir iha niyamahetur uktaḥ /
25.20.[3]	sa sarveṣv apy asti /
25.20.[4]	prāthamyasya vā hetutvaṃ śārṅgavidhāv uktam /
25.20.[5]	vṛṣabheti liṅgād ārṣabhasyopādānan na kevalam abhidhānasārūpyād eva //
25.21.[1]	vāśe iti ca liṅgād asyopādānam //
25.22.[1]	ṛṣabham eva viśeṣeṇonnatakakudam unnata iti vadanti /
25.22.[2]	yathā bhīmasenaṃ bhīma iti /
25.22.[3]	tato 'trāpy abhidhānasārūpyam eva liṅgaṃ bhavati //
25.23.[1]	jātaretaskam ukṣāṇam ṛṣabhaṃ pūrṇayauvanam /
25.23.[2]	vidyād vaśāṃ vṛṣārūḍhāṃ bṛhatkakudam unnatam //
25.23.[3]	ity ukṣādibhiś śabdaiś codita upādīyate gaur ajo vānyo vā yasmiṃs tasminn aukṣṇorandhrādīni /
25.23.[4]	yas tv ajaśabdena codita upādīyata ukṣa rṣabho vaśonnato vā tasminn ājīkam iti /
25.23.[5]	yadi tūbhayaśabdacoditas syād ajarṣabho 'javaśeti tatra jāteḥ prādhānyād ājīkam eva /
25.23.[6]	aparaṃ matam /
25.23.[7]	dviśabdacodite dve api sāmanī samuccinuyād iti //
25.24.[1]	paśubhyo 'nyo 'pi dravyaviśeṣo 'nūbandhyasthānam āpadyate /
25.24.[2]	tathābhāve saty āmikṣāyāṃ payo gāyet /
25.24.[3]	iha nidhanagataṃ liṅgam //
25.25.[1]	iha sāmagataṃ liṅgam abhidhānasārūpyam ca //
25.26.[1]	iha ca pūrvavat //
25.28.[1]	āvika iti svārthe taddhitaprayogaḥ /
25.28.[2]	avau meṣe cānūbandhyayor aurṇāyavaṃ gāyet /
25.28.[3]	ūrṇety avilomanāma /
25.28.[4]	tato 'vir ūrṇāyuḥ /
25.28.[5]	evam ihābhidhānasārūpyasiddhiḥ /
25.28.[6]	avāv evaṃ sidhyatu /
25.28.[7]	kathaṃ meṣe /
25.28.[8]	idam ucyate /
25.28.[9]	avijāter eveyam avāntarajātir yā meṣajātiḥ /
25.28.[10]	yathā paśujāter gojātiḥ /
25.28.[11]	ajajātir iti kuta iti cen meṣasyāpy aviśabdena loke vyavahāradarśanād yajñe ca meṣapaśoḥ praiṣeṣv aviśabdena nirdeśāt /
25.28.[12]	tathā cāśvalāyanīya uktam usro gaur meṣo 'viko hayo 'śva iti /
25.28.[13]	tato meṣeṇa duśśakam anavinā bhavitum /
25.28.[14]	yady evam apeyam āvikam iti smṛter meṣīpayo 'py apeyaṃ bhavati /
25.28.[15]	nāyaṃ paryanuyogaḥ paryāpto bādhitum /
25.28.[16]	apeyam eva meṣīpaya iti hy asmākaṃ siddhāntaḥ /
25.28.[17]	kva cid asya śiṣṭair api dṛṣṭaṃ pānam iti cen nācārasmṛtiviruddhapramāṇaṃ bhavitum utsahate /
25.28.[18]	yathā pānamārasya /
25.28.[19]	tato meṣasyāpy ūrṇāyutvād abhidhānasārūpyād evaurṇāyavam asmin bhavati /
25.28.[20]	sarveṣām anūbandhyasāmnāṃ vidhānād eva siddher yathāliṅgam ity uktam anarthakam /
25.28.[21]	nānarthakam aukṣṇorandhram ukṣaṇīti ca paya āmikṣāyām iti ca liṅgopāditsayā vaco vihita[m] iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
25.28.[22]	siddham anyatrāpi yathāliṅgam upādeyeṣu sāmasu spaṣṭaliṅgānām abhāva īdṛśair api śabdaleśaiś ca liṅgatvaṃ sāmnām avadhārya grahaṇaṃ kāryam /
25.28.[23]	nādityādiṣu paśuṣv adityādidevatyāny adityādiliṅgāni ca na santi sāmānīti viramed iti //
25.29.[1]	iha yajñaprayoge bahuśaḥ prāyaṇatulyam udayanaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dṛṣṭam iti ceṣṭyoś ca prāyaṇīyodayanīyayos tulyarūpatvāt pravadbhārgavasarūpaṃ jāgatam evodvad geyaṃ nānuṣṭubham /
25.29.[2]	iha taittirīyāḥ prāg anūbandhyāyā udayanīyayā caranti //
25.30.[1]	devayajanād gṛhān prati nivṛtto madhya udavasānīyayeṣṭyā yajate /
25.30.[2]	sodavasānīyā nāma /
25.30.[3]	iha ke cid iṣṭitaḥ pratinidhibhūtāṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ juhvati /
25.30.[4]	tasyām api geyam iṣṭipratinidhitvād avirodhāc ca //
25.31.[1]	sautrāmaṇī nāma haviryajñas surāpaśupuroḍāśadravyaḥ /
25.31.[2]	sautrāmaṇyāṃ yā surā tasyāṃ sāṃśānāni sāmāni gāyet /
25.31.[3]	dvividhā sautrāmaṇī /
25.31.[4]	kā cid agnivājapeyādīnāṃ kratūnām aṅgabhūtā /
25.31.[5]	kā cit pṛthag eva kartavyā phalāya /
25.31.[6]	tatra kratvaṅgabhūtāyāṃ yaḥ kratoḥ parigātā sa eva gāyati prastotā /
25.31.[7]	anyasyāṃ tv adhikṛtasya gātur abhāvāt saṃśayaḥ /
25.31.[8]	kim eṣām eva gānārthaṃ kaś cid upādeya uta yajamāna etāni gāyed iti /
25.31.[9]	kim atra prāptam ity ucyate /
25.31.[10]	nāsya saṃśayasya viṣayo 'sti /
25.31.[11]	kratvaṅgabhūtāyām eva hi sautrāmaṇyām imāni vidhīyante kratvadhikārān netarasyām ihādhikārābhāvāt /
25.31.[12]	yathā vakṣyamāṇāni paśubandhasāmāni kratvaṅgabhūteṣv eva paśuṣu bhavanti na nirūḍheṣu tadvat /
25.31.[13]	sāmānīty anarthakam /
25.31.[14]	nānarthakaṃ yathaitāni sāmāni syus tathā gāyed ity etadarthatvāt /
25.31.[15]	udṛgbhāgo hy eṣām aprathamānāṃ śrūyate /
25.31.[16]	tatrāsati yatne yathāpāṭham eva gīyerann iti kṛtvā kṛto 'yaṃ yatnaḥ /
25.31.[17]	tatas siddhaṃ prathamavat saṃpādyottarāṇy api geyānīti /
25.31.[18]	evam apy anuṣaṅganyāyād evāsyārthasya siddher ayaṃ yatno 'narthakaḥ /
25.31.[19]	nānarthako 'nuṣaṅganyāyasyānityatvajñāpanārthatvāt /
25.31.[20]	kim atas sidhyati /
25.31.[21]	anaśnatsaṃhitāyām eṣām anyeṣāñ cānuṣaṅgābhāvas sidhyati /
25.31.[22]	gāyed ity eṣāṃ nityatvārthaṃ somasāmavat //
26.1.[1]	athānantaraṃ paśubandheṣu kratvaṅgabhūteṣu geyāni sāmāny upadekṣyāmaḥ /
26.1.[2]	anūbandhyeṣūpadiṣṭatvād agnīṣomīyasavanapaśvartham idam ucyate //
26.2.[1]	savitṛdevatyāni sāvitrāṇi savitṛdṛṣṭāni ca sāvitrāṇi /
26.2.[2]	sāvitrāṇīty avadhāraṇam iha śakyam /
26.2.[3]	somasāmnān trīṇīti viśeṣaṇāt trīṇy eva hi tāni prathamād ūrdhvaṃ santi /
26.2.[4]	siddhe tu tritve trīṇīti tatra vacanam anyatra bahutvaśrutau sāmnān tritvam eva nāvadhāryam ity etadartham /
26.2.[5]	kiṃ punar ihāśrayaṇīyam /
26.2.[6]	yac chrutan tad āśrayanīyam /
26.2.[7]	bahutvañ ca śrutan nānyat /
26.2.[8]	tato bahūni geyāni /
26.2.[9]	nāsti saṃkhyāniyamaḥ /
26.2.[10]	evañ ced rākṣoghnasāṃśānānām api sarveṣāṃ grahaṇam uktaṃ na sidhyati /
26.2.[11]	śakyatvāt sidhyati /
26.2.[12]	śakyārambhaprasaṅgadoṣāddhi paśuṣv iha sarvagrahaṇapakṣo nirastaḥ /
26.2.[13]	tatas siddham /
26.2.[14]	paśubandheṣu trīṇi catvāri pañceti yathāvasāraṃ sāmāni gāyed iti //

26.7.[34]	kva cit saivobhayasmin /

26.7.[37]	yaddevatyaḥ paśus syāt taddevatyaṃ sāma tasmin gāyet taddṛṣṭaṃ vā /

26.7.[39]	itthaṃ vijñeyam /
26.7.[40]	yā devata rcas saiva sāmna iti /

26.7.[42]	tatas sārasvate pāvakā na iti bhāradvājaṃ gāyet /
26.7.[43]	aindrāgne vācas sāmendrāgnī apād iti /
26.7.[44]	yā saurye /
26.7.[45]	yā ca devatā sāmnaiva stūyate sāpi tasya devatā bhavati /
26.7.[46]	tatas saumya ā soteti gāyet /
26.7.[47]	tataś ca paraṃ tatsadṛśe vāgdevatye /
26.7.[48]	evañ ced yathāliṅgam iti etāvataiva sarvaṃ sidhyati /
26.7.[49]	liṅgenaiva hi devatā jñāyate /

26.7.[51]	nānarthakaṃ yathādevataṃ gānam itarasmān mukhyam iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
26.7.[52]	nanv asaty api yatne 'nukrāntāt prakārāl leśātītāl liṅgād yaddevatyaḥ paśus taddevatyānāṃ taddṛṣṭānāṃ vā sāmnāṃ gānaṃ mukhyaṃ bhavaty eva /
26.7.[53]	tataḥ punar eva yathādevatam ity anarthakam /
26.7.[54]	nānarthakaṃ pratyakṣan taddevatyāśravaṇāt saṃbhave yathā kathañ cid api devatām āśritya tāny eva yāni sāmāni bhavitum utsaheraṃs tāni gāyet tathāpy asaṃbhave yathāliṅgam ity etadarthatvāt /
26.7.[55]	tato 'gnīṣomīye paśāv imam ū ṣv ity āgneyyām ṛci somena dṛṣṭaṃ sāma saumīṣu cāyaṃ vicarṣaṇir hitaḥ pra soma devavītaye pavasva devavītaya ity etāsu yāny agninā dṛṣṭāni tāni gāyet /
26.7.[56]	na hy agnīṣomadevatyāny agnīṣomadṛṣṭāni vā lakṣyante //
26.7.[57]	dṛṣṭvāgnīṣomayoḥ ke cit pṛthak praṇayane stutim /
26.7.[58]	paśāv api tathecchanti na tad icchati no guruḥ //
26.7.[59]	yathā hy avasthitau yāge na hi praṇayane tathā /
26.7.[60]	nidhāyāgnin tatas somaḥ kevalaś ca praṇīyate //
26.7.[61]	tataś ca hotā tatrāgniṃ somañ ca stauti bhedataḥ /
26.7.[62]	sahayāge tatas sādhu sāmak.lptir iyaṃ kṛtā //

26.7.[64]	viśvedevendramaruta indrāgnī savitā tataḥ //

26.7.[66]	siddhāni tatra sāmāni vāg api syāt sarasvatī //
26.8.[1]	teṣāṃ sāmnāṃ yāni paśau vihitāni tāni vapānte vapākarmasamāptau gāyet /
26.8.[2]	mārjanād ūrdhvam ity arthaḥ /
26.8.[3]	iha paśāv ity ekavacanaṃ sāmaviṣayeṣu ca padeṣu yānītyādiṣu bahuvacanaṃ prayuñjāno jñāpayati /
26.8.[4]	pratipaśu sāmabahutvan dhruvam iti /

26.10.[1]	iyaṃ paribhāṣā sarvaparigāṇasādhāraṇā /
26.10.[2]	yad yat karma prati vihitāny etāni tat tat karmāpannas tan taṃ karmadeśaṃ prapannas san yajñopavītavān prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhan vopaviṣṭo vā madhyamayā vācā gāyed imāni parigāṇāni //
