26.12.[4]	atha vā hetau pañcamyarthe caturthī /
26.12.[5]	ekarcānām api trirabhyāse tṛcasādṛśyaṃ bhavati /
26.12.[6]	kimartham idan tṛcepsutāyā iti /
26.12.[7]	ucyate /
26.12.[8]	pūrvan tāvad vākyaṃ santanyādibhir anekarcagītaiḥ kṛtārtham idañ ca tārkṣyasāmādibhir ekarcagītaiḥ /
26.12.[9]	atha yāny ekarceṣu gīyante tṛceṣu ca yathā vāmadevyaṃ rathantaraṃ bṛhad iti teṣu saṃśayas syāt tṛceṣv ekarceṣv iti /
26.12.[10]	tatrāyaṃ vākyaśeṣas tṛcagānasiddhaye nyastaḥ /
26.12.[11]	evam asya yogaḥ /
26.12.[12]	trir gīyanta ekarcās tṛcepsutāyai gauṇatṛcakalpanārtham /
26.12.[13]	asaty eva ca mukhye gauṇam āśrayitavyam /
26.12.[14]	śakyate ca bṛhadrathantaravāmadevyeṣu mukhyam eva tṛcam āśrayitum /
26.12.[15]	tasmāt tṛceṣv evaitāni geyānīti /
26.12.[16]	atha vā santanyādīnām anekarcagītānān tṛcagānasyārthaprāptasyāvidheyatvāt pūrvo vidhir ihāpy agnyādheyavad bṛhadādīnān tṛcagānārthaṃ kalpyaḥ /
26.12.[17]	tṛcepsutāvādas tv ayam anyatrāpy eṣān tṛca ekarca iti saṃśaye tṛcopādānārthan nyasta iti kalpanaṃ samyag bhavati /
26.12.[18]	tataś śāntyādau vāmadevyasya tṛcopādānaṃ sidhyati /
26.12.[19]	santy anṛcāni sāmāni yathā vāco vrate sattrasya rddhīti /
26.12.[20]	santi dvyṛcāni yathātīṣaṅgās tavaśśāvyam iti /
26.12.[21]	santi bahvṛcāni yathā kaśyapavratam ādityavratam ilāndañ ca /
26.12.[22]	pākṣikāni sarvāṇy ekarceṣv evāntarbhavanti /
26.12.[23]	itthaṃ hi kalpanīyam /
26.12.[24]	yasya sāmno gītis sakṛn niṣṭhitā na punar āvartate tad anṛcan dvyṛcaṃ bahvṛcaṃ vā sad apy ekarcasādṛśyād ekarcam eveti /
26.12.[25]	ayukteyaṃ kalpaneti cen nācāryeṇa jñāpitatvād atīṣaṅga ekasyām iti //
26.13.[1]	tatra teṣu parisāmasu ye stobhā agnervratādiṣu tān padāya padāyānusaṃharet /
26.13.[2]	anukrameṇa saṃharet /
26.13.[3]	yathaivan teṣu ca tathā pratipādaṃ brūyād ity ācāryāṇāṃ samayaḥ /
26.13.[4]	kim idam ācāryasamaya iti /
26.13.[5]	kva cid vacanād upalabdho 'rthas tatsadṛśe 'nyasminn api kasmiṃś cid vinaiva vacanād yukta iti yathā vācāryaiḥ kalpyate sa ācāryasamayaḥ //
26.14.[1]	yathādhītāny evādhītarūpāṇy eva yathāmnātam eva geyāny etānīti vadanty anubrāhmaṇinaḥ /
26.14.[2]	evam iti vā yo 'rthas tasminn ayam evaśabdo grāhyaḥ /
26.14.[3]	tathā sati yathaitāny adhītāny evaṃ geyānīti yojyam /
26.14.[4]	avacanāt pratipādaṃ stobhānām āvṛttau vacanābhāvāt /
26.14.[5]	anubrāhmaṇāni nāma brāhmaṇāny evānuvartamānā ke cid granthaviśeṣāḥ /
26.14.[6]	tadvido 'nubrāhmaṇinaḥ /
26.14.[7]	athānayor ācāryasamayānubrāhmaṇimatayoḥ katarat pratipattavyam ity ākāṅkṣita ucyate //
26.15.[1]	asya stobhasya mantraikadeśābhyāsaḥ kasmāt syāt /
26.15.[2]	naivāyaṃ bhavitum arhatīty arthaḥ /
26.15.[3]	na hi mantrasyānāvṛttau tadekadeśasyāvṛttir ṛte vacanād yujyate /
26.15.[4]	evañ ca saty udvāsanasāmno 'vabhṛthasāmnaś ca stobhāvṛttir vacanata evopalabdhācāryeṇeti mantavyam /
26.15.[5]	sā ca tayos sarvatrāpi pravṛttayor bhavati //
26.15.[6]	udvāsanāvabhṛthayor ye dve sāmanī vihite te sattraṃ rākṣoghnatvāt paśuñ cāgneyam āgneyatvād gacchataḥ /
26.15.[7]	tatra saṃśayaḥ /
26.15.[8]	sarve nidhanam upayantīty ayaṃ vidhis sāmadharma ity atrāpi pravartetāho svid udvāsanāvabhṛthadharma iti nivarteteti /
26.15.[9]	tatredam ucyate /
26.15.[10]	yad udvāsane vihitaṃ sāma tasminn udvāsanīya eva sati yac cāvabhṛthe tasmiṃś cāvabhṛthasāmny eva sati sarvais sārdhan nidhanam upeyāt /
26.15.[11]	anyatra tv anyasāmavat svayam evopeyād ity uktaṃ bhavati /
26.15.[12]	udvāsanāvabhṛthadharma evāyaṃ yad asya sāmadvayasya sarve nidhanam upayantīti abhiprāyaḥ /
26.15.[13]	tulyam etad iṣṭāhotrīyasyāpy udvāsanīyatvāviśeṣāt //
26.16.[1]	yathā vārṣāhare na sārdham anyair nidhanopāyanan tadvad ity arthaḥ /
26.16.[2]	ayaṃ pūrvasya vidher dṛṣṭānto nyastaḥ /
26.16.[3]	evam asya prayojanam /
26.16.[4]	vacanapramāṇako vidhir yatra vacanan tatraivāvatiṣṭhate /
26.16.[5]	yathaikasaṃpraiṣayor ekasthānayor vārṣāhareṣṭāhotrīyayor yasmin vacanam asti tasminn iṣṭāhotrīya eva sarvopeyanidhanatvadharmo 'vasthitaḥ /
26.16.[6]	na vārṣāhare prāpnoti /
26.16.[7]	evam etayo rākṣoghnayor iṣṭāhotrīyasya ca yatra vacanan tatraivodvāsanāvabhṛthayor evāvatiṣṭhate /
26.16.[8]	nānyatra prāpnotīti /
26.16.[9]	evañ cet stobhāvṛttir apy etayor anyatra na prāpnoti /
26.16.[10]	atra brūmaḥ /
26.16.[11]	sāmnor anayor vidhānānantaraṃ kiñ cid apy anyad anapekṣya vihitaṃ padāya padāya stobham āheti /
26.16.[12]	sarvanidhanopāyanan tu vidhāya tataḥ kālasaṃbandhaḥ kṛtaḥ /
26.16.[13]	devān vā etasmin kāle rakṣāṃṣy anvasacantety adhikāreṇa /
26.16.[14]	tasmāt tatkālayor eva bhavati /
26.16.[15]	atha [vā] vārṣāhara iti saptamīnirdeśaṃ sādhīyas saṃskurvann apara āha /
26.16.[16]	vārṣāhare 'vabhṛthasāmni saty api na sārdhan nidhanam upeyāt /
26.16.[17]	yady apy asyāvabhṛthasāmatvena vidhānan nāsty ata eva yatnāt keṣāñ cit kva cid astīty anumantavyam //
26.17.[1]	pariniṣṭhitaḥ parigāṇādhikāraḥ /
26.17.[2]	atha vaikṛtaḥ kaś cid agniṣṭomamantraikadeśābhyāsaḥ tatprasaṅgād ihaiva kathyate /
26.17.[3]	yac chabdajātam apy avadhānenāvartate tad ihāvartīty abhipreyate /
26.17.[4]	vrataśukriyeṣu yad āvarti tat karmāpannās stotram āpannāś catuṣkuryuś catur vadeyuḥ /
26.17.[5]	bhrājādayaś śabdās trir ucyante pāṭhe teṣāñ catuś catur vacanam idaṃ vihitaṃ stotraviṣaye //
26.18.[1]	caturthī ṣaṣṭhyarthe /
26.18.[2]	bhrājābhrājayos tūpadravanidhane trirukte eva syātān na caturukte /
26.18.[3]	na cedam upadravanidhanayos trirvacanaṃ vidhīyate /
26.18.[4]	tuśabdo vijñāpayati pūrvasya vidher ayam apavāda iti /
26.18.[5]	tasmād upadravanidhanāvayavabhūtā bhrājādayaś śabdā upadravanidhanaśabdenātra gṛhītā iti cintyam /
26.18.[6]	dṛśyate hy avayaviśabdo 'vayave /
26.18.[7]	yathā yajñavid ayaṃ bahvṛco madhuro 'yam āmra iti //
26.19-20.[1]	vrataśukriyāntarbhūtasyāvartijātasya caturvacanaṃ vidhāya bhrājābhrājopadravanidhanaviṣaya eva kasya hetoḥ pratiṣidhyata iti ced evam ete bhrājābhrāje ekaviṃśe ekaviṃśasaṃpadyukte bhavataḥ /
26.19-20.[2]	itarathā hy ekaviṃśasaṃpannas syād ity abhiprāyaḥ /
26.19-20.[3]	vinā tu hetuvacanād ācāryavacanaprāmāṇyād dhetuvacanam anarthakam /
26.19-20.[4]	nānarthakam anyasyāpi kasya cid ihāvartinas trirvacanam asty ekaviṃśasaṃpadam anatirekārtham iti jñāpanārthatvāt /
26.19-20.[5]	kasyeti cet parastād vakṣyāmaḥ /
26.19-20.[6]	kiṃ punas sarveṣu vrataśukriyeṣv ekaviṃśasaṃpad asti /
26.19-20.[7]	asti /
26.19-20.[8]	tad eva hīdam āvarticatuṣkaraṇaṃ vihitam /
26.19-20.[9]	ime ca vayam etām ekaviṃśasaṃpadaṃ bālāvagataye kalpayiṣyāmaḥ /
26.19-20.[10]	bhrāje tāvad aṣṭādaśa bhrājaśabdās traya ṛkpādāḥ /
26.19-20.[11]	evam ekaviṃśaḥ /
26.19-20.[12]	atha vā bhrājaśabdeṣu trīṇy ṛgakṣarāṇi yojayet /
26.19-20.[13]	avaśiṣṭāny ekaviṃśatir eva /
26.19-20.[14]	evam asmin dvāv ekaviṃśau /
26.19-20.[15]	yathā bhrāje tathābhrāje /
26.19-20.[16]	atha vikarṇe sapta stobhāś caturvacanād aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ /
26.19-20.[17]	ta evam eva pañcakṛtva ucyante tac catvāriṃśacchatam /
26.19-20.[18]	yas tūttamastobhas sa punar eva paranidhanadvayārtham āvartamānaḥ pūrvañ catur ucyate paścāt tu trir eva /
26.19-20.[19]	tasya jñāpakam uktam /
26.19-20.[20]	te saptapūrveṇa catvāriṃśena śatena saṃbhūya saptaikaviṃśā bhavanti /
26.19-20.[21]	auhovāhāuvāśabdas triś śrūyate /
26.19-20.[22]	trīṇi nidhanāni ṣaṭtriṃśad ṛgakṣarāṇīti dvāv ekaviṃśau /
26.19-20.[23]	atha bhāse daśa stobhāś caturvacanāc catvāriṃśat /
26.19-20.[24]	evaṃ pañcakṛtva ucyante sā dviśatiḥ /
26.19-20.[25]	ihauhośabdā nava nidhanāc ca yo 'dhastanastobhas te dviśatyāṃ prakṣiptā daśaikaviṃśān saṃpādayanti /
26.19-20.[26]	bhadram ityādayo nava vyāhṛtayo bhāśśabdadaśamā dvātriṃśad ṛgakṣarāṇi ca saṃbhūya dvāv ekaviṃśau /
26.19-20.[27]	atha mahādivākīrtye dvāv ādyau stobhau caturvacanād aṣṭau /
26.19-20.[28]	anantaran nidhanam /
26.19-20.[29]	tāni nava /
26.19-20.[30]	tataḥ prathamañ ca purīṣapadam anyaś ca stobho dvyabhyāsenānyasyāvartamānau pūrvair navabhis saha saptadaśa /
26.19-20.[31]	teṣu parasmin purīṣapadacatuṣṭaye prakṣipta ekaviṃśo niṣpadyate /
26.19-20.[32]	vayomanaḥprabhṛtayo vayobhūtāntās sapta vyāhṛtayo dviś śrūyante tāś caturdaśa /
26.19-20.[33]	dvitīye śravaṇe yas stobhas sa ekaviṃśaṃ pūrayati /
26.19-20.[34]	nidhanadvayaṃ kṣaṇam avatiṣṭhatāṃ pañcottarā stobhāś caturvacanād viṃśatiḥ /
26.19-20.[35]	yad ado nidhanam ī iti tad ekaviṃśaṃ pūrayati /
26.19-20.[36]	atha hośabdo auvāśabdaś caturuktaḥ pañca /
26.19-20.[37]	te caturuktā viṃśatiḥ /
26.19-20.[38]	yad ado nidhanam ū iti tad ekaviṃśaṃ pūrayati /
26.19-20.[39]	athaikas stobhaḥ pratipādan nidhāya ca catuś catur abhyasyamāno nidhanena sahaikaviṃśan niṣpādayati /
26.19-20.[40]	ṛkpādāś catvāraś catasraś ca tadādisthā vyāhṛtayo dyaur ityādayaś ca trayaś caturuktās stobhā viṃśatir bhavanti /
26.19-20.[41]	anantareṇa nidhanenaikaviṃśaṃ saṃpannam /
26.19-20.[42]	bhū[mi]r ityādayaś ca trayaś caturvacanād dvādaśa /
26.19-20.[43]	nidhanam eṣān trayodaśa /
26.19-20.[44]	atha dvau stobhāv āyur jyotir iti /
26.19-20.[45]	tayoḥ pūrvaś catur ucyata uttaras tūktāj jñāpakāt trir eva /
26.19-20.[46]	te sapta trayodaśabhis saṃbhūya viṃśatiḥ /
26.19-20.[47]	nidhanenaikaviṃśaḥ pūryate /
26.19-20.[48]	dvau bhrāja eko vābhrāje tadvan nava ca sapta ca /
26.19-20.[49]	brahmaṇas sāmni hotuś ca bhāse dvādaśa te khalu //
26.19-20.[50]	ekaviṃśās samāsena triṃśad dvātriṃśad eva vā /
26.19-20.[51]	śukriyeṣu vikāro 'yam etasyai saṃpade śrutaḥ //
26.21.[1]	mahāvrate 'hani sāmasu yad āvartiśabdajātan tat sarvaṃ pañcoktaṃ kuryuḥ pañcakṛtvo vadeyuḥ /
26.21.[2]	rājanarauhiṇakacatustriṃśatsaṃmitāny asya vidher viṣayaḥ /
26.21.[3]	nanv anyeṣv api sāmasu tasminn ahani santy āvartīni /
26.21.[4]	satyam etat /
26.21.[5]	na tu teṣāṃ mahāvratena viśeṣaṇam eṣu satsu saṃbhavati /
26.21.[6]	eṣāṃ hi mahāvrata eva pravṛttir dṛṣṭā nānyatra /
26.21.[7]	teṣām eva mahāvratena viśeṣaṇaṃ yuktaṃ na tu yeṣāṃ mahāvrate 'nyatra ca /
26.21.[8]	na hi kratur ubhayasāmā rathantarasāmety ucyata indrāgnigupto vendragupta iti /
26.21.[9]	yac cedam uktaṃ sāmatrayan tasya mahāvrate pravṛttir dṛṣṭā bhadrādīnān tv anyatrāpi /
26.21.[10]	tatas siddhaṃ rājanarauhiṇakacatustriṃśatsaṃmitāny asya vidher viṣaya iti /
26.21.[11]	kiṃ punar ayaṃ vidhiḥ pravartaka āho svin nivartako 'pi /
26.21.[12]	kaś cātra viśeṣaḥ /
26.21.[13]	yadi pravartaka eva kiṭkiṭākārāḥ pañcadaśakṛtva eva yathāmnāyam abhyasyeran /
26.21.[14]	atha nivartako 'pi pañcadaśakṛtva eva te 'py abhyasyeran /
26.21.[15]	tathā ca sati tasyāśītisaṃpad vihanyeta /
26.21.[16]	yady evam avighātārtham asyās saṃpadaḥ pravartaka evātra vidhir bhavatu /
26.21.[17]	mā kiṭkiṭākāreṣu pravartiṣṭa /
26.21.[18]	sarvam iti kimartham /
26.21.[19]	vrataśukriyeṣv āvartinas sarvañ catur ucyata ity evamartham /
26.21.[20]	nanu tatraiva hetuvacanāt siddham /
26.21.[21]	satyam etat /
26.21.[22]	siddhasyaiva tv idan dṛḍhīkaraṇam /
26.21.[23]	nanu punar ayaṃ mahāvrataśabdaḥ pṛṣṭhe mukhyas saṃstavanasaṃbandhād ahani pravartate /
26.21.[24]	tataḥ pṛṣṭhaviṣaya evāyaṃ vidhir bhavatu /
26.21.[25]	atra brūmaḥ /
26.21.[26]	yady ayaṃ vidhiḥ pṛṣṭhaviṣaya eva syāt prakṣāveṣu na prasajet tathā ca saty anyatra prakṣāvebhya ity anarthakaṃ syāt /
26.21.[27]	iha ke cit prājñaṃ manyamānāḥ pralapanti kila mahāvrate pṛṣṭhe pañcasāmātmake prāpiteyam āvartipañcoktatānyatra prakṣāvebhya iti rājanād anyebhyo 'pi nivartyata iti /
26.21.[28]	te 'sya prativacanan dadatu /
26.21.[29]	pañcoktaṃ rājana iti kṛtvā mā vā bhūd uttaraṃ vākyam iti /
26.21.[30]	atha vāsya vidheḥ pṛṣṭhaviṣayatve doṣo 'yam aparihāraḥ prādur bhavati rauhiṇake /
26.21.[31]	tad vā aśītibhis saṃpannam iti yad aśītisaṃpannatvam uktaṃ tad rauhiṇakāvartiṇāṃ pañcoktatvābhāve mṛṣā bhavati /
26.21.[32]	yac ca sāmendrasya mahāvratam iti tasmin liṅgadevatābhyāṃ paśuparigāṇārthaṃ prapanne sati tu viṣayatāpy asya vidher anenaiva pratyuktā /
26.21.[33]	tasmād ihāhar eva mahāvrataśabdenopalakṣyata iti samyak /
26.21.[34]	yathā mahāvratam atirātra iti /
26.21.[35]	tatrāpy uktaṃ sāmatrayam evāsya vidher viṣayaḥ /
26.21.[36]	nanu catustriṃśatsaṃmite pañcakṛtva evāvartijātaṃ paṭhyate triḥ prakṣāvāḥ /
26.21.[37]	teṣv ayaṃ vidhir neṣyate /
26.21.[38]	tasmād rājanarauhiṇakayor apīti vaktavyam /
26.21.[39]	tataś caivam artho bhavati mā ca bhūd uttaraṃ vākyam iti /
26.21.[40]	atra brūmaḥ /
26.21.[41]	bhavaduktavan nyaste 'py atrārthas sidhyati /
26.21.[42]	arthāntarasya tu jñāpanārthaṃ mahāvrataśabdenaivaitat sāmatrayam upalakṣyate /
26.21.[43]	kin tad arthāntaram iti cet tasmin mahāvratam upayantītyādinā vacanena yasyāhno mahāvrataṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ syāt tasmin rauhiṇakacatustriṃśatsaṃmitayor api prayogaḥ kārya iti /
26.21.[44]	evam idaṃ vrataśukriyeṣu rājanarauhiṇakayoś cāmnāyavirodhena śabdānām abhyāsādhikyaṃ vihitam /
26.21.[45]	tatra vrataśukriyeṣu yo vidhis sa brāhmaṇāntarād āgato 'vagantavyaḥ /
26.21.[46]	rājanarauhiṇakayos tu yo 'yaṃ vikāras so 'smadbrāhmaṇād evāgacchati /
26.21.[47]	[tathā] hi sāmanī prakṛtya śrūyate /
26.21.[48]	tad vā aśītibhis saṃpannam ekaikasyāṃ stotriyāyān dve dve aśītyau saṃpadyete iti ca tad vā aśītibhis sampannam āśayanty evainam eteneti ca /
26.21.[49]	tāsām aśītīnāṃ saṃpattyartham asmin sāmadvaye vikāraḥ kriyate /
26.21.[50]	katham iti ced rājane tāvat sapta stobhā ṛkpādena sahāṣṭau /
26.21.[51]	te pañcakṛtvo 'bhyasyante /
26.21.[52]	sārdhā dvāviṃśatiḥ /
26.21.[53]	sābhyāsās te catvāriṃśat saṃpannāḥ /
26.21.[54]	evam uttareṣv api pādeṣu /
26.21.[55]	te dve aśītyau /
26.21.[56]	nidhaneṣu pṛthak pañcaviṃśasaṃpat saṃpāditā /
26.21.[57]	ta u vai pañca pañcaviṃśās sāmanidhanānāṃ saṃstutānāṃ saṃpadyanta iti vāgādiṣu pañcasu nidhanāvayaveṣu nidhanaśabdaś śrūyate /
26.21.[58]	pañcaviṃśastome sati pañcaviṃśaṃ śataṃ bhavati /
26.21.[59]	atha rauhiṇake ṣaṭ stobhāḥ pañcakṛtvo 'bhyasyamānāḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ kiṭkiṭākārais saha pañcacatvāriṃśad bhavanti /
26.21.[60]	evam eva pañcakṛtvaḥ kṛte sapañcaviṃśatir dviśatī /
26.21.[61]	tataḥ paran nidhanāny anantarhitāni dvādaśa /
26.21.[62]	tataḥ para upadravaḥ /
26.21.[63]	tataḥ paran nidhanam /
26.21.[64]	tāni caturdaśa /
26.21.[65]	teṣāṃ yoga ekonam aśītitrayaṃ saṃvartate /
26.21.[66]	yadi tatra catvāra ṛkpādāḥ praviśeyus tat tryadhikaṃ syāt /
26.21.[67]	tathā ca saty aśītibhis sampannam iti vacanaṃ vihanyeta /
26.21.[68]	tasmād anapekṣya pādānāṃ pṛthag avasthānam ṛg ekadhaiva prakṣeptavyā /
26.21.[69]	evam etad aśītitrayam aśītibhis sampannam iti śrutyuktam anyūnam anadhikaṃ bhavati /
26.21.[70]	pañcaviṃśasaṃpad atrāpy asti /
26.21.[71]	yāsau dviśatī sapañcaviṃśā tato nava pañcaviṃśās saṃvartante /
26.21.[72]	ṛgakṣarāṇi ṣaṭtriṃśat /
26.21.[73]	teṣv amīṣāñ caturdaśānāṃ prakṣepe dvau pañcaviṃśau bhavataḥ /
26.21.[74]	catustriṃśatsaṃmite nāmarūpaiva saṃpat /
26.21.[75]	sā dvividhā /
26.21.[76]	samudāyagatāvayavagatā ca /
26.21.[77]	pūrvasyān tāvad anantarhitās trayas stobhāḥ pratipādaṃ pratiprakṣāvan nidhanāya cāvartamānāś caturviṃśatir ṛkpādair aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ /
26.21.[78]	navasu prakṣāveṣu traya evānantarhitā gaṇyante /
26.21.[79]	tair ekatriṃśadbhir nidhanāvayavaiś catustriṃśaḥ pūryate /
26.21.[80]	athāvayavagatā /
26.21.[81]	tasyān trayas stobhāḥ pañcakṛtvo 'bhyasyamānāḥ pañcadaśa rkpādena ṣoḍaśa /
26.21.[82]	punar api te stobhāḥ pūrvavad evāvṛttāḥ pañcadaśa prakṣāvair aṣṭādaśa /
26.21.[83]	pūrvaiṣ ṣoḍaśabhis saha yogād eṣāñ catustriṃśas saṃvartate /
26.21.[84]	evaṃ pratipādañ catustriṃśatsaṃpad bhavati /
26.21.[85]	antyasya tu prakṣāvatrayasya sthāne naidhanaṃ vacanatrayaṃ praviśati //
26.21.[86]	aṅgāni yeṣāṃ prakṣāvās sāṅgas tv ātmā mahāvratam /
26.21.[87]	saṃpādayantu te 'śītiṃ śrutāṃ rauhiṇake dhiyā //
26.22.[1]	prakṣāvā iti kṣauśabdānām eṣāṃ yājñikaprasiddhā saṃjñā /
26.22.[2]	teṣv api pūrvasya vidheḥ prasaṅga idam ucyate /
26.22.[3]	prakṣāvebhyo 'nyatra pūrvo vidhir bhavati /
26.22.[4]	prakṣāveṣu na bhavatīty arthaḥ /
26.22.[5]	evañ cen na prakṣāveṣv iti kartavyam /
26.22.[6]	naitad yuktam /
26.22.[7]	pratiṣedhāntan tarhi sūtram evaṃ syāt /
26.22.[8]	tad amaṅgalaṃ bhavet /
26.22.[9]	tatparihārāya vidhir evāyaṃ kṛtaḥ /
26.22.[10]	atha vedaṃ pūrvavākyāntarbhūtam eva bhavatu na vākyāntaram /
26.22.[11]	tathāpy ukto 'rthas sidhyati /
26.22.[12]	evam idaṃ yatnato maṅgalāntatvaṃ sūtrasya kṛtam //
